令 $a = -2, b = 3, m = 2$ 及 $n = 3$ , 并设 $t = \frac{x - 2}{x + 3}$ , 即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x - 2) ^ {2} (x + 3) ^ {3}} = \frac {1}{5 ^ {4}} \int \frac {(1 - t) ^ {3}}{t ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} t = \frac {1}{5 ^ {4}} \int \left(\frac {1}{t ^ {2}} - \frac {3}{t} + 3 - t\right) \mathrm {d} t = \frac {1}{6 2 5} \left(- \frac {1}{t} - 3 \ln | t | + 3 t - \frac {t ^ {2}}{2}\right) + C \\ = \frac {1}{6 2 5} \left[ - \frac {x + 3}{x - 2} - 3 \ln \left| \frac {x - 2}{x + 3} \right| + \frac {3 (x - 2)}{x + 3} - \frac {(x - 2) ^ {2}}{2 (x + 3) ^ {2}} \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1923】若 $P_{n}(x)$ 为 $x$ 的 $n$ 次多项式，计算 $\int \frac{P_n(x)}{(x - a)^{n + 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 利用泰勒公式.

解 由于 $P_{n}(x)$ 为 $x$ 的 $n$ 次多项式，故得

$$
P _ {n} (x) = \sum_ {k = 0} ^ {n} \frac {P _ {n} ^ {(k)} (a)}{k !} (x - a) ^ {k},
$$

其中 $P_{n}^{(0)}(a) = P_{n}(a), 0! = 1.$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {P _ {n} (x)}{(x - a) ^ {n + 1}} d x = \sum_ {k = 0} ^ {n - 1} \frac {1}{k !} P _ {n} ^ {(k)} (a) \int \frac {d x}{(x - a) ^ {n - k + 1}} + \frac {1}{n !} P _ {n} ^ {(n)} (a) \int \frac {d x}{x - a} \\ = - \sum_ {k = 0} ^ {n - 1} \frac {P _ {n} ^ {(k)} (a)}{k ! (n - k) (x - a) ^ {n - k}} + \frac {1}{n !} P _ {n} ^ {(n)} (a) \ln | x - a | + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\frac{P_n^{(n)}(a)}{n!} = a_0$ 为 $P_{n}(x)$ 的首项系数，即

$$
P _ {n} (x) = a _ {0} (x - a) ^ {n} + a _ {1} (x - a) ^ {n - 1} + \dots + a _ {n - 1} (x - a) + a _ {n}.
$$

【1924】设 $R(x) = R^{*}(x^{2})$ ，其中 $R^{*}$ 为有理函数，则函数 $R(x)$ 分解为有理分式时有什么特性？

解设 $R^{*}(x) = P(x) + H(x)$ ，其中 $P(x)$ 是多项式；若 $R^{*}(x)$ 本身也为多项式，则 $H(x) \equiv 0$ ；否则 $H(x) = \frac{P_{1}(x)}{Q_{1}(x)}$ 是真分式，而 $P_{1}(x), Q_{1}(x)$ 也均为多项式.

设 $Q_{1}(x)$ 有非负实根为 $a_{i}^{2}$ ，其重数为 $\alpha_{i}(i = 1,2,\dots ,m)$ ；负根为 $-b_{k}^{2}$ ，其重数为 $\beta_{k}(k = 1,2,\dots ,t)$ ；二次因式为 $x^{2} + C_{p}x + D_{p}$ ，其重数为 $\gamma_{p}(p = 1,2,\dots ,s)$ ，其中 $C_p^2 -4D_p < 0$ 。于是，

$$
Q _ {1} (x) = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} (x - a _ {i} ^ {2}) ^ {\alpha_ {i}} \prod_ {k = 1} ^ {t} (x + b _ {k} ^ {2}) ^ {\beta_ {k}} \prod_ {p = 1} ^ {s} (x ^ {2} + C _ {p} x + D _ {p}) ^ {\gamma_ {p}}, & m \neq 0, t \neq 0, s \neq 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {k = 1} ^ {t} (x + b _ {k} ^ {2}) ^ {\beta_ {k}} \prod_ {p = 1} ^ {s} (x ^ {2} + C _ {p} x + D _ {p}) ^ {\gamma_ {p}}, & m = 0, t \neq 0, s \neq 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} (x - a _ {i} ^ {2}) ^ {\alpha_ {i}} \prod_ {p = 1} ^ {s} (x ^ {2} + C _ {p} x + D _ {p}) ^ {\gamma_ {p}}, & m \neq 0, t = 0, s \neq 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} (x - a _ {i} ^ {2}) ^ {\alpha_ {i}} \prod_ {k = 1} ^ {t} (x + b _ {k} ^ {2}) ^ {\beta_ {k}}, & m \neq 0, t \neq 0, s = 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} (x - a _ {i} ^ {2}) ^ {\alpha_ {i}}, & m \neq 0, t = 0, s = 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {k = 1} ^ {t} (x + b _ {k} ^ {2}) ^ {\beta_ {k}}, & m = 0, t \neq 0, s = 0, \\ a _ {0} \prod_ {p = 1} ^ {s} (x ^ {2} + C _ {p} x + D _ {p}) ^ {\gamma_ {p}}, & m = 0, t = 0, s \neq 0. \end{array} \right.
$$

以下就 $Q_{1}(x)$ 表达式中的第一种情形予以论证

由 $C_p^2 - 4D_p < 0$ ，可得

$$
x ^ {4} + C _ {p} x ^ {2} + D _ {p} = \left(x ^ {2} + E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) \left(x ^ {2} - E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) \quad (p = 1, 2, \dots , s),
$$

则此时有

$$
Q _ {1} \left(x ^ {2}\right) = a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} \left(x - a _ {i}\right) ^ {\alpha_ {i}} \left(x + a _ {i}\right) ^ {\alpha_ {i}} \prod_ {k = 1} ^ {t} \left(x ^ {2} + b _ {k} ^ {2}\right) ^ {\beta_ {k}} \prod_ {p = 1} ^ {s} \left(x ^ {2} + E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) ^ {\gamma_ {p}} \left(x ^ {2} - E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) ^ {\gamma_ {p}},
$$

以及

$$
\begin{array}{l} H (x ^ {2}) = \frac {P _ {1} (x ^ {2})}{Q _ {1} (x ^ {2})} \\ = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {m} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {a _ {i}} \left[ \frac {A _ {k}}{(a _ {i} - x) ^ {i}} + \frac {A _ {k} ^ {\prime}}{(a _ {i} + x) ^ {i}} \right] + \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {t} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\beta_ {k}} \frac {B _ {k} x + C _ {k}}{(x ^ {2} + b _ {k} ^ {2}) ^ {i}} + \sum_ {p = 1} ^ {s} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\gamma_ {p}} \left[ \frac {M _ {p} x + N _ {p}}{(x ^ {2} + E _ {p} x + F _ {p}) ^ {i}} + \frac {M _ {p} ^ {\prime} x + N _ {p} ^ {\prime}}{(x ^ {2} - E _ {p} x + F _ {p}) ^ {i}} \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

显然有 $H(x^{2}) = H((-x)^{2})$ ，由 $H(x^2)$ 的分解式的唯一性，比较系数，即得常数关系为：

$$
A _ {k 1} ^ {\prime} = A _ {k 1}, M _ {p 2} ^ {\prime} = - M _ {p 2}, N _ {p 2} ^ {\prime} = N _ {p 2}, B _ {k 3} = 0.
$$

$$
\left(t _ {1} = 1, 2, \dots , a _ {i}, i = 1, 2, \dots , m; t _ {2} = 1, 2, \dots , \gamma_ {p}, p = 1, 2, \dots , s; t _ {3} = 1, 2, \dots , \beta_ {k}, k = 1, 2, \dots , t\right)
$$

最后得 $R(x) = P(x^{2}) + H(x^{2}) = P(x^{2}) + \sum_{i = 1}^{m}\sum_{t = 1}^{\alpha_{i}}A_{it}\left[\frac{1}{(a_{i} - x)^{t}} +\frac{1}{(a_{i} + x)^{t}}\right] + \sum_{k = 1}^{t}\sum_{i = 1}^{\beta_{k}}\frac{C_{k}}{(x^{2} + b_{k}^{2})^{t}}$

$$
+ \sum_ {p - 1} ^ {s} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\gamma_ {p}} \left[ \frac {M _ {p} x + N _ {p}}{\left(x ^ {2} + E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) ^ {c}} - \frac {M _ {p} x - N _ {p}}{\left(x ^ {2} - E _ {p} x + F _ {p}\right) ^ {c}} \right].
$$

如若 $H(x)\neq 0$ ，而 $m = 0$ ，但 $t\neq 0,s\neq 0$ 时，则在上述表达式中就应缺乏第二项的和式，形如

$$
R (x) = P \left(x ^ {2}\right) + \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {i} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\beta_ {k}} + \sum_ {p = 1} ^ {i} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {\gamma_ {p}},
$$

其他情形可以类似推演，此处不再一一细叙.至于当 $H(x)\equiv 0$ 时，当然有 $R(x) = P(x^{2})$

另外，本题也可在复数域上作分解考虑

仍记 $R^{*}(x) = P(x) + H(x)$ , 其中 $P(x)$ 为多项式, 而 $H(x)$ 要么是零 (当 $R^{*}(x)$ 为多项式时), 要么是一个真分式, 例如 $H(x) \neq 0$ 时, 记 $H(x) = \frac{P_{1}(x)}{Q_{1}(x)}$ 是其真分式. $P_{1}(x), Q_{1}(x)$ 为多项式. 若记 $Q_{1}(x)$ 在复数域中的根为 $\alpha_{i}$ , 其相应重数记为 $n_{i} (i = 1,2,\dots,m$ ; 显然 $m \geqslant 1$ ), 即

$$
Q _ {1} (x) = a _ {0} \prod_ {i = 1} ^ {m} (x - \alpha_ {i}) ^ {n _ {i}},
$$

那么 $Q_{1}(x^{2})$ 中的每一项 $x^{2} - \alpha_{i}$ 可分解为一次式乘积

$$
x ^ {2} - a _ {i} = (x - b _ {i}) (x + b _ {i}),
$$

于是， $Q_{1}(x^{2}) = a_{0}\prod_{i = 1}^{m}(x - b_{i})^{n_{i}}(x + b_{i})^{n_{i}}.$

相应地有 $H(x^{2}) = \frac{P_{1}(x^{2})}{Q_{1}(x^{2})} = \sum_{i = 1}^{m}\sum_{k = 1}^{n_{i}}\left[\frac{B_{ik}}{(x - b_{i})^{k}} +\frac{B_{ik}^{\prime}}{(x + b_{i})^{k}}\right] = \sum_{i = 1}^{m}\sum_{k = 1}^{n_{i}}\left[\frac{A_{ik}}{(x - b_{i})^{k}} +\frac{A_{ik}^{\prime}}{(x + b_{i})^{k}}\right].$

由 $H(x^{2}) = H((-x)^{2})$ ，从 $H(x^{2})$ 的分解式的唯一性，比较系数，即得

$$
A _ {i} ^ {\prime} = A _ {i k} (k = 1, 2, \dots , n _ {i}; i = 1, 2, \dots , m).
$$

最后得到 $R(x) = P(x^{2}) + H(x^{2}) = P(x^{2}) + \sum_{i = 1}^{m}\sum_{k = 1}^{n_{i}}\left[\frac{A_{ik}}{(b_{i} - x)^{k}} +\frac{A_{ik}}{(b_{i} + x)^{k}}\right],$

其中 $b_{i}$ 为分母 $Q_{1}(x^{2})$ 的根， $A_{\star}$ 为常系数.

【1925】 计算 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x^{2n}}$ ，式中 $n$ 为正整数.

解 先将被积函数分解成部分分式之和，我们可以证明：

$$
\frac {1}{1 + x ^ {2 n}} = \frac {1}{n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \frac {1 - x \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi}{x ^ {2} - 2 x \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi + 1}.
$$

事实上，记多项式 $x^{2n} + 1$ 的 $2n$ 个根为 $a_{k}$ $(k = 1,2,\dots ,2n)$ ，显然 $a_{k} = \cos \frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi +\mathrm{i}\sin \frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi$ 其中 $\mathrm{i}^2 = -1.$ 于是，

$$
\left| a _ {k} \right| = 1, \quad a _ {k} ^ {2 n} = - 1, \quad \bar {a} _ {k} = a _ {2 n - k + 1}, a _ {k} \bar {a} _ {k} = 1, \quad a _ {k} + \bar {a} _ {k} = 2 \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi .
$$

设 $\frac{1}{1 + x^{2n}} = \sum_{k=1}^{2n} \frac{A_k}{x - a_k},$

即 $1 = \sum_{k=1}^{2n} \frac{A_k(1 + x^{2n})}{x - a_k}$ .

令 $x \rightarrow a_{i}$ , 并应用洛必达法则, 即得

$$
1 = \lim  _ {x \rightarrow a _ {i}} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {2 n} \frac {A _ {k} (1 + x ^ {2 n})}{x - a _ {k}} = \lim  _ {x \rightarrow a _ {i}} \frac {A _ {i} (1 + x ^ {2 n})}{x - a _ {i}} = \lim  _ {x \rightarrow a _ {i}} (2 n A _ {i} x ^ {2 n - 1}) = 2 n A _ {i} \frac {a _ {i} ^ {2 n}}{a _ {i}} = - \frac {2 n A _ {i}}{a _ {i}} \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots , 2 n),
$$

即 $A_{k} = -\frac{a_{k}}{2n}$ $(k = 1,2,\dots ,2n)$ .于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {1}{1 + x ^ {2 n}} = - \frac {1}{2 n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {2 n} \frac {a _ {k}}{x - a _ {k}} = - \frac {1}{2 n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \left(\frac {a _ {k}}{x - a _ {k}} + \frac {\bar {a} _ {k}}{x - \bar {a} _ {k}}\right) = - \frac {1}{2 n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \frac {(a _ {k} + \bar {a} _ {k}) x - 2 a _ {k} \bar {a} _ {k}}{x ^ {2} - (a _ {k} + \bar {a} _ {k}) x + a _ {k} \bar {a} _ {k}} \\ = \frac {1}{n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \frac {1 - x \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi}{x ^ {2} - 2 x \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi + 1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

最后得到 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x^{2n}} = \frac{1}{n}\sum_{k = 1}^{n}\int \frac{1 - x\cos\frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi}{x^2 - 2x\cos\frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi + 1}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{2n}\sum_{k = 1}^{n}\left(\cos \frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi \int \frac{2x - 2\cos\frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi}{x^2 - 2x\cos\frac{2k - 1}{2n}\pi + 1}\mathrm{d}x\right)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} + \frac {1}{n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \left[ \sin^ {2} \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\left(x - \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi\right) ^ {2} + \sin^ {2} \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi} \right] \\ = - \frac {1}{2 n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \left[ \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi \ln \left(x ^ {2} - 2 x \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi + 1\right) \right] \\ + \frac {1}{n} \sum_ {k = 1} ^ {n} \left(\sin \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi \arctan \frac {x - \cos \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi}{\sin \frac {2 k - 1}{2 n} \pi}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

# § 3. 无理函数的积分法

利用化被积函数为有理函数的方法，求下列积分：

【1926】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{x}}.$

解设 $\sqrt{x} = t$ ，则 $x = t^2$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = 2t\mathrm{dt}$ ，代入得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{1 + \sqrt {x}} = 2 \int \frac {t \mathrm {d} t}{1 + t} = 2 \int \left(1 - \frac {1}{1 + t}\right) \mathrm {d} t = 2 [ t - \ln (1 + t) ] + C = 2 \sqrt {x} - 2 \ln (1 + \sqrt {x}) + C.
$$

【1927】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x(1 + 2\sqrt{x} + \sqrt[3]{x})}$

解设 $\sqrt[6]{x} = t$ ，则 $x = t^6$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = 6t^{5}\mathrm{dt}$ .代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} r}{x (1 + 2 \sqrt {x} + \sqrt [ 3 ]{x})} = 6 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t (1 + 2 t ^ {3} + t ^ {2})} = 6 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t (1 + t) (2 t ^ {2} - t + 1)} = 6 \int \left[ \frac {1}{t} - \frac {1}{4 (1 + t)} - \frac {6 t - 1}{4 (2 t ^ {2} - t + 1)} \right] \mathrm {d} t \\ = 6 \left\{\ln t - \frac {1}{4} \ln | 1 + t | - \frac {3}{8} \int \frac {4 t - 1}{2 t ^ {2} - t + 1} d t - \frac {1}{1 6} \int \frac {d (t - \frac {1}{4})}{(t - \frac {1}{4}) ^ {2} + \frac {7}{1 6}} \right\} \\ = 6 \left\{\ln | t | - \frac {1}{4} \ln | 1 + t | - \frac {3}{8} \ln (2 t ^ {2} - t + 1) - \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {7}} \arctan \frac {4 t - 1}{\sqrt {7}} \right\} + C \\ = \frac {3}{4} \ln \frac {t ^ {8}}{(1 + t) ^ {2} (2 t ^ {2} - t + 1) ^ {3}} - \frac {3}{2 \sqrt {7}} \arctan \frac {4 t - 1}{\sqrt {7}} + C \\ = \frac {3}{4} \ln \frac {x \sqrt [ 3 ]{x}}{(1 + \sqrt [ 6 ]{x}) ^ {2} (2 \sqrt [ 3 ]{x} - \sqrt [ 6 ]{x} + 1) ^ {3}} - \frac {3}{2 \sqrt {7}} \arctan \frac {4 \sqrt [ 6 ]{x} - 1}{\sqrt {7}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1928】 $\int \frac{x\sqrt[3]{2 + x}}{x + \sqrt[3]{2 + x}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\sqrt[3]{2 + x} = t$ ，则 $x = t^3 - 2, \mathrm{d}x = 3t^2\mathrm{d}t.$ 代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {x \sqrt [ 3 ]{2 + x}}{x + \sqrt [ 3 ]{2 + x}} d x = 3 \int \frac {t ^ {6} - 2 t ^ {3}}{t ^ {3} + t - 2} d t = 3 \int \left(t ^ {3} - t + \frac {t ^ {2} - 2 t}{t ^ {3} + t - 2}\right) d t \\ = \frac {3}{4} t ^ {4} - \frac {3}{2} t ^ {2} + 3 \int \left[ - \frac {1}{4 (t - 1)} + \frac {\frac {5}{4} t - \frac {1}{2}}{t ^ {2} + t + 2} \right] d t \\ = \frac {3}{4} t ^ {4} - \frac {3}{2} t ^ {2} - \frac {3}{4} \ln | t - 1 | + \frac {1 5}{8} \int \frac {2 t + 1}{t ^ {2} + t + 2} d t - \frac {2 7}{8} \int \frac {d (t + \frac {1}{2})}{(t + \frac {1}{2}) ^ {2} + \frac {7}{4}} \\ = \frac {3}{4} t ^ {4} - \frac {3}{2} t ^ {2} - \frac {3}{4} \ln | t - 1 | + \frac {1 5}{8} \ln (t ^ {2} + t + 2) - \frac {2 7}{4 \sqrt {7}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 t + 1}{\sqrt {7}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt[3]{2 + x}$

【1929】 $\int \frac{1 - \sqrt{x + 1}}{1 + \sqrt[3]{x + 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $\sqrt[6]{x + 1} = t$

解设 $\sqrt[6]{x + 1} = t$ ，则 $x = t^6 - 1, \mathrm{d}x = 6t^5\mathrm{d}t.$ 代入得

$$
\int \frac {1 - \sqrt {x + 1}}{1 + \sqrt [ 3 ]{x + 1}} d x = 6 \int \frac {t ^ {5} (1 - t ^ {3})}{1 + t ^ {2}} d t = 6 \int \left(- t ^ {6} + t ^ {4} + t ^ {3} - t ^ {2} - t + 1 + \frac {t - 1}{1 + t ^ {2}}\right) d t
$$

$$
= - \frac {6}{7} t ^ {7} + \frac {6}{5} t ^ {5} + \frac {3}{2} t ^ {4} - 2 t ^ {3} - 3 t ^ {2} + 6 t + 3 \ln (1 + t ^ {2}) - 6 \arctan t + C,
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt[6]{x + 1}$

【1930】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x}(1 + \sqrt[4]{x})^3}$

解设 $\sqrt[4]{x} = t$ ，则 $x = t^4$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = 4t^{3}\mathrm{dt}$ 代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {x} (1 + \sqrt [ 4 ]{x}) ^ {3}} = 4 \int \frac {t \mathrm {d} t}{(1 + t) ^ {3}} = 4 \int \left[ \frac {1}{(1 + t) ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{(1 + t) ^ {3}} \right] \mathrm {d} t = - \frac {4}{1 + t} + \frac {2}{(1 + t) ^ {2}} + C \\ = \frac {2}{(1 + \sqrt [ 4 ]{x}) ^ {2}} - \frac {4}{1 + \sqrt [ 4 ]{x}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1931】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x + 1} - \sqrt{x - 1}}{\sqrt{x + 1} + \sqrt{x - 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 注意 $\frac{\sqrt{x + 1} - \sqrt{x - 1}}{\sqrt{x + 1} + \sqrt{x - 1}} = \frac{(\sqrt{x + 1} - \sqrt{x - 1})^2}{(x + 1) - (x - 1)} = x - \sqrt{x^2 - 1}$ .

解设 $\sqrt{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}} = t$ ，则 $x = \frac{t^2 + 1}{t^2 - 1}$ $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{4t}{(t^2 - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 代人得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sqrt {x + 1} - \sqrt {x - 1}}{\sqrt {x + 1} + \sqrt {x - 1}} d x = \int \frac {\sqrt {\frac {x + 1}{x - 1}} - 1}{\sqrt {\frac {x + 1}{x - 1}} + 1} d x = - 4 \int \frac {t d t}{(t - 1) (t + 1) ^ {3}} \\ = \int \left[ - \frac {2}{(t + 1) ^ {3}} + \frac {1}{(t + 1) ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2 (t + 1)} - \frac {1}{2 (t - 1)} \right] d t = \frac {1}{(t + 1) ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{t + 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \frac {t + 1}{t - 1} \right| + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {1}{2} x ^ {2} - \frac {1}{2} x \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln | x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} | + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

如果不限制将被积函数化为有理函数，本题的解法可简单些.事实上，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sqrt {x + 1} - \sqrt {x - 1}}{\sqrt {x + 1} + \sqrt {x - 1}} d x = \int \frac {(\sqrt {x + 1} - \sqrt {x - 1}) ^ {2}}{(x + 1) - (x - 1)} d x = \int (x - \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}) d x \\ = \frac {1}{2} x ^ {2} - \frac {1}{2} x \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln | x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} | + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1932】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{(x + 1)^2(x - 1)^4}}.$

提示 令 $\sqrt[3]{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}} = t.$

解设 $\sqrt[3]{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}} = t$ ，则 $x = \frac{t^3 + 1}{t^3 - 1},\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{6t^2}{(t^3 - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 代人得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 3 ]{(x + 1) ^ {2} (x - 1) ^ {4}}} = - \frac {3}{2} \int \mathrm {d} t = - \frac {3}{2} t + C = - \frac {3}{2} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {x + 1}{x - 1}} + C.
$$

【1933】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[4]{x^3(a - x)}} (a > 0).$

提示 令 $\sqrt[4]{\frac{a - x}{x}} = t$ ，并分别利用1921题的递推公式及1884题的结果.

解设 $\sqrt[4]{\frac{a - x}{x}} = t$ ，则 $x = \frac{a}{1 + t^4}$ $\mathrm{dx} = -\frac{4at^3}{(1 + t^4)^2}\mathrm{dt}.$ 代人得

$$
\int \frac {x \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 4 ]{x ^ {3} (a - x)}} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 4 ]{\frac {a - x}{x}}} = - 4 a \int \frac {t ^ {2}}{(1 + t ^ {4}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} t = - 4 a \int \left[ \frac {t}{(t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1) (t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1)} \right] ^ {2} \mathrm {d} t
$$

$$
= - \frac {a}{2} \int \left(\frac {1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} - \frac {1}{t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}\right) ^ {2} d t = - \frac {a}{2} \int \frac {d t}{(t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1) ^ {2}} - \frac {a}{2} \int \frac {d t}{(t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1) ^ {2}} + a \int \frac {d t}{t ^ {4} + 1}.
$$

现在分别求上述积分，利用1921题的递推公式，即得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1) ^ {2}} = \frac {2 t - \sqrt {2}}{2 (t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1)} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} = \frac {2 t - \sqrt {2}}{2 (t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1)} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(t - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}\right)}{\left(t - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac {2 t - \sqrt {2}}{2 \left(t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1\right)} + \sqrt {2} \arctan (\sqrt {2} t - 1) + C _ {1}
$$

及 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{(t^2 + t\sqrt{2} + 1)^2} = \frac{2t + \sqrt{2}}{2(t^2 + t\sqrt{2} + 1)} +\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{t^2 + t\sqrt{2} + 1} = \frac{2t + \sqrt{2}}{2(t^2 + t\sqrt{2} + 1)} +\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left(t + \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}\right)}{\left(t + \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}\right)^2 + \frac{1}{2}}.$

$$
= \frac {2 t + \sqrt {2}}{2 \left(t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1\right)} + \sqrt {2} \arctan (\sqrt {2} t + 1) + C _ {2}.
$$

利用1884题的结果，即得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{t^4 + 1} = \frac{1}{4\sqrt{2}}\ln \frac{t^2 + t\sqrt{2} + 1}{t^2 - t\sqrt{2} + 1} +\frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\arctan \frac{t\sqrt{2}}{1 - t^2} +C_3.$

最后得到

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {x \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 4 ]{x ^ {3} (a - x)}} = - \frac {a}{2} \left[ \frac {2 t - \sqrt {2}}{2 (t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1)} + \frac {2 t + \sqrt {2}}{2 (t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1)} \right] - \frac {a \sqrt {2}}{2} \left[ \arctan (\sqrt {2} t - 1) + \arctan (\sqrt {2} t + 1) \right] \\ + \frac {a}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} + \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {t \sqrt {2}}{1 - t ^ {2}}\right) + C _ {4} \\ = - \frac {a t ^ {3}}{1 + t ^ {4}} + \frac {a}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} - \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {t \sqrt {2}}{1 - t ^ {2}}\right) + C _ {4} \\ = - \frac {a t ^ {3}}{1 + t ^ {4}} + \frac {a}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} + \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {1 - t ^ {2}}{t \sqrt {2}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt[4]{\frac{a - x}{x}} (0 <   x <   a).$

【1934】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[n]{(x - a)^{n + 1}(x - b)^{n - 1}}}$ （ $n$ 为正整数）.

解当 $a = b$ 时，显然被积函数为 $(x - a)^{-2}$ ，因此，所求的积分为 $-\frac{1}{x - a} + C$ ；当 $a \neq b$ 时，设 $\sqrt[n]{\frac{x - b}{x - a}} = t$

则 $x = a + \frac{a - b}{t^n - 1},\quad \mathrm{d}x = -\frac{n(a - b)t^{n - 1}}{(t^n - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}t,x - a = \frac{a - b}{t^n - 1},\quad x - b = \frac{(a - b)t^n}{t^n - 1}.$

代人得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[n]{(x - a)^{n + 1}(x - b)^{n - 1}}} = -\frac{n}{a - b}\int \mathrm{d}t = -\frac{n}{a - b} t + C = -\frac{n}{a - b}\sqrt[n]{\frac{x - b}{x - a}} +C.$

【1935】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{x} + \sqrt{1 + x}}.$

提示 设 $\sqrt{x} = \frac{t^2 - 1}{2t}$ ，并限制 $t > 1$

解设 $\sqrt{x} = \frac{t^2 - 1}{2t}$ 并限制 $t > 1$ ，则 $x = \left(\frac{t^2 - 1}{2t}\right)^2, \mathrm{d}x = \frac{t^4 - 1}{2t^3} \mathrm{d}t, \sqrt{x + 1} = \frac{t^2 + 1}{2t}, t = \sqrt{x} + \sqrt{x + 1}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{x} + \sqrt{x + 1}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{t^4 - 1}{t^3(t + 1)}\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}\int \left(1 - \frac{1}{t} +\frac{1}{t^2} -\frac{1}{t^3}\right)\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}\left(t - \ln t - \frac{1}{t} +\frac{1}{2t^2}\right) + C_1$

$$
= \sqrt {x} - \frac {1}{2} \ln (\sqrt {x} + \sqrt {x + 1}) + \frac {x}{2} - \frac {1}{2} \sqrt {x (x + 1)} + C.
$$

【1936】证明：若 $p + q = kn$ ，式中 $\pmb{k}$ 为整数，则积分

$$
\int R [ x, (x - a) ^ {\frac {p}{n}} (x - b) ^ {\frac {q}{n}} ] \mathrm {d} x
$$

（式中 $R$ 为有理函数及 $p, q, n$ 为整数）为初等函数.

证 当 $a = b$ 时， $(x - a)^{\frac{p}{n}}(x - b)^{\frac{q}{n}} = (x - a)^{k}$ ，则积分显然为初等函数。

当 $a \neq b$ 时，设 $\frac{x - a}{x - b} = y (\neq 1)$ ，则

$$
x = \frac {a - b y}{1 - y}, \quad \mathrm {d} x = \frac {a - b}{(1 - y) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} y, \quad x - a = \frac {(a - b) y}{1 - y}, \quad x - b = \frac {a - b}{1 - y}.
$$

代入得 $\int R[x, (x - a)^{\frac{p}{n}}(x - b)^{\frac{q}{n}}] \mathrm{d}x = (a - b) \int R\left[\frac{a - by}{1 - y}, y^{\frac{p}{n}}\left(\frac{a - b}{1 - y}\right)^{k}\right] \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{(1 - y)^{2}}.$

再设 $\sqrt[n]{y} = t$ ，则 $y = t^n, \mathrm{d}y = nt^{n-1} \mathrm{d}t.$ 从而，上述积分化为

$$
\int R [ x, (x - a) ^ {\frac {p}{n}} (x - b) ^ {\frac {q}{n}} ] \mathrm {d} x = n (a - b) \int R \left[ \frac {a - b t ^ {n}}{1 - t ^ {n}}, t ^ {p} \left(\frac {a - b}{1 - t ^ {n}}\right) ^ {k} \right] \frac {t ^ {n} - 1}{(1 - t ^ {n}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} t,
$$

因为被积函数为 $t$ 的有理函数，所以，积分是初等函数

求最简单二次无理式的积分：

【1937】 $\int \frac{x^2}{\sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{x^2}{\sqrt{1 + x + x^2}} \, \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{x^2 + x + 1}{\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} \, \mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2} \int \frac{2x + 1}{\sqrt{1 + x + x^2}} \, \mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2} \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \sqrt {\left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}} d \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d \left(1 + x + x ^ {2}\right)}{\sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right)}{\sqrt {\left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}}} \\ = \frac {2 x + 1}{4} \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}} + \frac {3}{8} \ln \left(x + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}\right) - \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{2} \ln \left(x + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}\right) + C \\ = \frac {2 x - 3}{4} \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{8} \ln \left(x + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1938】+ $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}.$

解设 $x + 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ ，则 $x = \frac{1 - t}{t},\mathrm{d}t = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t,\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = \frac{\sqrt{t^2 - t + 1}}{|t|} = \operatorname {sgn}t\frac{\sqrt{t^2 - t + 1}}{t}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = -\operatorname {sgn}t\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{t^2 - t + 1}} = -\operatorname {sgn}t\ln \left|t - \frac{1}{2} +\sqrt{t^2 - t + 1}\right| + C_1$

$$
= - \operatorname {s g n} (x + 1) \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 [ \operatorname {s g n} (x + 1) ] \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{2 (x + 1)} \right| + C _ {1}.
$$

当 $x + 1 > 0$ 时， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = -\ln \left|\frac{1 - x + 2\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}{x + 1}\right| + C;$

当 $x + 1 <   0$ 时， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = \ln \left|\frac{1 - x - 2\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}{2(x + 1)}\right| + C_1$

$$
= \ln \left| \frac {- 3 (x + 1)}{2 (1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1})} \right| + C _ {1} = - \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} \right| + C.
$$

总之， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = -\ln \left|\frac{1 - x + 2\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}{x + 1}\right| + C.$

【1939】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x)^2\sqrt{1 - x^2}}.$

提示 令 $\sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}} = t.$

解 设 $\sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}} = t$ ，则 $x = \frac{1 - t^2}{1 + t^2}, \mathrm{d}x = -\frac{4t}{(1 + t^2)^2}\mathrm{d}t, 1 - x = \frac{2t^2}{1 + t^2}, \sqrt{1 - x^2} = \frac{2t}{1 + t^2}$ .

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x)^2\sqrt{1 - x^2}} = -\frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1 + t^2}{t^4}\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{6t^3} +\frac{1}{2t} +C = \frac{2 - x}{3(1 - x)^2}\sqrt{1 - x^2} +C.$

【1940】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2x + 2}}{x}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $\sqrt{x^2 + 2x + 2} = t - x$

解设 $\sqrt{x^2 + 2x + 2} = t - x$ ，则 $x = \frac{t^2 - 2}{2(t + 1)},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{t^2 + 2t + 2}{2(t + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}t,\sqrt{x^2 + 2x + 2} = \frac{t^2 + 2t + 2}{2(t + 1)}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2x + 2}}{x}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{(t^2 + 2t + 2)^2}{(t^2 - 2)(t + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}t$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} \int \left[ 1 + \frac {2}{t + 1} - \frac {1}{(t + 1) ^ {2}} - \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{t + \sqrt {2}} + \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{t - \sqrt {2}} \right] d t \\ = \frac {t}{2} + \ln | t + 1 | + \frac {1}{2 (t + 1)} - \sqrt {2} \ln \left| \frac {t + \sqrt {2}}{t - \sqrt {2}} \right| + C _ {1} \\ = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2 x + 2} + \ln (x + 1 + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2 x + 2}) - \sqrt {2} \ln \left| \frac {x + 2 + \sqrt {2 (x ^ {2} + 2 x + 2)}}{x} \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1941】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}}.$

提示 令 $1 + x = \frac{1}{t}$ ，并就 $1 + x > 0$ 及 $1 + x < 0$ 两种情况分别求解.

解设 $1 + x = \frac{1}{t}$ 则 $x = \frac{1 - t}{t},\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t,\sqrt{1 - x - x^2} = \frac{\sqrt{t^2 + t - 1}}{|t|} = \operatorname {sgn}t\frac{\sqrt{t^2 + t - 1}}{t}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}} = \int \left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}} -\frac{1}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}}\right)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {1 - x - x ^ {2}}} + \operatorname {s g n} t \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{\sqrt {t ^ {2} + t - 1}} \\ = \arcsin \left(\frac {2 x + 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + [ \operatorname {s g n} (1 + x) ] \ln \left| \frac {3 + x + 2 [ \operatorname {s g n} (x + 1) ] \sqrt {1 - x - x ^ {2}}}{2 (1 + x)} \right| + C _ {1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

当 $x + 1 > 0$ 时， $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}} = \arcsin \left(\frac{2x + 1}{\sqrt{5}}\right) + \ln \left|\frac{3 + x + 2\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}}{1 + x}\right| + C;$

当 $x + 1 <   0$ 时， $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}} = \arcsin \left(\frac{2x + 1}{\sqrt{5}}\right) - \ln \left|\frac{3 + x - 2\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}}{2(1 + x)}\right| + C_1$

$$
= \arcsin \left(\frac {2 x + 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + \ln \left| \frac {3 + x + 2 \sqrt {1 - x - x ^ {2}}}{1 + x} \right| + C.
$$

总之， $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}} = \arcsin \left(\frac{2x + 1}{\sqrt{5}}\right) + \ln \left|\frac{3 + x + 2\sqrt{1 - x - x^2}}{2(1 + x)}\right| + C.$

注 以后诸题中, 出现二次无理式时也会碰到用 $\operatorname{sgn} t$ 的问题, 可参照 1938 题及 1941 题类似地处理. 在解这类习题时, 不妨就开方后取正值求解. 如无特殊情况, 今后不再另加说明.

【1942】 $\int \frac{1 - x + x^2}{\sqrt{1 + x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{1 - x + x^2}{\sqrt{1 + x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{(x^2 - x - 1) + 2}{\sqrt{1 + x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = -\int \sqrt{\frac{5}{4} - \left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right)^2}\mathrm{d}\left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right) + 2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right)}{\sqrt{\frac{5}{4} - \left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right)^2}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1 - 2 x}{4} \sqrt {1 + x - x ^ {2}} - \frac {5}{8} \arcsin \left(\frac {2 x - 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + 2 \arcsin \left(\frac {2 x - 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + C \\ = \frac {1 - 2 x}{4} \sqrt {1 + x - x ^ {2}} - \frac {1 1}{8} \arcsin \left(\frac {1 - 2 x}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

利用公式 $\int \frac{P_n(x)}{y} \mathrm{d}x = Q_{n-1}(x)y + \lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{y}$ ，式中 $y = \sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c}$ ， $P_n(x)$ 为 $n$ 次多项式， $Q_{n-1}(x)$ 为 $n-1$ 次多项式及 $\lambda$ 为常数，求下列积分：

【1943】 $\int \frac{x^3}{\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\int \frac{x^3}{\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = (ax^2 +bx + c)\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}},$

两边对 $x$ 求导数，得

$$
\frac {x ^ {3}}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} = (2 a x + b) \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} + \frac {(a x ^ {2} + b x + c) (1 - x)}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} + \frac {\lambda}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}}.
$$

从而有

$$
x ^ {3} \equiv (2 a x + b) (1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}) + (a x ^ {2} + b x + c) (1 - x) + \lambda .
$$

比较等式两端 $x$ 的同次幂系数，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} x ^ {3} \left| - 3 a = 1, \right. \\ x ^ {2} \left| 5 a - 2 b = 0, \right. \\ x ^ {1} \left| 2 a + 3 b - c = 0, \right. \\ x ^ {0} \left| b + c + \lambda = 0. \right. \end{array}
$$

由此， $a = -\frac{1}{3},b = -\frac{5}{6},c = -\frac{19}{6},\lambda = 4.$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {x ^ {3}}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} d x = - \frac {1 9 + 5 x + 2 x ^ {2}}{6} \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} + 4 \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} \\ = - \frac {1 9 + 5 x + 2 x ^ {2}}{6} \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} + 4 \arcsin \left(\frac {x - 1}{\sqrt {2}}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1944】 $\int \frac{x^{10}}{\sqrt{1 + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\int \frac{x^{10}}{\sqrt{1 + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = (ax^9 +bx^8 +cx^7 +dx^6 +ex^5 +fx^4 +gx^3 +hx^2 +lx + m)\sqrt{1 + x^2} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + x^2}},$ 从而有

$$
\begin{array}{l} x ^ {1 0} \equiv (9 a x ^ {8} + 8 b x ^ {7} + 7 c x ^ {6} + 6 d x ^ {5} + 5 e x ^ {4} + 4 f x ^ {3} + 3 g x ^ {2} + 2 h x + l) (1 + x ^ {2}) \\ + x \left(a x ^ {9} + b x ^ {8} + c x ^ {7} + d x ^ {6} + e x ^ {5} + f x ^ {4} + g x ^ {3} + h x ^ {2} + l x + m\right) + \lambda . \\ \end{array}
$$

比较等式两端 $x$ 的同次幂系数，求得

$$
a = \frac {1}{1 0}, b = 0, c = - \frac {9}{8 0}, d = 0, e = \frac {2 1}{1 6 0}, f = 0, g = - \frac {2 1}{1 2 8}, h = 0, l = \frac {6 3}{2 5 6}, m = 0, \lambda = - \frac {6 3}{2 5 6}.
$$

于是， $\int \frac{x^{10}}{\sqrt{1 + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = \left(\frac{63}{256} x - \frac{21}{128} x^3 +\frac{21}{160} x^5 -\frac{9}{80} x^7 +\frac{1}{10} x^9\right)\sqrt{1 + x^2} -\frac{63}{256}\ln (x + \sqrt{1 + x^2}) + C.$

【1945】 $\int x^4\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^4\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{x^4(a^2 - x^2)}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = (Ax^5 +Bx^4 +Cx^3 +Dx^2 +Ex + F)\sqrt{a^2 - x^2} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}},$

从而有 $x^4 (a^2 - x^2) \equiv (5Ax^4 + 4Bx^3 + 3Cx^2 + 2Dx + E)(a^2 - x^2) - x(Ax^5 + Bx^4 + Cx^3 + Dx^2 + Ex + F) + \lambda.$

比较等式两端 $x$ 同次幂的系数，求得

$$
A = \frac {1}{6}, \quad B = 0, \quad C = - \frac {a ^ {2}}{2 4}, \quad D = 0, E = - \frac {a ^ {4}}{1 6}, \quad F = 0, \quad \lambda = \frac {a ^ {4}}{1 6}.
$$

于是， $\int x^4\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}\mathrm{d}x = \left(\frac{1}{6} x^5 -\frac{a^2}{24} x^3 -\frac{a^4}{16} x\right)\sqrt{a^2 - x^2} +\frac{a^4}{16}\arcsin \frac{x}{|a|} +C(a\neq 0).$

【1946】 $\int \frac{x^3 - 6x^2 + 11x - 6}{\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\int \frac{x^3 - 6x^2 + 11x - 6}{\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3}}\mathrm{d}x = (ax^2 +bx + c)\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3}},$

从而有 $x^{3} - 6x^{2} + 11x - 6 \equiv (2ax + b)(x^{2} + 4x + 3) + (x + 2)(ax^{2} + bx + c) + \lambda.$

比较等式两端 $x$ 同次幂的系数，求得 $a = \frac{1}{3}, b = -\frac{14}{3}, c = 37, \lambda = -66.$

于是， $\int \frac{x^3 - 6x^2 + 11x - 6}{\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3}}\mathrm{d}x = \left(\frac{1}{3} x^2 -\frac{14}{3} x + 37\right)\sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3} -66\ln \left|x + 2 + \sqrt{x^2 + 4x + 3}\right| + C.$

【1947】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^3\sqrt{x^2 + 1}}.$

解设 $x = \frac{1}{t}$ ，则 $\mathrm{dx} = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{dt}$ ，这里碰到二次无理式 $\sqrt{x^2 + 1}$ 需引用 $\operatorname {sgn}t$ 的问题，不妨设

$$
\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 1} = \frac {\sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}}{t} (t > 0).
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^3\sqrt{x^2 + 1}} = -\int \frac{t^2}{\sqrt{t^2 + 1}}\mathrm{d}t = -\int \frac{(t^2 + 1) - 1}{\sqrt{t^2 + 1}}\mathrm{d}t = -\int \sqrt{t^2 + 1}\mathrm{d}t + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{t^2 + 1}}$

$$
= - \frac {t}{2} \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1} - \frac {1}{2} \ln | t + \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1} | + \ln | t + \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1} | + C = - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 1}}{2 x ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {1 + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 1}}{| x |} + C.
$$

【1948】+ $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^4\sqrt{x^2 - 1}}.$

解 不妨设 $x = \frac{1}{t} > 0$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 由 $|x| > 1$ 知必有 $|t| < 1$ ，则有

$$
\sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} = \frac {\sqrt {1 - t ^ {2}}}{t} \quad (0 <   t <   1).
$$

代人得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^4\sqrt{x^2 - 1}} = -\int \frac{t^3}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}\mathrm{d}t = \int \frac{t(1 - t^2) - t}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}\mathrm{d}t = \int t\sqrt{1 - t^2}\mathrm{d}t - \int \frac{t}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}\mathrm{d}t$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{2} \int (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {1}{2}} d (1 - t ^ {2}) + \frac {1}{2} \int (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} d (1 - t ^ {2}) = - \frac {1}{3} (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {1}{2}} + C \\ = \frac {1 + 2 x ^ {2}}{3 x ^ {3}} \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1949】+ $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^3\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 1}}.$

解设 $x - 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 不妨设 $t > 0$ ，则有

$$
\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 3 x + 1} = \frac {\sqrt {5 t ^ {2} + 5 t + 1}}{t}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^3\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 1}} = -\int \frac{t^2}{\sqrt{5t^2 + 5t + 1}}\mathrm{d}t = (at + b)\sqrt{5t^2 + 5t + 1} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{5t^2 + 5t + 1}},$

从而有 $-t^{2} \equiv a(1 + 5t + 5t^{2}) + \left(5t + \frac{5}{2}\right)(at + b) + \lambda.$

比较等式两端 $t$ 的同次幂系数，求得 $a = -\frac{1}{10}, b = \frac{3}{20}, \lambda = -\frac{11}{40}.$

于是， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^3\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 1}} = \left(-\frac{t}{10} +\frac{3}{20}\right)\sqrt{5t^2 + 5t + 1} -\frac{11}{40}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{5t^2 + 5t + 1}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {3 - 2 t}{2 0} \sqrt {5 t ^ {2} + 5 t + 1} - \frac {1 1}{4 0 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| t + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {t ^ {2} + t + \frac {1}{5}} \right| + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {3 x - 5}{2 0 (x - 1) ^ {2}} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 3 x + 1} - \frac {1 1}{4 0 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {5} (x + 1) + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 3 x + 1}}{x - 1} \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1950】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x + 1)^3\sqrt{x^2 + 2x}}.$

解设 $x + 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ 则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 先设 $t > 0$ ，则有 $\sqrt{x^2 + 2x} = \frac{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}{t}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x + 1)^5\sqrt{x^2 + 2x}} = -\int \frac{t^4}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}\mathrm{d}t = (at^3 +bt^2 +ct + e)\sqrt{1 - t^2} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}.$

从而有 $-t^4 \equiv (3at^2 + 2bt + c)(1 - t^2) - t(at^3 + bt^2 + ct + e) + \lambda.$

比较等式两端 $t$ 的同次幂系数，求得 $a = \frac{1}{4}, b = 0, c = \frac{3}{8}, e = 0, \lambda = -\frac{3}{8}.$

于是， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x + 1)^5\sqrt{x^2 + 2x}} = \left(\frac{1}{4} t^3 +\frac{3}{8} t\right)\sqrt{1 - t^2} -\frac{3}{8}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 - t^2}}$

$$
= \frac {3 x ^ {2} + 6 x + 5}{8 (x + 1) ^ {4}} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2 x} - \frac {3}{8} \arcsin \frac {1}{x + 1} + C.
$$

再设 $t < 0$ ，则答案前一项不改变符号，但后一项要改变符号，因此，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) ^ {5} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2 x}} = \frac {3 x ^ {2} + 6 x + 5}{8 (x + 1) ^ {4}} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2 x} - \frac {3}{8} \arcsin \frac {1}{| x + 1 |} + C,
$$

其中 $x > 0$ 或 $x < -2$ .

【1951】在什么条件下，积分 $\int \frac{a_1x^2 + b_1x + c_1}{\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c}}\mathrm{d}x$ 是代数函数？

解设 $\int \frac{a_1x^2 + b_1x + c_1}{\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c}}\mathrm{d}x = (Ax + B)\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c} +\lambda \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c}},$

从而有 $a_{1}x^{2} + b_{1}x + c_{1}\equiv A(ax^{2} + bx + c) + \left(ax + \frac{b}{2}\right)(Ax + B) + \lambda .$

比较等式两端 $x$ 的同次幂系数，当 $a \neq 0$ 时求得

$$
A = \frac {a _ {1}}{2 a}, \quad B = \frac {4 a b _ {1} - 3 a _ {1} b}{4 a ^ {2}}, \lambda = \frac {8 a ^ {2} c _ {1} + 3 a _ {1} b ^ {2} - 4 a (a _ {1} c + b b _ {1})}{8 a ^ {2}}.
$$

于是，当 $a \neq 0$ 且 $8a^2c_1 + 3a_1b^2 = 4a(a_1c + bb_1)$ 时， $\lambda = 0$ ，积分为代数函数；当 $a = 0$ 时积分显然为代数函数。

分解有理函数 $\frac{P(x)}{Q(x)}$ 为最简分式，求积分 $\int \frac{P(x)}{Q(x)y} \, \mathrm{d}x$ ，式中 $y = \sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c}$ 。

【1952】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^2\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}.$

解 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^2\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^2\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}} +\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}.$

设 $x - 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ 则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 不妨设 $t > 0$ ，则有 $\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2} = \frac{\sqrt{2t^2 - 1}}{t}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)^2\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}} = -\int \frac{t\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{2t^2 - 1}} -\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{2t^2 - 1}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{2} \sqrt {2 t ^ {2} - 1} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln | \sqrt {2} t + \sqrt {2 t ^ {2} - 1} | + C \\ = \frac {\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}}{2 (1 - x)} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {2} + \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}}{1 - x} \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1953】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - 1)\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - 1)\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \left(\frac{1}{x + 1} +\frac{1}{x - 1}\right)\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1}}$

$$
= \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - x - 1}} + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x - 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - x - 1}} = \frac {1}{2} I _ {1} + \frac {1}{2} I _ {2}.
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，设 $x + 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ 则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 不妨设 $t > 0$ ，则有 $\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1} = \frac{\sqrt{t^2 - 3t + 1}}{t}.$

代入 $I_{1}$ ，得 $I_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x + 1)\sqrt{x^{2} - x - 1}} = -\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{t^{2} - 3t + 1}} = -\ln \left|t - \frac{3}{2} +\sqrt{t^{2} - 3t + 1}\right| + C_{1}$

$$
= - \ln \left| \frac {3 x + 1 - 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} - x - 1}}{x + 1} \right| + C _ {2};
$$

对于 $I_{2}$ ，设 $x - 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ ，同上可得 $I_{2} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x - 1)\sqrt{x^{2} - x - 1}} = \arcsin \left(\frac{x - 3}{|x - 1|\sqrt{5}}\right) + C_{3}.$

于是， $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - 1)\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1}} = -\frac{1}{2}\ln \left|\frac{3x + 1 - 2\sqrt{x^2 - x - 1}}{x + 1}\right| + \frac{1}{2}\arcsin \left(\frac{x - 3}{|x - 1|\sqrt{5}}\right) + C.$

【1954】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}{(x + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}{(x + 1)^2} \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{x^2 + x + 1}{(x + 1)^2} \cdot \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = \int \frac{(x + 1)^2 - (x + 1) + 1}{(x + 1)^2} \cdot \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}$

$$
= \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) ^ {2} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} = I _ {1} - I _ {2} + I _ {3}.
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，显然有

对于 $I_{2}$ ，利用1938题的结果，即得

$$
I _ {2} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} = - \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} \right| + C _ {2};
$$

对于 $I_{3}$ ，设 $x + 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ 则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2}\mathrm{d}t.$ 不妨设 $t > 0$ ，则有 $\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = \frac{\sqrt{t^2 - t + 1}}{t}.$

代入 $I_{3}$ ，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \sqrt {t ^ {2} - t + 1} - \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| t - \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {t ^ {2} - t + 1} \right| + C _ {3} \\ = - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} - \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} \right| + C _ {4}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{(x + 1) ^ {2}} d x = \ln \left(x + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}\right) - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} \right| + C.
$$

如用下述解法更简单些：

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{(x + 1) ^ {2}} d x = - \int \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} d \left(\frac {1}{x + 1}\right) = - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} + \int \frac {\left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) d x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} \\ = - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} \\ = - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} + \ln \left(x + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}\right) + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \frac {1 - x + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{x + 1} \right| ^ {*}) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）利用1938题的结果.

【1955】 $\int \frac{x^3}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{x^3}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{(x^3 + 1) - 1}{(1 + x)\sqrt{1 + 2x - x^2}}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {x ^ {2} - x + 1}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} d x - \int \frac {d x}{(1 + x) \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} \\ = - \int \frac {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} d x + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {(2 x - 2) d x}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} + 3 \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} - \int \frac {d x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} \\ = - \int \sqrt {2 - (x - 1) ^ {2}} d (x - 1) - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d (1 + 2 x - x ^ {2})}{\sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} + 3 \int \frac {d (x - 1)}{\sqrt {2 - (x - 1) ^ {2}}} - I _ {1} \\ = \frac {1 - x}{2} \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} - \arcsin \left(\frac {x - 1}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} + 3 \arcsin \left(\frac {x - 1}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - I _ {1} \\ = - \frac {x + 1}{2} \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} + 2 \arcsin \left(\frac {x - 1}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - I _ {1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，设 $x + 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ ，可得

$$
I _ {1} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arcsin \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{x + 1}\right) + C _ {1}.
$$

于是，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {x ^ {3}}{(x + 1) \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} d x = - \frac {1 + x}{2} \sqrt {1 + 2 x - x ^ {2}} - 2 \arcsin \left(\frac {1 - x}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arcsin \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{1 + x}\right) + C.
$$

【1956】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - 3x + 2)\sqrt{x^2 - 4x + 3}}.$

解 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - 3x + 2)\sqrt{x^2 - 4x + 3}} = \int \left(\frac{2}{x - 2} -\frac{1}{x - 1}\right)\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 - 4x + 3}}$

$$
= \int \frac {2 \mathrm {d} x}{(x - 2) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}} - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x - 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}} = 2 I _ {1} - I _ {2}.
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，设 $x - 2 = \frac{1}{t}$ 可得

$$
I _ {1} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x - 2) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}} = - \arcsin \left(\frac {1}{| x - 2 |}\right) + C _ {1};
$$

对于 $I_{2}$ ，设 $x - 1 = \frac{1}{t}$ 可得

$$
I _ {2} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x - 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}} = \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}}{x - 1} + C _ {2}.
$$

于是，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {x \mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} - 3 x + 2) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}} = - 2 \arcsin \left(\frac {1}{| x - 2 |}\right) - \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - 4 x + 3}}{x - 1} + C,
$$

其中 $x < 1$ 或 $x > 3$ .

【1957】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x^2)\sqrt{1 - x^2}}.$

解设 $x = \sin t$ ，并限制 $-\frac{\pi}{2} < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = \cos t\mathrm{d}t,\quad \sqrt{1 - x^2} = \cos t.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x^2)\sqrt{1 - x^2}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + \sin^2 t} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{2\sin^2 t + \cos^2 t} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sqrt{2} \tan t)}{(\sqrt{2} \tan t)^2 + 1}$

$$
= \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan (\sqrt {2} \tan t) + C = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{\sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}}\right) + C.
$$

【1958】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 1)\sqrt{x^2 - 1}}.$

解当 $x > 1$ 时，设 $x = \mathrm{sect}$ ，并限制 $0 < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ ，则 $\mathrm{dx} = \mathrm{sect}\tan t\mathrm{dt},\quad \sqrt{x^2 - 1} = \tan t.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 1)\sqrt{x^2 - 1}} = \int \frac{\sec t\mathrm{d}t}{1 + \sec^2t} = \int \frac{\cos t}{\cos^2t + 1}\mathrm{d}t = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sin t)}{2 - \sin^2t}$

$$
= \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {2} + \sin t}{\sqrt {2} - \sin t} \right| + C = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {2} x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}}{\sqrt {2} x - \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}} \right| + C.
$$

当 $x < -1$ 时，仍设 $x = \sec t$ ，但限制 $\pi < t < \frac{3}{2}\pi$ ，经计算可获得同样的结果。

总之，当 $|x| > 1$ 时，

$$
\int \frac {d x}{(x ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}} = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {x \sqrt {2} + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}}{x \sqrt {2} - \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}} \right| + C.
$$

【1959】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x^4)\sqrt{1 + x^2}}.$

解设 $x = \tan t$ ，并限制 $-\frac{\pi}{2} < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ 且 $|t| \neq \frac{\pi}{4}$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = \sec^2 t \, \mathrm{d}t$ ， $\sqrt{1 + x^2} = \sec t.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x^4)\sqrt{x^2 + 1}} = \int \frac{\sec^2 t \, \mathrm{d}t}{(1 - \tan^4 t) \sec t} = \int \frac{\cos^3 t \, \mathrm{d}t}{1 - 2\sin^2 t} = \int \frac{1 - \sin^2 t}{1 - 2\sin^2 t} \, \mathrm{d}(\sin t)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {1 - 2 \sin^ {2} t}{1 - 2 \sin^ {2} t} d (\sin t) + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d (\sin t)}{1 - 2 \sin^ {2} t} = \frac {1}{2} \sin t + \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {1 + \sqrt {2} \sin t}{1 - \sqrt {2} \sin t} \right| + C \\ = \frac {x}{2 \sqrt {1 + x ^ {2}}} + \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {1 + x ^ {2}} + x \sqrt {2}}{\sqrt {1 + x ^ {2}} - x \sqrt {2}} \right| + C \quad (| x | \neq 1). \\ \end{array}
$$

【1960】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2}}{x^2 + 1}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2}}{x^2 + 1}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{(x^2 + 2)\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + 2}} = \int \left(1 + \frac{1}{x^2 + 1}\right)\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + 2}}$

$$
= \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2}} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2}} = \ln (x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2}) + I _ {1}.
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，设 $x = \sqrt{2} \tan t$ ，并限制 $-\frac{\pi}{2} < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ 则 $\mathrm{dx} = \sqrt{2} \sec^2 t \, \mathrm{dt}$ ， $\sqrt{x^2 + 2} = \sqrt{2} \sec t$

代入得 $I_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^{2} + 1)\sqrt{x^{2} + 2}} = \int \frac{\sec t\mathrm{d}t}{1 + 2\tan^{2}t} = \int \frac{\cos t\mathrm{d}t}{1 + \sin^{2}t} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sin t)}{1 + \sin^{2}t} = \arctan (\sin t) + C_{1}$

$$
= \arctan \left(\frac {x}{\sqrt {2 + x ^ {2}}}\right) + C _ {1} = - \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 2}}{x}\right) + C.
$$

于是，最后得到 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2}}{x^2 + 1} \mathrm{d}x = \ln (x + \sqrt{x^2 + 2}) - \arctan \left(\frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 2}}{x}\right) + C.$

化二次三项式为标准形式，计算下列积分：

【1961】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x - 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x - 1}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left[\left(x + \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 + \frac{3}{4}\right]\sqrt{\left(x + \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 - \frac{5}{4}}.$

当 $x + \frac{1}{2} > \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}$ 时，设 $x + \frac{1}{2} = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2} \sec t$ ，并限制 $0 < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ ，则

$$
\mathrm {d} x = \frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} \sec t \tan t \mathrm {d} t, \quad \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x - 1} = \frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} \tan t, \quad x ^ {2} + x + 1 = \frac {1}{4} (5 \sec^ {2} t + 3).
$$

代人得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x - 1}} = 4\int \frac{\sec t\mathrm{d}t}{5\sec^2t + 3} = 4\int \frac{\cos t\mathrm{d}t}{5 + 3\cos^2t} = 4\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sqrt{3}\sin t)}{(\sqrt{8})^2 - (\sqrt{3}\sin t)^2}$

$$
= 4 \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \cdot \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {8}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {8} + \sqrt {3} \sin t}{\sqrt {8} - \sqrt {3} \sin t} \right| + C = \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} \left| \frac {(2 x + 1) \sqrt {2} + \sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x - 1)}}{(2 x + 1) \sqrt {2} - \sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x - 1)}} \right| + C.
$$

当 $x + \frac{1}{2} < -\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}$ 时，仍设 $x + \frac{1}{2} = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}\sec t$ 但限制 $\pi < t < \frac{3}{2}\pi.$ 经计算可获同样的结果.

总之，当 $\left|x + \frac{1}{2}\right| > \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}$ 时，

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} + x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x - 1}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {(2 x + 1) \sqrt {2} + \sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x - 1)}}{(2 x + 1) \sqrt {2} - \sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x - 1)}} \right| + C.
$$

【1962】 $\int \frac{x^2\mathrm{d}x}{(4 - 2x + x^2)\sqrt{2 + 2x - x^2}}.$

解 $\int \frac{x^2\mathrm{d}x}{(4 - 2x + x^2)\sqrt{2 + 2x - x^2}} = \int \frac{(x - 1)^2 + 2(x - 1) + 1}{[3 + (x - 1)^2]\sqrt{3 - (x - 1)^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

设 $x - 1 = \sqrt{3}\sin t$ ，并限制 $-\frac{\pi}{2} < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ 则 $\mathrm{dx} = \sqrt{3}\cos t\mathrm{dt},\sqrt{2 + 2x - x^2} = \sqrt{3}\cos t.$

代入得 $\int \frac{x^2\mathrm{d}x}{(4 - 2x + x^2)\sqrt{2 + 2x - x^2}} = \int \frac{1 + 2\sqrt{3}\sin t + 3\sin^2t}{3(1 + \sin^2t)}\mathrm{d}t$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \mathrm {d} t + \frac {2}{\sqrt {3}} \int \frac {\sin t}{1 + \sin^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t - \frac {2}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{1 + \sin^ {2} t} = t - \frac {2}{\sqrt {3}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cos t)}{2 - \cos^ {2} t} - \frac {2}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\tan t)}{1 + 2 \tan^ {2} t} \\ = t - \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {2} + \cos t}{\sqrt {2} - \cos t} \right| - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{3} \arctan (\sqrt {2} \tan t) + C \\ = \arcsin \frac {x - 1}{\sqrt {3}} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {6} + \sqrt {2 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}}{\sqrt {6} - \sqrt {2 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{3} \arctan \frac {(x - 1) \sqrt {2}}{\sqrt {2 + 2 x - x ^ {2}}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1963】 $\int \frac{(x + 1)\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{(x + 1)\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = \int \frac{\left(x + \frac{1}{2}\right) + \frac{1}{2}}{\left[\left(x + \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 + \frac{3}{4}\right]^{\frac{3}{2}}}\mathrm{d}\left(x + \frac{1}{2}\right)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) d \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right)}{\left[ \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right)}{\left[ \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} \\ = \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left[ \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4} \right]}{\left[ \left(x + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} + \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {x + \frac {1}{2}}{\frac {3}{4} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} \\ = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} + \frac {2 x + 1}{3 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} + C = \frac {2 (x - 1)}{3 \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1781题的结果.

【1964】利用分式线性代换 $x = \frac{\alpha + \beta t}{1 + t}$ ，计算积分： $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 - x + 1)\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}$

解 分式线性代换 $x = \frac{\alpha + \beta t}{1 + t}$ 给出

$$
x ^ {2} \pm x + 1 = \frac {\left(\beta^ {2} \pm \beta + 1\right) t ^ {2} + \left[ 2 \alpha \beta \pm (\alpha + \beta) + 2 \right] t + \left(\alpha^ {2} \pm \alpha + 1\right)}{(1 + t) ^ {2}}.
$$

要求 $2\alpha \beta \pm (\alpha + \beta) + 2 = 0$ 即化成标准形式，当 $\alpha + \beta = 0$ 及 $\alpha \beta = -1$ 时即得上式.例如，取 $\alpha = -1$ ， $\beta = 1$

我们有 $x = \frac{t - 1}{1 + t}$ 或 $t = \frac{1 + x}{1 - x},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2\mathrm{d}t}{(1 + t)^2},x^2 -x + 1 = \frac{t^2 + 3}{(t + 1)^2},\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = \frac{\sqrt{1 + 3t^2}}{t + 1},$

其中不妨设 $t + 1 > 0$ ，于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} - x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} = 2 \int \frac {t + 1}{(t ^ {2} + 3) \sqrt {1 + 3 t ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} t = 2 \int \frac {t \mathrm {d} t}{(t ^ {2} + 3) \sqrt {1 + 3 t ^ {2}}} + 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(t ^ {2} + 3) \sqrt {1 + 3 t ^ {2}}} \\ = 2 \left(I _ {1} + I _ {2}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

对于 $I_{1}$ ，设 $u = \sqrt{1 + 3t^2}$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}u = \frac{3t\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + 3t^2}}, t^2 + 3 = \frac{u^2 + 8}{3}.$

代入 $I_{1}$ ，得

$$
I _ {1} = \int \frac {t d t}{(t ^ {2} + 3) \sqrt {1 + 3 t ^ {2}}} = \int \frac {d u}{u ^ {2} + 8} = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {u}{2 \sqrt {2}}\right) + C _ {1} = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{(1 - x) \sqrt {2}}\right) + C _ {1}.
$$

对于 $I_{2}$ ，设 $u = \frac{3t}{\sqrt{1 + 3t^2}}$ 则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + 3t^2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{3 - u^2}, t^2 + 3 = \frac{27 - 8u^2}{3(3 - u^2)},$

代入 $I_{2}$ ，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {2} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(t ^ {2} + 3) \sqrt {1 + 3 t ^ {2}}} = 3 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u}{2 7 - 8 u ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {3 \sqrt {3} + 2 \sqrt {2} u}{3 \sqrt {3} - 2 \sqrt {2} u} \right| + C _ {2} \\ = \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x + 1)} + (x + 1) \sqrt {2}}{\sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x + 1)} - (x + 1) \sqrt {2}} \right| + C _ {2} = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - x + 1}}{\sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x + 1)} - (x + 1) \sqrt {2}} \right| + C _ {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} - x + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}} = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan \left[ \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1}}{(x - 1) \sqrt {2}} \right] + \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - x + 1}}{\sqrt {3 (x ^ {2} + x + 1)} - (x + 1) \sqrt {2}} \right| + C.
$$

【1965】+ 求 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 2)\sqrt{2x^2 - 2x + 5}}.$

解此题与1964题均属于下述类型的积分

$$
\int \frac {M x + N}{(x ^ {2} + p x + q) ^ {m} \sqrt {a x ^ {2} + b x + c}} d x
$$

（参看微积分学教程（Γ.M.菲赫金哥尔茨）第二卷第一分册55页“272.其他的计算方法”）

设 $x = \frac{\alpha + \beta t}{1 + t}$ ，适当选择 $\alpha$ 与 $\beta$ ，使得在两个三项式中同时消去一次项。为此，将 $x = \frac{\alpha + \beta t}{1 + t}$ 分别代入 $x^2 + 2$ 及 $2x^2 - 2x + 5$ 中，并令一次项的系数等于零，求得

$$
\alpha = - 1, \quad \beta = 2,
$$

即设 $x = \frac{2t - 1}{1 + t}$ 从而有

$$
\mathrm {d} x = \frac {3}{(t + 1) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} t, \quad x ^ {2} + 2 = \frac {3 (2 t ^ {2} + 1)}{(t + 1) ^ {2}}, \sqrt {2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5} = \frac {3 \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}}{| t + 1 |}.
$$

以下不妨设 $t + 1 > 0$ 代入得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} + 2) \sqrt {2 x - 2 x + 5}} = \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {t + 1}{(2 t ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}} \mathrm {d} t = \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {t \mathrm {d} t}{(2 t ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}} + \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(2 t ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}}.
$$

对于右端的第一个积分，设 $u = \sqrt{t^2 + 1}$ ，代入后计算得

$$
\frac {1}{3} \int \frac {t d t}{(2 t ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}} = \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {d u}{2 u ^ {2} - 1} = \frac {1}{6 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {2} u - 1}{\sqrt {2} u + 1} + C _ {1} = \frac {1}{6 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {2 (2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5)} + (x - 2)}{\sqrt {2 (2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5)} - (x - 2)} + C _ {1}.
$$

对于右端的第二个积分，设 $u = \frac{t}{\sqrt{t^2 + 1}}$ ，代入后计算得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(2 t ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {t ^ {2} + 1}} = \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u}{1 + u ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{3} \arctan u + C _ {2} = \frac {1}{3} \arctan \left(\frac {1 + x}{\sqrt {2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5}}\right) + C _ {2} \\ = - \frac {1}{3} \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt {2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5}}{x + 1}\right) + C _ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，最后得到 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 2)\sqrt{2x^2 - 2x + 5}}$

$$
= \frac {1}{6 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {2 (2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5)} + (x - 2)}{\sqrt {2 (2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5)} - (x - 2)} - \frac {1}{3} \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt {2 x ^ {2} - 2 x + 5}}{x + 1}\right) + C.
$$

# 利用欧拉代换

（1）若 $a > 0$ ， $\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c} = \pm \sqrt{a} x + z$ （2）若 $c > 0$ ， $\sqrt{ax^2 + bx + c} = xz\pm \sqrt{c}$   
(3) $\sqrt{a(x - x_1)(x - x_2)} = z(x - x_1)$ .

求下列积分：

【1966】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}}.$

提示 令 $\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = z - x$ .

解设 $\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = z - x$ ，则 $x = \frac{z^2 - 1}{1 + 2z},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2(z^2 + z + 1)}{(1 + 2z)^2}\mathrm{d}z,\sqrt{x^2 + x + 1} = \frac{z^2 + z + 1}{1 + 2z}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{z^2 + z + 1}{z\left(z + \frac{1}{2}\right)^2}\mathrm{d}z = \frac{1}{2}\int \left[\frac{4}{z} -\frac{3}{z + \frac{1}{2}} -\frac{3}{2\left(z + \frac{1}{2}\right)^2}\right]\mathrm{d}z$

$$
= \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {z ^ {4}}{\left| z + \frac {1}{2} \right| ^ {3}} + \frac {3}{4 \left(z + \frac {1}{2}\right)} + C _ {1} = \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {z ^ {4}}{\left| 2 z + 1 \right| ^ {3}} + \frac {3}{2 (2 z + 1)} + C,
$$

其中 $z = x + \sqrt{x^2 + x + 1}$

【1967】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{1 - 2x - x^2}}.$

提示 令 $\sqrt{1 - 2x - x^2} = xz - 1$

解设 $\sqrt{1 - 2x - x^2} = xz - 1$ ，则

$$
z = \frac {1 + \sqrt {1 - 2 x - x ^ {2}}}{x}, \quad x = \frac {2 (z - 1)}{z ^ {2} + 1}, d x = \frac {2 (1 + 2 z - z ^ {2})}{(z ^ {2} + 1) ^ {2}} d z, \quad \sqrt {1 - 2 x - x ^ {2}} + 1 = \frac {2 z (z - 1)}{z ^ {2} + 1}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{1 - 2x - x^2}} = \int \frac{1 + 2z - z^2}{z(z - 1)(z^2 + 1)}\mathrm{d}z = \int \left[\frac{1}{z - 1} -\frac{1}{z} -\frac{2}{z^2 + 1}\right]\mathrm{d}z$

$$
= \ln \left| \frac {z - 1}{z} \right| - 2 \arctan z + C,
$$

其中 $z = \frac{1 + \sqrt{1 - 2x - x^2}}{x}$

【1968】 $\int x\sqrt{x^2 - 2x + 2}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\sqrt{x^2 - 2x + 2} = z - x$ ，则 $x = \frac{z^2 - 2}{2(z - 1)},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{z^2 - 2z + 2}{2(z - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z,\sqrt{x^2 - 2x + 2} = \frac{z^2 - 2z + 2}{2(z - 1)}.$

代人得 $\int x\sqrt{x^2 - 2x + 2}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{8}\int \frac{(z^2 - 2)(z^2 - 2z + 2)^2}{(z - 1)^4}\mathrm{d}z$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{8} \int \frac {\left[ (z - 1) ^ {2} + 2 (z - 1) - 1 \right] \left[ (z - 1) ^ {2} + 1 \right] ^ {2}}{(z - 1) ^ {4}} d z \\ = \frac {1}{8} \int \left\{\left[ (z - 1) ^ {2} - (z - 1) ^ {- 4} \right] + \left[ 2 (z - 1) + 2 (z - 1) ^ {- 3} \right] + \left[ 1 - (z - 1) ^ {- 2} \right] + 4 (z - 1) ^ {- 1} \right\} d (z - 1) \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
= \frac {1}{8} \left\{\frac {1}{3} \left[ (z - 1) ^ {3} + (z - 1) ^ {- 3} \right] + \left[ (z - 1) ^ {2} - (z - 1) ^ {2} \right] + \left[ (z - 1) + (z - 1) ^ {- 1} \right] \right\} + \frac {1}{2} \ln | z - 1 | + C,
$$

其中 $z = x + \sqrt{x^2 - 2x + 2}$

【1969】 $\int \frac{x - \sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2}}{x + \sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2}x}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2} = z(x + 1)$

解设 $\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2} = z(x + 1)$ ，则 $x = \frac{2 - z^2}{z^2 - 1},\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{2z}{(z^2 - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z,\quad \sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2} = \frac{z}{z^2 - 1}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{x - \sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2}}{x + \sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{2z(2 - z - z^2)}{(z^2 - z - 2)(z^2 - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \left[ - \frac {1 7}{1 0 8 (z + 1)} + \frac {5}{1 8 (z + 1) ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{3 (z + 1) ^ {3}} + \frac {3}{4 (z - 1)} - \frac {1 6}{2 7 (z - 2)} \right] d z \\ = - \frac {1 7}{1 0 8} \ln | z + 1 | - \frac {5}{1 8 (z + 1)} - \frac {1}{6 (z + 1) ^ {2}} + \frac {3}{4} \ln | z - 1 | - \frac {1 6}{2 7} \ln | z - 2 | + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 3x + 2}}{x + 1}.$

【1970】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{[1 + \sqrt{x(1 + x)}]^2}$

解设 $\sqrt{x(1 + x)} = z + x$ ，则 $x = \frac{z^2}{1 - 2z},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2z(1 - z)}{(1 - 2z)^2}\mathrm{d}z,1 + \sqrt{x(1 + x)} = \frac{1 - z - z^2}{1 - 2z}.$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{[1 + \sqrt{x(1 + x)}]^2} = 2\int \frac{z(1 - z)}{(1 - z - z^2)^2}\mathrm{d}z = 2\int \frac{(1 - z - z^2) + (2z + 1) - 2}{(1 - z - z^2)^2}\mathrm{d}z$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} z}{1 - z - z ^ {2}} - 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (1 - z - z ^ {2})}{(1 - z - z ^ {2}) ^ {2}} - 4 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 - z - z ^ {2}) ^ {2}} \\ = 2 \int \frac {d (z + \frac {1}{2})}{\frac {5}{4} - (z + \frac {1}{2}) ^ {2}} + \frac {2}{1 - z - z ^ {2}} - 4 \left\{\frac {2 z + 1}{5 (1 - z - z ^ {2})} + \frac {2}{5} \int \frac {d (z + \frac {1}{2})}{\frac {5}{4} - (z + \frac {1}{2}) ^ {2}} * \right\} \\ = \frac {2}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} + z + \frac {1}{2}}{\frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} - z - \frac {1}{2}} \right| + \frac {2}{1 - z - z ^ {2}} - \frac {4 (2 z + 1)}{5 (1 - z - z ^ {2})} + C = \frac {2}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {5} + 2 z + 1}{\sqrt {5} - 2 z - 1} \right| + \frac {2 (3 - 4 z)}{5 (1 - z - z ^ {2})} + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \sqrt{x(1 + x)} -x.$

\*) 利用 1921 题的递推公式.

利用不同方法，计算下列积分：

【1971】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + 1} - \sqrt{x^2 - 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^2 + 1} - \sqrt{x^2 - 1}} = \int \frac{\sqrt{x^2 + 1} + \sqrt{x^2 - 1}}{(x^2 + 1) - (x^2 - 1)}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \sqrt{x^2 + 1}\mathrm{d}x + \frac{1}{2}\int \sqrt{x^2 - 1}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {x}{4} (\sqrt {x ^ {2} + 1} + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}) + \frac {1}{4} \ln \left| \frac {x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} + 1}}{x + \sqrt {x ^ {2} - 1}} \right| + C.
$$

【1972】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x^3)\sqrt{1 - x^2}}.$

提示 令 $\frac{1 + x}{1 - x} = z$ ，并利用1884题的结果.

解设 $\frac{1 + x}{1 - x} = z$ ，则 $x = \frac{z - 1}{z + 1},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2}{(z + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z.$

代入得 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 - x^3)\sqrt{1 - x^2}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{(z^2 - 1)\mathrm{d}z}{\sqrt{z}(3z^2 + 1)} = \int \frac{(z^2 - 1)\mathrm{d}(\sqrt{z})}{3z^2 + 1} = \int \left[\frac{1}{3} -\frac{4}{3(3z^2 + 1)}\right]\mathrm{d}(\sqrt{z})$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {\sqrt {z}}{3} - \frac {4}{3} \cdot \frac {1}{\sqrt [ 4 ]{3}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\sqrt [ 4 ]{3 z ^ {2}})}{(\sqrt [ 4 ]{3 z ^ {2}}) ^ {4} + 1} = \frac {\sqrt {z}}{3} - \frac {4}{3 \sqrt [ 4 ]{3}} \left[ \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {z \sqrt {3} + \sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}} + 1}{z \sqrt {3} - \sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}} + 1} + \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}}}{1 - z \sqrt {3}}\right) \right] ^ {*}) + C \\ = \frac {\sqrt {z}}{3} - \frac {1}{3 \sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2}} \left[ \ln \frac {z \sqrt {3} + \sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}} + 1}{z \sqrt {3} - \sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}} + 1} - 2 \arctan \left(\frac {\sqrt [ 4 ]{1 2 z ^ {2}}}{z \sqrt {3} - 1}\right) \right] + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \frac{1 + x}{1 - x}$

\*)利用1884题的结果.

【1973】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{1 - x} + \sqrt{1 + x}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{1 - x} + \sqrt{1 + x}} = \int \frac{-\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{1 - x} + \sqrt{1 + x}}{(\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{1 - x} + \sqrt{1 + x})(-\sqrt{2} + \sqrt{1 - x} + \sqrt{1 + x})}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {- \sqrt {2} + \sqrt {1 - x} + \sqrt {1 + x}}{2 \sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} d x = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {1 + x}} + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {1 - x}} \\ = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arcsin x + \sqrt {1 + x} - \sqrt {1 - x} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1974】 $\int \frac{x + \sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}{1 + x + \sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{x + \sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}{1 + x + \sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{(x + \sqrt{1 + x + x^2})(1 + x - \sqrt{1 + x + x^2})}{(1 + x)^2 - (1 + x + x^2)}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int \frac {\sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}} - 1}{x} d x = \int \frac {\sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{x} d x - \ln | x |.
$$

对于积分 $\int \frac{\sqrt{1 + x + x^2}}{x} \mathrm{d}x$ ，设 $x = \frac{1}{t}$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{t^2} \mathrm{d}t$ ， $\sqrt{1 + x + x^2} = \frac{\sqrt{t^2 + t + 1}}{|t|}$ 。

不妨设 $t > 0$ ，代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{x} d x = - \int \frac {\sqrt {t ^ {2} + t + 1}}{t ^ {2}} d t = \int \sqrt {t ^ {2} + t + 1} d \left(\frac {1}{t}\right) \\ = \frac {\sqrt {t ^ {2} + t + 1}}{t} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {2 t + 1}{t \sqrt {1 + t + t ^ {2}}} d t = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} - \int \frac {d t}{\sqrt {1 + t + t ^ {2}}} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d t}{t \sqrt {1 + t + t ^ {2}}} \\ = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} - \ln \left(t + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {1 + t + t ^ {2}}\right) + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(\frac {1}{t}\right)}{\sqrt {\left(\frac {1}{t}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {1}{t}\right) + 1}} \\ = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} - \ln \frac {2 + x + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{2 x} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left(\frac {1}{t} + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {\frac {1}{t ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{t} + 1}\right) + C _ {1} \\ = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} - \ln \frac {2 + x + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{2 x} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {2 x + 1 + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{2} + C _ {1} \\ = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {2 x + 1 + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{(2 + x + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}) ^ {2}} + \ln x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，当 $x > 0$ 时，最后得到

$$
\int \frac {x + \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{1 + x + \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}} d x = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + x + 1} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {2 x + 1 + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}}{(2 + x + 2 \sqrt {1 + x + x ^ {2}}) ^ {2}} + C.
$$

当 $x < 0$ 时，可获得同样的结果

【1975】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x(x + 1)}}{\sqrt{x} + \sqrt{x + 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x(x + 1)}}{\sqrt{x} + \sqrt{x + 1}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\sqrt{x(x + 1)}(\sqrt{x + 1} - \sqrt{x})}{(x + 1) - x}\mathrm{d}x = \int [(x + 1)\sqrt{x} - x\sqrt{x + 1}]\mathrm{d}x.$

$$
= \int \left[ x ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + x ^ {\frac {1}{2}} - (x + 1) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + (x + 1) ^ {\frac {1}{2}} \right] d x = \frac {2}{3} \left[ (x + 1) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + x ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \right] - \frac {2}{5} \left[ (x + 1) ^ {\frac {5}{2}} - x ^ {\frac {5}{2}} \right] + C.
$$

【1976】 $\int \frac{(x^2 - 1)\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 1)\sqrt{x^4 + 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{(x^2 - 1)\mathrm{d}x}{(x^2 + 1)\sqrt{x^4 + 1}} = \int \frac{\frac{x^2 - 1}{(x^2 + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\frac{x^4 + 1}{(x^2 + 1)^2}}} = \int \frac{\frac{x^2 - 1}{(x^2 + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - \left(\frac{x\sqrt{2}}{x^2 + 1}\right)^2}}.$

下面我们先考虑积分 $\int \frac{x^2 - 1}{(x^2 + 1)^2} \, \mathrm{d}x$ . 设 $x = \tan t, -\frac{\pi}{2} < t < \frac{\pi}{2}$ , 则有 $\mathrm{d}x = \sec^2 t \, \mathrm{d}t$ . 代入得

$$
\int \frac {x ^ {2} - 1}{(x ^ {2} + 1) ^ {2}} d x = \int \frac {\tan^ {2} t - 1}{\sec^ {4} t} \sec^ {2} t d t = \int (\sin^ {2} t - \cos^ {2} t) d t = - \int \cos 2 t d t = - \frac {1}{2} \sin 2 t + C _ {1} = - \frac {x}{1 + x ^ {2}} + C _ {1},
$$

从而，可得 $\frac{x^2 - 1}{(x^2 + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\mathrm{d}\left(\frac{x\sqrt{2}}{1 + x^2}\right)$ 于是，

$$
\int \frac {(x ^ {2} - 1) \mathrm {d} x}{(x ^ {2} + 1) \sqrt {x ^ {4} + 1}} = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{1 + x ^ {2}}\right)}{\sqrt {1 - \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{1 + x ^ {2}}\right) ^ {2}}} = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arcsin \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{1 + x ^ {2}}\right) + C.
$$

【1977】 $\int \frac{x^2 + 1}{(x^2 - 1)\sqrt{x^4 + 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解仿照1976题，可得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {x ^ {2} + 1}{(x ^ {2} - 1) \sqrt {x ^ {4} + 1}} d x = \int \frac {\frac {x ^ {2} + 1}{(x ^ {2} - 1) ^ {2}}}{\sqrt {\frac {x ^ {4} + 1}{(x ^ {2} - 1) ^ {2}}}} d x = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int \frac {d \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{x ^ {2} - 1}\right)}{\sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{x ^ {2} - 1}\right) ^ {2}}} \\ = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {x \sqrt {2}}{x ^ {2} - 1} + \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {x \sqrt {2}}{x ^ {2} - 1}\right) ^ {2}} \right| + C = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {x \sqrt {2} + \sqrt {x ^ {4} + 1}}{x ^ {2} - 1} \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1978】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{x^4 + 2x^2 - 1}}.$

提示 令 $\frac{1}{x} = \sqrt{t}$ （这里设 $x > 0$ 若 $x < 0$ ，则令 $\frac{1}{x} = -\sqrt{t}$ ，最后结果相同）.

解 作代换 $\frac{1}{x} = \sqrt{t}$ （这里设 $x > 0$ 。若 $x < 0$ ，则作变换 $\frac{1}{x} = -\sqrt{t}$ ，最后结果相同），则

$$
\mathrm {d} x = - \frac {1}{2 t \sqrt {t}} \mathrm {d} t, \quad \sqrt {x ^ {4} + 2 x ^ {2} - 1} = \frac {\sqrt {1 + 2 t - t ^ {2}}}{t}
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{x^4 + 2x^2 - 1}} = -\frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + 2t - t^2}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(1 - t)}{\sqrt{2 - (1 - t)^2}} = \frac{1}{2}\arcsin \left(\frac{1 - t}{\sqrt{2}}\right) + C$

$$
= \frac {1}{2} \arcsin \left(\frac {x ^ {2} - 1}{x ^ {2} \sqrt {2}}\right) + C \quad (| x | > \sqrt {\sqrt {2} - 1}).
$$

【1979】 $\int \frac{(x^2 + 1)\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{x^4 + x^2 + 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{(x^2 + 1)\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{x^4 + x^2 + 1}} = \int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x^4 + x^2 + 1}} +\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{x^4 + x^2 + 1}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(x ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2}\right)}{\sqrt {\left(x ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}}} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(\frac {1}{x ^ {2}}\right)}{\sqrt {\left(\frac {1}{x ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}}} = \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {x ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {x ^ {4} + x ^ {2} + 1}}{\frac {1}{x ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {4} + x ^ {2} + 1}{x ^ {4}}}} + C. \\ = \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {x ^ {2} (1 + 2 x ^ {2} + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {4} + x ^ {2} + 1})}{2 + x ^ {2} + 2 \sqrt {x ^ {4} + x ^ {2} + 1}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1980】 证明：积分

$$
\int R (x, \sqrt {a x + b}, \sqrt {c x + d}) \mathrm {d} x (R \text {为 有 理 函 数})
$$

的求法，归结为有理函数的积分法

证明思路 当 $a, c$ 中至少有一个为零时，则积分的求法显然可归结为有理函数的积分法。

当 $a \neq 0$ 及 $c \neq 0$ 时，设 $\sqrt{ax + b} = z$ ，则 $\sqrt{cx + d} = \sqrt{c_1z^2 + d_1}$ ，其中 $c_1 = \frac{c}{a}$ ， $d_1 = d - \frac{bc}{a}$ 。从而，原积分变形为

$$
\int R \left(\frac {z ^ {2} - b}{a}, z, \sqrt {c _ {1} z ^ {2} + d _ {1}}\right) \frac {2}{a} z \mathrm {d} z = \int R _ {1} (z, \sqrt {c _ {1} z ^ {2} + d _ {1}}) \mathrm {d} z,
$$

其中 $R_{1}$ 为有理函数.

若 $c_{1} > 0$ ，设 $\sqrt{c_{1}z^{2} + d_{1}} = \pm \sqrt{c_{1}} z + u$ ；若 $d_{1} > 0$ ，设 $\sqrt{c_{1}z^{2} + d_{1}} = zu\pm \sqrt{d_{1}}$ ，即可将被积函数有理化从而命题获证.

证 当 $a, c$ 中至少有一个为零时，则积分

$$
\int R (x, \sqrt {a x + b}, \sqrt {c x + d}) \mathrm {d} x
$$

的求法显然可归结为有理函数的积分法

当 $a \neq 0, c \neq 0$ 时，设 $\sqrt{ax + b} = z$ ，则

$$
x = \frac {z ^ {2} - b}{a}, \quad \mathrm {d} x = \frac {2}{a} z \mathrm {d} z, \sqrt {c x + d} = \sqrt {\frac {c}{a} z ^ {2} + d - \frac {b c}{a}} = \sqrt {c _ {1} z ^ {2} + d _ {1}},
$$

式中 $c_{1} = \frac{c}{a}$ ， $d_{1} = d - \frac{bc}{a}$ 代人得

$$
\int R (x, \sqrt {a x + b}, \sqrt {c x + d}) \mathrm {d} x = \int R \left(\frac {z ^ {2} - b}{a}, z, \sqrt {c _ {1} z ^ {2} + d _ {1}}\right) \frac {2}{a} z \mathrm {d} z = \int R _ {1} \left(z, \sqrt {c _ {1} z ^ {2} + d _ {1}}\right) \mathrm {d} z,
$$

其中 $R_{1}$ 为有理函数.

再设 $\sqrt{c_1z^2 + d_1} = \pm \sqrt{c_1} z + u (c_1 > 0)$ 或 $\sqrt{c_1z^2 + d_1} = zu \pm \sqrt{d_1} (d_1 > 0)$ ——欧拉代换，就可将被积函数有理化.于是，积分

$$
\int R (x, \sqrt {a x + b}, \sqrt {c x + b}) d x
$$

的求法可归结为有理函数的积分法.

二项微分式的积分

$$
\int x ^ {m} (a + b x ^ {n}) ^ {p} \mathrm {d} x, \quad (\text {式 中} m, n \text {和} p \text {为 有 理 数})
$$

仅在下列三种情形可化为有理函数的积分（切比雪夫定理）：

第一种情形， $p$ 为整数.此时令 $x = z^{N}$ ，其中 $N$ 为分数 $m$ 和 $_n$ 的公分母

第二种情形， $\frac{m + 1}{n}$ 为整数.此时令 $a + bx^{n} = z^{N}$ ，其中 $N$ 为分数 $\pmb{\varPhi}$ 的分母

第三种情形， $\frac{m + 1}{n} + p$ 为整数.此时利用代换： $ax^{-n} + b = z^{N}$ ，其中 $N$ 为分数 $p$ 的分母

若 $n = 1$ ，则这些情形等价于：（1） $\pmb{p}$ 为整数.（2） $m$ 为整数.（3） $m + p$ 为整数

计算下列积分：

【1981】 $\int \sqrt{x^3 + x^4}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $x^{-1} + 1 = z^2$

解 $\sqrt{x^3 + x^4} = x^{\frac{3}{2}}(1 + x)^{\frac{1}{2}}$ ， $m = \frac{3}{2}$ ， $n = 1$ ， $p = \frac{1}{2}$ ； $\frac{m + 1}{n} + p = 3$ ，这是二项微分式的第三种情形.

设 $x^{-1} + 1 = z^2$ ，则 $x = \frac{1}{z^2 - 1},\quad \mathrm{d}x = -\frac{2z}{(z^2 - 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z,\quad \sqrt{x^3 + x^4} = \frac{z}{(z^2 - 1)^2}$

（不妨设 $z > 0$ ，以下各题不再说明）.代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \sqrt {x ^ {3} + x ^ {4}} d x = - 2 \int \frac {z ^ {2}}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {4}} d z = - 2 \int \frac {d z}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {4}} - 2 \int \frac {d z}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} \\ = - 2 \left[ - \frac {z}{6 (z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} - \frac {5}{6} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} z}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} \right] ^ {*}) - 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} z}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} = \frac {z}{3 (z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} - \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} z}{(z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} \\ = \frac {z}{3 (z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {3}} + \frac {z}{1 2 (z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {2}} - \frac {z}{8 (z ^ {2} - 1)} + \frac {1}{1 6} \ln \frac {z + 1}{z - 1} + C \\ = \frac {1}{3} \sqrt {(x + x ^ {2}) ^ {3}} - \frac {1 + 2 x}{8} \sqrt {x + x ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{8} \ln (\sqrt {x} + \sqrt {1 + x}) + C (x > 0). \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1921题的结果.

【1982】 $\int \frac{\sqrt{x}}{(1 + \sqrt[3]{x})^2}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $x = z^6$

解 $\frac{\sqrt{x}}{(1 + \sqrt[3]{x})^2} = x^{\frac{1}{2}}(1 + x^{\frac{1}{3}})^{-2}$ . $m = \frac{1}{2}, n = \frac{1}{3}, p = -2$ ; $p$ 为整数, 这是二项微分式的第一种情形.

设 $x = z^6$ ，则 $\mathrm{d}x = 6z^{5}\mathrm{d}z,\sqrt{x} = z^{3},\sqrt[3]{x} = z^{2}$ .代人得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sqrt {x}}{(1 + \sqrt [ 3 ]{x}) ^ {2}} d x = 6 \int \frac {z ^ {8}}{(z ^ {2} + 1) ^ {2}} d z = 6 \int \left[ z ^ {4} - 2 z ^ {2} + 3 - \frac {4}{z ^ {2} + 1} + \frac {1}{(z ^ {2} + 1) ^ {2}} \right] d z \\ = \frac {6}{5} z ^ {5} - 4 z ^ {3} + 1 8 z - 2 4 \arctan z + 6 \left[ \frac {z}{2 \left(z ^ {2} + 1\right)} + \frac {1}{2} \arctan z \right] ^ {*} + C \\ = \frac {6}{5} x ^ {\frac {5}{6}} - 4 x ^ {\frac {1}{2}} + 1 8 x ^ {\frac {1}{6}} + \frac {3 x ^ {\frac {1}{6}}}{1 + x ^ {\frac {1}{3}}} - 2 1 \arctan \left(x ^ {\frac {1}{6}}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1921题的结果.

【1983】 $\int \frac{x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \sqrt[3]{x^2}}}$

提示 令 $1 + x^{\frac{2}{3}} = z^{2}$

解 $\frac{x}{\sqrt{1 + \sqrt[3]{x^2}}} = x(1 + x^{\frac{2}{3}})^{-\frac{1}{2}}$ $m = 1$ ， $n = \frac{2}{3}$ ， $p = -\frac{1}{2}$ ； $\frac{m + 1}{n} = 3$ ，这是二项微分式的第二种情形.

设 $1 + x^{\frac{2}{3}} = z^{2}$ ，则 $x = (z^{2} - 1)^{\frac{3}{2}},\mathrm{d}x = 3z(z^{2} - 1)^{\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{d}z.$ 代人得

$$
\int \frac {x \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {1 + \sqrt [ 3 ]{x ^ {2}}}} = 3 \int (z ^ {2} - 1) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z = \frac {3}{5} z ^ {5} - 2 z ^ {3} + 3 z + C,
$$

其中 $z = \sqrt{1 + \sqrt[3]{x^2}}$

【1984】 $\int \frac{x^5\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - x^2}}.$

解 $\frac{x^5}{\sqrt{1 - x^2}} = x^5 (1 - x^2)^{-\frac{1}{2}}$ ， $m = 5$ ， $n = 2$ ， $p = -\frac{1}{2}$ ； $\frac{m + 1}{n} = 3$ ，这是二项微分式的第二种情形.

设 $\sqrt{1 - x^2} = z$ （不妨设 $x > 0$ ），则 $x = \sqrt{1 - z^2}$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = -\frac{z}{\sqrt{1 - z^2}}\mathrm{dz}$ 。代入得

$$
\int \frac {x ^ {5} \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} = - \int (1 - z ^ {2}) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z = - z + \frac {2}{3} z ^ {3} - \frac {1}{5} z ^ {5} + C,
$$

其中 $z = \sqrt{1 - x^2}$

【1985】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{1 + x^3}}.$

提示 令 $x^{-3} + 1 = z^3$

解 $\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{1 + x^3}} = x^0 (1 + x^3)^{-\frac{1}{3}}, m = 0, n = 3, p = -\frac{1}{3}; \frac{m + 1}{n} + p = 0$ 这是二项微分式的第三种情形.

设 $x^{-3} + 1 = z^3$ ，则 $x = (z^{3} - 1)^{-\frac{1}{3}}$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = -z^2 (z^3 -1)^{-\frac{4}{3}}\mathrm{dz}$ 代人得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 3 ]{1 + x ^ {3}}} = - \int \frac {z}{z ^ {3} - 1} \mathrm {d} z = - \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} z}{z - 1} + \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {z - 1}{z ^ {2} + z + 1} \mathrm {d} z \\ = - \frac {1}{3} \ln | z - 1 | + \frac {1}{6} \ln (z ^ {2} + z + 1) - \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 z + 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + C \\ = \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {z ^ {2} + z + 1}{(z - 1) ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 z + 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \frac{\sqrt[3]{1 + x^3}}{x}$

【1986】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[4]{1 + x^4}}.$

解 $\frac{1}{\sqrt[4]{1 + x^4}} = x^0 (1 + x^4)^{-\frac{1}{4}}, m = 0, n = 4, p = -\frac{1}{4}; \frac{m + 1}{n} + p = 0$ 这是二项微分式的第三种情形.

设 $x^{-4} + 1 = z^4$ ，则 $z = \frac{\sqrt[4]{1 + x^4}}{x}$ （ $z > 0, x > 0$ ）， $x = (z^4 - 1)^{-\frac{1}{4}}$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = -z^3 (z^4 - 1)^{-\frac{5}{4}} \mathrm{d}z.$ 代入得

$$
\int \frac {d x}{\sqrt [ 4 ]{1 + x ^ {4}}} = - \int \frac {z ^ {2}}{z ^ {4} - 1} d z = \int \left[ \frac {1}{4 (z + 1)} - \frac {1}{4 (z - 1)} - \frac {1}{2 (z ^ {2} + 1)} \right] d z = \frac {1}{4} \ln \left| \frac {z + 1}{z - 1} \right| - \frac {1}{2} \arctan z + C,
$$

其中 $z = \frac{\sqrt[4]{1 + x^4}}{x}$

【1987】+ $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt[6]{1 + x^6}}.$

解 $\frac{1}{x\sqrt[6]{1 + x^6}} = x^{-1}(1 + x^6)^{-\frac{1}{6}}$ ， $m = -1, n = 6, p = -\frac{1}{6}$ ； $\frac{m + 1}{n} = 0$ ，这是二项微分式的第二种情形.

设 $1 + x^{6} = z^{6}$ ，则 $z = \sqrt[6]{1 + x^6}$ （ $z > 0, x > 0$ ）， $x = \sqrt[6]{z^6 - 1}$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = z^5 (z^6 - 1)^{-\frac{5}{6}} \mathrm{d}z.$ 代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{x \sqrt [ 6 ]{1 + x ^ {6}}} = \int \frac {z ^ {4} \mathrm {d} z}{z ^ {6} - 1} = \int \left[ - \frac {1}{6 (z + 1)} + \frac {z + 1}{6 (z ^ {2} - z + 1)} + \frac {1}{6 (z - 1)} + \frac {- z + 1}{6 (z ^ {2} + z + 1)} \right] \mathrm {d} z \\ = \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {z - 1}{z + 1} + \frac {1}{1 2} \ln \frac {z ^ {2} - z + 1}{z ^ {2} + z + 1} + \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {3}} \left[ \arctan \left(\frac {2 z - 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + \arctan \left(\frac {2 z + 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) \right] + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {z - 1}{z + 1} + \frac {1}{1 2} \ln \frac {z ^ {2} - z + 1}{z ^ {2} + z + 1} + \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {z ^ {2} - 1}{z \sqrt {3}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \sqrt[6]{1 + x^6}$

【1988】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^3\sqrt[5]{1 + \frac{1}{x}}}$

解 $\frac{1}{x^3\sqrt[5]{1 + \frac{1}{x}}} = x^{-3}(1 + x^{-1})^{-\frac{1}{5}}$ . $m = -3, n = -1, p = -\frac{1}{5}; \frac{m + 1}{n} = 2$ 这是二项微分式的第二种

情形. 设 $1 + x^{-1} = z^5$ ，则 $x = (z^5 - 1)^{-1}$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = -5z^4 (z^5 - 1)^{-2} \, \mathrm{d}z$ 。代入得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{x ^ {3} \sqrt [ 5 ]{1 + \frac {1}{x}}} = - 5 \int z ^ {3} (z ^ {5} - 1) \mathrm {d} z = - \frac {5}{9} z ^ {9} + \frac {5}{4} z ^ {4} + C,
$$

其中 $z = \sqrt[5]{1 + \frac{1}{x}}.$

【1989】 $\int \sqrt[3]{3x - x^3}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\sqrt[3]{3x - x^3} = x^{\frac{1}{3}}(3 - x^2)^{\frac{1}{3}}$ $m = \frac{1}{3},n = 2,p = \frac{1}{3};\frac{m + 1}{n} +p = 1$ ，这是二项微分式的第三种情形.

设 $3x^{-2} - 1 = z^3$ （不妨设 $x > 0$ ），则

$$
z = \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 x - x ^ {3}}}{x}, \quad x = \frac {\sqrt {3}}{\sqrt {z ^ {3} + 1}}, \quad d x = - \frac {3 \sqrt {3}}{2} \cdot \frac {z ^ {2}}{(z ^ {3} + 1) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} d z.
$$

代入得 $\int \sqrt[3]{3x - x^3}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{9}{2}\int \frac{z^3}{(z^3 + 1)^2}\mathrm{d}z = -\frac{9}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{z^3 + 1} +\frac{9}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{(z^3 + 1)^2}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {9}{2} \left[ \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {(z + 1) ^ {2}}{z ^ {2} - z + 1} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 z - 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) \right] ^ {*}) + \frac {9}{2} \left[ \frac {z}{3 (z ^ {3} + 1)} + \frac {1}{9} \ln \frac {(z + 1) ^ {2}}{z ^ {2} - z + 1} \right. \\ + \frac {2}{3 \sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 z - 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) \bigg ] ^ {* *}) + C = \frac {3 z}{2 (z ^ {3} + 1)} - \frac {1}{4} \ln \frac {(z + 1) ^ {2}}{z ^ {2} - z + 1} - \frac {\sqrt {3}}{2} \arctan \left(\frac {2 z - 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $z = \frac{\sqrt[3]{3x - x^3}}{x}$

\*) 利用1881题的结果.

\*\*）利用1892题的结果.

【1990】在什么情形下，积分 $\int \sqrt{1 + x^m}\mathrm{d}x$ （ $m$ 为有理数)为初等函数？

解 $\sqrt{1 + x^m} = x^0 (1 + x^m)^{\frac{1}{2}}$ 由于 $p = \frac{1}{2}$ 故由切比雪夫定理知，仅在下述两种情形，此函数的积分可化为有理函数的积分.

第一种情形， $\frac{1}{m}$ 为整数，即 $m = \frac{1}{k_1} = \frac{2}{2k_1}$ 其中 $k_{1} = \pm 1,\pm 2,\dots$

第二种情形， $\frac{1}{m} +\frac{1}{2}$ 为整数，即 $m = \frac{2}{2k_2 - 1}$ ，其中 $k_{2} = 0,\pm 1,\pm 2,\dots$

综上所述，即得：当 $m = \frac{2}{k}$ （式中 $k = \pm 1, \pm 2, \dots$ ）时，积分 $\int \sqrt{1 + x^m} \mathrm{d}x$ 为初等函数.

# §4. 三角函数的积分法

形如

$$
\int \sin^ {m} x \cos^ {n} x \mathrm {d} x \quad (m   \text {及}   n   \text {为 整 数})
$$

的积分，可利用巧妙的变换或运用递推公式计算。

求下列积分：

【1991】 $\int \cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \cos^4 x\cos x\mathrm{d}x = \int (1 - \sin^2 x)^2\mathrm{d}(\sin x)$

$$
= \int (1 - 2 \sin^ {2} x + \sin^ {4} x) d (\sin x) = \sin x - \frac {2}{3} \sin^ {3} x + \frac {1}{5} \sin^ {5} x + C.
$$

【1992】 $\int \sin^6 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin^6 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \left(\frac{1 - \cos 2x}{2}\right)^3\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{8}\int (1 - 3\cos 2x + 3\cos^2 2x - \cos^3 2x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {x}{8} - \frac {3}{1 6} \sin 2 x + \frac {3}{8} \int \frac {1 + \cos 4 x}{2} d x - \frac {1}{8} \int (1 - \sin^ {2} 2 x) \cos 2 x d x \\ = \frac {x}{8} - \frac {3}{1 6} \sin 2 x + \frac {3 x}{1 6} + \frac {3}{6 4} \sin 4 x - \frac {1}{1 6} \int (1 - \sin^ {2} 2 x) d (\sin 2 x) \\ = \frac {5 x}{1 6} - \frac {3}{1 6} \sin 2 x + \frac {3}{6 4} \sin 4 x - \frac {1}{1 6} \sin 2 x + \frac {1}{4 8} \sin^ {3} 2 x + C \\ = \frac {5 x}{1 6} - \frac {1}{4} \sin 2 x + \frac {3}{6 4} \sin 4 x + \frac {1}{4 8} \sin^ {3} 2 x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【1993】 $\int \cos^6 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \cos^6 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \sin^6\left(x - \frac{\pi}{2}\right)\mathrm{d}\left(x - \frac{\pi}{2}\right)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {5}{1 6} \left(x - \frac {\pi}{2}\right) - \frac {1}{4} \sin 2 \left(x - \frac {\pi}{2}\right) + \frac {3}{6 4} \sin 4 \left(x - \frac {\pi}{2}\right) + \frac {1}{4 8} \sin^ {3} 2 \left(x - \frac {\pi}{2}\right) ^ {*}) + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {5 x}{1 6} + \frac {1}{4} \sin 2 x + \frac {3}{6 4} \sin 4 x - \frac {1}{4 8} \sin^ {3} 2 x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1992题的结果.

【1994】 $\int \sin^2 x\cos^4 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin^2 x\cos^4 x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int \sin^2 2x\cos^2 x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{8}\int \sin^2 2x(1 + \cos 2x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{8} \int \frac {1 - \cos 4 x}{2} d x + \frac {1}{1 6} \int \sin^ {2} 2 x d (\sin 2 x) = \frac {x}{1 6} - \frac {1}{6 4} \sin 4 x + \frac {1}{4 8} \sin^ {3} 2 x + C.
$$

【1995】 $\int \sin^4 x\cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin^4 x\cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \sin^4 x(1 - \sin^2 x)^2\mathrm{d}(\sin x) = \frac{1}{5}\sin^5 x - \frac{2}{7}\sin^7 x + \frac{1}{9}\sin^9 x + C.$

【1996】 $\int \sin^5 x\cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin^5 x\cos^5 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{1}{32}\sin^5 2x\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{64}\int (1 - \cos^2 2x)^2\mathrm{d}(\cos 2x)$

$$
= - \frac {1}{6 4} \cos 2 x + \frac {1}{9 6} \cos^ {3} 2 x - \frac {1}{3 2 0} \cos^ {5} 2 x + C.
$$

【1997】 $\int \frac{\sin^3x}{\cos^4x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^3 x}{\cos^4 x} \mathrm{d}x = -\int \frac{1 - \cos^2 x}{\cos^4 x} \mathrm{d}(\cos x) = \frac{1}{3 \cos^3 x} - \frac{1}{\cos x} + C.$

【1998】 $\int \frac{\cos^4x}{\sin^3x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\cos^4 x}{\sin^3 x} \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\cos^3 x}{\sin^3 x} \mathrm{d}(\sin x) = -\frac{1}{2} \int \cos^3 x \mathrm{d}\left(\frac{1}{\sin^2 x}\right)$

$$
= - \frac {\cos^ {3} x}{2 \sin^ {2} x} - \frac {3}{2} \int \frac {\cos^ {2} x \sin x}{\sin^ {2} x} d x = - \frac {\cos^ {3} x}{2 \sin^ {2} x} - \frac {3}{2} \int \frac {1 - \sin^ {2} x}{\sin x} d x
$$

$$
= - \frac {\cos^ {3} x}{2 \sin^ {2} x} - \frac {3}{2} \ln \left| \tan \frac {x}{2} \right| - \frac {3}{2} \cos x + C
$$

【1999】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x}$
