解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x} = -\int \frac{1}{\sin x} \mathrm{d}(\cot x) = -\frac{\cot x}{\sin x} - \int \cot x \frac{\cos x}{\sin^2 x} \mathrm{d}x = -\frac{\cos x}{\sin^2 x} - \int \frac{1 - \sin^2 x}{\sin^3 x} \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= - \frac {\cos x}{\sin^ {2} x} - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin^ {3} x} + \ln \left| \tan \frac {x}{2} \right|,
$$

于是， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x} = -\frac{\cos x}{2 \sin^2 x} + \frac{1}{2} \ln \left| \tan \frac{x}{2} \right| + C.$

【2000】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos^3 x}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos^3 x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right)}{\sin^3\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right)} = -\frac{\cos\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right)}{2\sin^2\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right)} + \frac{1}{2}\ln \left|\tan \left(\frac{x + \frac{\pi}{2}}{2}\right)\right|^*) + C$

$$
= \frac {\sin x}{2 \cos^ {2} x} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\pi}{4}\right) \right| + C.
$$

\*）利用1999题的结果.

【2001】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 x \cos^4 x}$ .

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 x \cos^4 x} = 16 \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 2x} = -8 \int \csc^2 2x \, \mathrm{d}(\cot 2x)$

$$
= - 8 \int (1 + \cot^ {2} 2 x) d (\cot 2 x) = - 8 \cot 2 x - \frac {8}{3} \cot^ {3} 2 x + C.
$$

【2002】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x}$ .

提示：多次利用等式 $1 = \sin^2 x + \cos^2 x$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x} = \int \frac{\sin^2 x + \cos^2 x}{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x} \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x \cos^5 x} + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3 x \cos^3 x}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\sin^ {2} x + \cos^ {2} x}{\sin x \cos^ {5} x} d x + \int \frac {\sin^ {2} x + \cos^ {2} x}{\sin^ {3} x \cos^ {3} x} d x = \int \frac {\sin x}{\cos^ {5} x} d x + 2 \int \frac {d x}{\sin x \cos^ {3} x} + \int \frac {d x}{\sin^ {3} x \cos x} \\ = - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cos x)}{\cos^ {5} x} + 2 \int \frac {\sin x}{\cos^ {3} x} \mathrm {d} x + 3 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin x \cos x} + \int \frac {\cos x}{\sin^ {3} x} \mathrm {d} x \\ = \frac {1}{4 \cos^ {4} x} - 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cos x)}{\cos^ {3} x} + 3 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\tan x)}{\tan x} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\sin x)}{\sin^ {3} x} = \frac {1}{4 \cos^ {4} x} + \frac {1}{\cos^ {2} x} + 3 \ln | \tan x | - \frac {1}{2 \sin^ {2} x} + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {1}{4} \tan^ {4} x + \frac {3}{2} \tan^ {2} x - \frac {1}{2} \cot^ {2} x + 3 \ln | \tan x | + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2003】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x\cos^4x}$

提示：与2002题相同.

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x\cos^4x} = \int \frac{\sin^2x + \cos^2x}{\sin x\cos^4x}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\sin x}{\cos^4x}\mathrm{d}x + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x\cos^2x}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cos x)}{\cos^ {4} x} + \int \frac {\sin x}{\cos^ {2} x} \mathrm {d} x + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin x} = \frac {1}{3 \cos^ {3} x} - \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cos x)}{\cos^ {2} x} + \ln \left| \tan \frac {x}{2} \right| \\ = \frac {1}{3 \cos^ {3} x} + \frac {1}{\cos x} + \ln \left| \tan \frac {x}{2} \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2004】 $\int \tan^5 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \tan^5 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \tan x(\sec^2 x - 1)^2\mathrm{d}x = \int \sec^4 x\tan x\mathrm{d}x - 2\int \sec^2 x\tan x\mathrm{d}x + \int \tan x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \sec^ {3} x d (\sec x) - 2 \int \sec x d (\sec x) - \int \frac {d (\cos x)}{\cos x} = \frac {1}{4} \sec^ {4} x - \sec^ {2} x - \ln | \cos x | + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {1}{4} \tan^ {4} x - \frac {1}{2} \tan^ {2} x - \ln | \cos x | + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2005】 $\int \cot^6 x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \cot^6 x\mathrm{d}x = \int \cot^2 x(\csc^2 x - 1)^2\mathrm{d}x = \int \cot^2 x\csc^4 x\mathrm{d}x - 2\int \cot^2 x\csc^2 x\mathrm{d}x + \int \cot^2 x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \int \cot^ {2} x (1 + \cot^ {2} x) d (\cot x) + 2 \int \cot^ {2} x d (\cot x) + \int (\csc^ {2} x - 1) d x \\ = - \frac {1}{3} \cot^ {3} x - \frac {1}{5} \cot^ {5} x + \frac {2}{3} \cot^ {3} x - \cot x - x + C = - \frac {1}{5} \cot^ {5} x + \frac {1}{3} \cot^ {3} x - \cot x - x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2006】 $\int \frac{\sin^4 x}{\cos^6 x} \mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^4 x}{\cos^6 x} \mathrm{d}x = \int \tan^4 x \mathrm{d}(\tan x) = \frac{1}{5} \tan^5 x + C.$

【2007】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x}} = \int \frac{\sin^2 x \mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x}} + \int \frac{\cos^2 x \mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\sin^3 x \cos^5 x}} = \int \sqrt{\tan x} \mathrm{d}(\tan x) - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\cot x)}{\sqrt{\cot x}}$

$$
= \frac {2}{3} \sqrt {\tan^ {3} x} - 2 \sqrt {\cot x} + C.
$$

【2008】+ $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x\sqrt[3]{\sin^2x}}.$

解设 $t = \sqrt[3]{\sin x}$ ，不妨只考虑 $\cos x$ 为正的情况，即 $-\frac{\pi}{2} < x < \frac{\pi}{2}$ 且 $x \neq 0$ ，则有

$$
\mathrm {d} x = \frac {3 t ^ {2}}{\sqrt {1 - t ^ {6}}} \mathrm {d} t, \quad \cos x = \sqrt {1 - t ^ {6}}.
$$

代人得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x\sqrt[3]{\sin^2x}} = 3\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 - t^6} = \frac{3}{2}\int \left(\frac{1}{1 - t^3} +\frac{1}{1 + t^3}\right)\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}\int \left(\frac{1}{1 - t} +\frac{t + 2}{1 + t + t^2}\right)\mathrm{d}t + \frac{3}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + t^3}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{2} \ln | 1 - t | + \frac {1}{4} \int \frac {2 t + 1}{t ^ {2} + t + 1} d t + \frac {3}{4} \int \frac {d (t + \frac {1}{2})}{(t + \frac {1}{2}) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}} + \frac {3}{2} \left[ \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {(t + 1) ^ {2}}{t ^ {2} - t + 1} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \frac {2 t - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] ^ {*}) + C \\ = \frac {1}{4} \ln \frac {(t + 1) ^ {2} (t ^ {2} + t + 1)}{(1 - t) ^ {2} (t ^ {2} - t + 1)} + \frac {\sqrt {3}}{2} \left[ \arctan \left(\frac {2 t + 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + \arctan \left(\frac {2 t - 1}{\sqrt {3}}\right) \right] + C \\ = \frac {1}{4} \ln \frac {(1 + t) ^ {3} (1 - t ^ {3})}{(1 - t) ^ {3} (1 + t ^ {3})} + \frac {\sqrt {3}}{2} \arctan \left(\frac {t \sqrt {3}}{1 - t ^ {2}}\right) + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt[3]{\sin x}$

\*) 利用1881题的结果.

【2009】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\tan x}}.$

解设 $t = \sqrt{\tan x}$ ，则 $x = \arctan t^2$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = \frac{2t}{1 + t^4}\mathrm{dt}$ 代人得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {\tan x}} = 2 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{1 + t ^ {4}} = 2 \left(\frac {1}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} + \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \frac {t \sqrt {2}}{1 - t ^ {2}}\right) ^ {*}) + C \\ = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {t ^ {2} + t \sqrt {2} + 1}{t ^ {2} - t \sqrt {2} + 1} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan \frac {t \sqrt {2}}{1 - t ^ {2}} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt{\tan x}$

\*) 利用1884题的结果.

【2010】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{\tan x}}.$

解设 $\sqrt[3]{\tan x} = t$ ，则 $x = \arctan t^3$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = \frac{3t^2}{1 + t^6}\mathrm{dt}$ 代人得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt [ 3 ]{\tan x}} = 3 \int \frac {t \mathrm {d} t}{1 + t ^ {6}} = \frac {3}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(t ^ {2}\right)}{1 + \left(t ^ {2}\right) ^ {3}} = \frac {3}{2} \left[ \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {\left(t ^ {2} + 1\right) ^ {2}}{t ^ {4} - t ^ {2} + 1} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \frac {2 t ^ {2} - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] ^ {*}) + C \\ = \frac {1}{4} \ln \frac {(t ^ {2} + 1) ^ {2}}{t ^ {4} - t ^ {2} + 1} + \frac {\sqrt {3}}{2} \arctan \frac {2 t ^ {2} - 1}{\sqrt {3}} + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $t = \sqrt[3]{\tan x}$

\*) 利用1881题的结果.

【2011】推出下列积分的递推公式

(1) $I_{n} = \int \sin^{n}x\mathrm{d}x;$ (2） $K_{n} = \int \cos^{n}x\mathrm{d}x\quad (n > 2).$

利用这些公式计算 $\int \sin^6 x\mathrm{d}x$ 和 $\int \cos^8 x\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 利用分部积分法，易得：

(1) $I_{n} = -\frac{\cos x \sin^{n-1} x}{n} + \frac{n-1}{n} I_{n-2}$ ;

(2) $K_{n} = \frac{\sin x\cos^{n - 1}x}{n} +\frac{n - 1}{n} K_{n - 2}$

解（1） $I_{n} = \int \sin^{n}x\mathrm{d}x = -\int \sin^{n - 1}x\mathrm{d}(\cos x) = -\cos x\sin^{n - 1}x + (n - 1)\int \cos^{2}x\sin^{n - 2}x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= - \cos x \sin^ {n - 1} x + (n - 1) \int (1 - \sin^ {2} x) \sin^ {n - 2} x d x = - \cos x \sin^ {n - 1} x + (n - 1) I _ {n - 2} + (1 - n) I _ {n},
$$

于是， $I_{n} = -\frac{\cos x \sin^{n-1} x}{n} + \frac{n-1}{n} I_{n-2}$ ;

利用此公式及 $I_0 = \int \mathrm{d}x = x + C$ ，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {6} = \int \sin^ {6} x \mathrm {d} x = - \frac {\cos x \sin^ {5} x}{6} + \frac {5}{6} I _ {4} = - \frac {\cos x \sin^ {5} x}{6} - \frac {5 \cos x \sin^ {3} x}{2 4} + \frac {5}{8} I _ {2} \\ = - \frac {\cos x \sin^ {5} x}{6} - \frac {5 \cos x \sin^ {3} x}{2 4} - \frac {5 \cos x \sin x}{1 6} + \frac {5}{1 6} x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

(2) $K_{n} = \int \cos^{n}x\mathrm{d}x = \int \cos^{n - 1}x\mathrm{d}(\sin x)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \sin x \cos^ {n - 1} x + (n - 1) \int \sin^ {2} x \cos^ {n - 2} x d x = \sin x \cos^ {n - 1} x + (n - 1) \int (1 - \cos^ {2} x) \cos^ {n - 2} x d x \\ = \sin x \cos^ {n - 1} x + (n - 1) K _ {n - 2} - (n - 1) K _ {n}, \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $K_{n} = \frac{\sin x\cos^{n - 1}x}{n} +\frac{n - 1}{n} K_{n - 2};$

利用此公式及 $K_{0} = x + C$ ，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} K _ {8} = \int \cos^ {8} x d x = \frac {1}{8} \sin x \cos^ {7} x + \frac {7}{8} K _ {6} = \dots \\ = \frac {1}{8} \sin x \cos^ {7} x + \frac {7}{4 8} \sin x \cos^ {5} x + \frac {3 5}{1 9 2} \sin x \cos^ {3} x + \frac {3 5}{1 2 8} \sin x \cos x + \frac {3 5}{1 2 8} x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2012】推出下列积分的递推公式：

(1) $I_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^{n}x}; \quad (2) K_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos^{n}x} \quad (n > 2).$

利用这些公式计算 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^5 x}$ 和 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos^7 x}$ .

提示 利用分部积分法及 $1 = \sin^2 x + \cos^2 x$ ，易得

(1) $I_{n} = -\frac{\cos x}{(n - 1)\sin^{n - 1}x} + \frac{n - 2}{n - 1} I_{n - 2}$ ; (2) $K_{n} = \frac{\sin x}{(n - 1)\cos^{n - 1}x} + \frac{n - 2}{n - 1} K_{n - 2}$ .

解 (1) $I_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^{n}x} = \int \frac{\sin^{2}x + \cos^{2}x}{\sin^{n}x}\mathrm{d}x = I_{n - 2} - \frac{1}{n - 1}\int \cos x\mathrm{d}\left(\frac{1}{\sin^{n - 1}x}\right)$

$$
= I _ {n - 2} - \frac {\cos x}{(n - 1) \sin^ {n - 1} x} - \frac {1}{n - 1} I _ {n - 2} = - \frac {\cos x}{(n - 1) \sin^ {n - 1} x} + \frac {n - 2}{n - 1} I _ {n - 2};
$$

利用此公式及 $I_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x} = \ln \left|\tan \frac{x}{2}\right| + C$ ，即得

$$
I _ {5} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin^ {5} x} = - \frac {\cos x}{4 \sin^ {4} x} + \frac {3}{4} I _ {3} = \dots = - \frac {\cos x}{4 \sin^ {4} x} - \frac {3 \cos x}{8 \sin^ {2} x} + \frac {3}{8} \ln | \tan \frac {x}{2} | + C.
$$

(2) $K_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos^{n}x} = \int \frac{\sin^{2}x + \cos^{2}x}{\cos^{n}x}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{n - 1}\int \sin x\mathrm{d}\left(\frac{1}{\cos^{n - 1}x}\right) + K_{n - 2}$

$$
= \frac {\sin x}{(n - 1) \cos^ {n - 1} x} - \frac {1}{n - 1} K _ {n - 2} + K _ {n - 2} = \frac {\sin x}{(n - 1) \cos^ {n - 1} x} + \frac {n - 2}{n - 1} K _ {n - 2};
$$

利用此公式及 $K_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x} = \ln \left|\tan \left(\frac{x}{2} + \frac{\pi}{4}\right)\right| + C$ ，即得

$$
K _ {7} = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\cos^ {7} x} = \frac {\sin x}{6 \cos^ {6} x} + \frac {5}{6} K _ {5} = \dots = \frac {\sin x}{6 \cos^ {6} x} + \frac {5 \sin x}{2 4 \cos^ {4} x} + \frac {5 \sin x}{1 6 \cos^ {2} x} + \frac {5}{1 6} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\pi}{4}\right) \right| + C.
$$

为了计算下面的积分，可以运用公式

I. $\sin \alpha \sin \beta = \frac{1}{2} [\cos (\alpha -\beta) - \cos (\alpha +\beta)]$   
I $\cos \alpha \cos \beta = \frac{1}{2} [\cos (\alpha +\beta) + \cos (\alpha -\beta)]$   
Ⅲ. $\sin \alpha \cos \beta = \frac{1}{2} [\sin (\alpha -\beta) + \sin (\alpha +\beta)]$

求积分：

【2013】 $\int \sin 5x\cos x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin 5x\cos x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int [\sin 4x + \sin 6x]\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{8}\cos 4x - \frac{1}{12}\cos 6x + C.$

【2014】 $\int \cos x\cos 2x\cos 3x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \cos x\cos 2x\cos 3x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \cos 2x(\cos 4x + \cos 2x)\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int (\cos 6x + \cos 2x)\mathrm{d}x + \frac{1}{4}\int (1 + \cos 4x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{2 4} \sin 6 x + \frac {1}{8} \sin 2 x + \frac {1}{1 6} \sin 4 x + \frac {x}{4} + C.
$$

【2015】 $\int \sin x\sin \frac{x}{2}\sin \frac{x}{3}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin x\sin \frac{x}{2}\sin \frac{x}{3}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \left(\cos \frac{2}{3} x - \cos \frac{4}{3} x\right)\sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} \int \cos \frac {2}{3} x \sin \frac {x}{2} d x - \frac {1}{2} \int \cos \frac {4}{3} x \sin \frac {x}{2} d x \\ = \frac {1}{4} \int \left(\sin \frac {7}{6} x - \sin \frac {1}{6} x\right) d x - \frac {1}{4} \int \left(\sin \frac {1 1}{6} x - \sin \frac {5}{6} x\right) d x \\ = - \frac {3}{1 4} \cos \frac {7}{6} x + \frac {3}{2} \cos \frac {x}{6} + \frac {3}{2 2} \cos \frac {1 1}{6} x - \frac {3}{1 0} \cos \frac {5}{6} x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2016】 $\int \sin x\sin (x + a)\sin (x + b)\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sin x\sin (x + a)\sin (x + b)\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \sin x[\cos (a - b) - \cos (2x + a + b)]\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{2} \cos x \cos (a - b) - \frac {1}{4} \int [ \sin (3 x + a + b) - \sin (x + a + b) ] d x \\ = - \frac {1}{2} \cos x \cos (a - b) + \frac {1}{1 2} \cos (3 x + a + b) - \frac {1}{4} \cos (x + a + b) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2017】 $\int \cos^2 ax\cos^2 bx\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \cos^2 ax\cos^2 bx\mathrm{d}x = \int (\cos ax\cos bx)^2\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int [\cos (a - b)x + \cos (a + b)x]^2\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{4} \int [ \cos^ {2} (a - b) x + \cos^ {2} (a + b) x + 2 \cos (a - b) x \cos (a + b) x ] d x \\ = \frac {1}{8} \int [ 2 + \cos 2 (a + b) x + \cos 2 (a - b) x ] d x + \frac {1}{4} \int (\cos 2 a x + \cos 2 b x) d x \\ = \frac {x}{4} + \frac {\sin 2 (a + b) x}{1 6 (a + b)} + \frac {\sin 2 (a - b) x}{1 6 (a - b)} + \frac {1}{8 a} \sin 2 a x + \frac {1}{8 b} \sin 2 b x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2018】 $\int \sin^3 2x\cos^2 3x\mathrm{d}x.$

解先利用三角公式化简 $\sin^3 2x\cos^2 3x\mathrm{d}x$ ，得

$$
\sin^ {3} 2 x \cos^ {2} 3 x = - \frac {1}{1 6} \sin 1 2 x + \frac {3}{1 6} \sin 8 x - \frac {1}{8} \sin 6 x - \frac {3}{1 6} \sin 4 x + \frac {3}{8} \sin 2 x.
$$

于是， $\int \sin^3 2x\cos^2 3x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{192}\cos 12x - \frac{3}{128}\cos 8x + \frac{1}{48}\cos 6x + \frac{3}{64}\cos 4x - \frac{3}{16}\cos 2x + C.$

为了计算下面的积分，可以运用恒等式：

$$
\sin (\alpha - \beta) \equiv \sin [ (x + \alpha) - (x + \beta) ], \quad \cos (\alpha - \beta) \equiv \cos [ (x + \alpha) - (x + \beta) ].
$$

求积分：

【2019】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin(x + a)\sin(x + b)}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin(x + a)\sin(x + b)} = \frac{1}{\sin(a - b)}\int \frac{\sin[(x + a) - (x + b)]}{\sin(x + a)\sin(x + b)}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{\sin (a - b)} \int \left[ \frac {\cos (x + b)}{\sin (x + b)} - \frac {\cos (x + a)}{\sin (x + a)} \right] d x = \frac {1}{\sin (a - b)} \ln \left| \frac {\sin (x + b)}{\cos (x + a)} \right| + C,
$$

其中 $\sin (a - b)\neq 0.$

【2020】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin(x + a)\cos(x + b)}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin(x + a)\cos(x + b)} = \frac{1}{\cos(a - b)}\int \frac{\cos[(x + a) - (x + b)]}{\sin(x + a)\cos(x + b)}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{\cos (a - b)} \int \left[ \frac {\cos (x + a)}{\sin (x + a)} + \frac {\sin (x + b)}{\cos (x + b)} \right] d x = \frac {1}{\cos (a - b)} \ln \left| \frac {\sin (x + a)}{\cos (x + b)} \right| + C.
$$

其中 $\cos (a - b)\neq 0.$

【2021】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos(x + a)\cos(x + b)}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos(x + a)\cos(x + b)} = \frac{1}{\sin(a - b)}\int \frac{\sin[(x + a) - (x + b)]\mathrm{d}x}{\cos(x + a)\cos(x + b)}$

$$
= \frac {1}{\sin (a - b)} \int \left[ \frac {\sin (x + a)}{\cos (x + a)} - \frac {\sin (x + b)}{\cos (x + b)} \right] d x = \frac {1}{\sin (a - b)} \ln \left| \frac {\cos (x + b)}{\cos (x + a)} \right| + C,
$$

其中 $\sin (a - b)\neq 0^{*}$

\*) 当 $a - b = 2k\pi (k = 0, \pm 1, \pm 2, \dots)$ 时，是更简单的积分，2019题及2020题与本题类似，解法从略.

【2022】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x - \sin a}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x - \sin a} = \frac{1}{\cos a}\int \frac{\cos\left(\frac{x + a}{2} - \frac{x - a}{2}\right)}{\sin x - \sin a}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\cos a}\int \frac{\cos\frac{x + a}{2}\cos\frac{x - a}{2} + \sin\frac{x + a}{2}\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}{2\cos\frac{x + a}{2}\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{2 \cos a} \int \left(\frac {\cos \frac {x - a}{2}}{\sin \frac {x - a}{2}} + \frac {\sin \frac {x + a}{2}}{\cos \frac {x + a}{2}}\right) d x = \frac {1}{\cos a} \ln \left| \frac {\sin \frac {x - a}{2}}{\cos \frac {x + a}{2}} \right| + C,
$$

其中 $\cos a\neq 0$

【2023】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x + \cos a}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x + \cos a} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right)}{\sin\left(x + \frac{\pi}{2}\right) - \sin\left(a + \frac{3}{2}\pi\right)}$

$$
= \frac {1}{\cos \left(a + \frac {3}{2} \pi\right)} \ln \left| \frac {\sin \frac {x - a - \pi}{2}}{\cos \frac {x + a + 2 \pi}{2}} \right| ^ {*}) + C = \frac {1}{\sin a} \ln \left| \frac {\cos \frac {x - a}{2}}{\cos \frac {x + a}{2}} \right| + C,
$$

其中 $\sin a\neq 0$

\*) 利用2022题的结果.

【2024】 $\int \tan x \tan (x + a) \, \mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \tan x \tan (x + a) \, \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\sin x \sin (x + a)}{\cos x \cos (x + a)} \, \mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\cos x \cos (x + a) + \sin x \sin (x + a) - \cos x \cos (x + a)}{\cos x \cos (x + a)} d x = \int \frac {\cos a - \cos x \cos (x + a)}{\cos x \cos (x + a)} d x \\ = - x + \cos a \int \frac {d x}{\cos (x + a) \cos x} = - x + \cot a \ln \left| \frac {\cos x}{\cos (x + a)} \right| ^ {\prime \prime} + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\sin a\neq 0$

\*) 利用2021题的结果.

形如

的积分在一般情形下可利用代换 $\tan \frac{x}{2} = t$ 化为有理函数的积分.

（1）若等式

$R(-\sin x, \cos x) \equiv -R(\sin x, \cos x)$ 或 $R(\sin x, -\cos x) \equiv -R(\sin x, \cos x)$

成立，则最好利用相应的代换 $\cos x = t$ 或 $\sin x = t$ .

(2) 若等式 $R(-\sin x, -\cos x) \equiv R(\sin x, \cos x)$ 成立，则最好利用代换 $\tan x = t$

求积分：

【2025】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2\sin x - \cos x + 5}$

解设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ 则 $\sin x = \frac{2t}{1 + t^2},\cos x = \frac{1 - t^2}{1 + t^2},\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2\mathrm{d}t}{1 + t^2}.$ 代人得

$$
\int \frac {d x}{2 \sin x - \cos x + 5} = \int \frac {d t}{3 t ^ {2} + 2 t + 2} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {5}} \arctan \left(\frac {3 t + 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + C = \frac {1}{\sqrt {5}} \arctan \left(\frac {3 \tan \frac {x}{2} + 1}{\sqrt {5}}\right) + C.
$$

【2026】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(2 + \cos x)\sin x}$

解设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ，同2025题，得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(2 + \cos x) \sin x} = \int \frac {1 + t ^ {2}}{t (3 + t ^ {2})} \mathrm {d} t = \int \left[ \frac {1}{3 t} + \frac {2 t}{3 (3 + t ^ {2})} \right] \mathrm {d} t = \frac {1}{3} \ln | t (3 + t ^ {2}) | + C _ {1}
$$

$\text{串}$ 由于 $t(3 + t^2) = \tan \frac{x}{2}\left(2 + \sec^2\frac{x}{2}\right) = \frac{\sin\frac{x}{2}}{\cos^3\frac{x}{2}}\left(1 + 2\cos^2\frac{x}{2}\right)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {(1 - \cos x) (2 + \cos x) ^ {2}}{(1 + \cos x) ^ {3}} + C. \\ = \frac {\left(\frac {1 - \cos x}{2}\right) ^ {\frac {1}{2}}}{\left(\frac {1 + \cos x}{2}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} (\cos x + 2) = 2 \left[ \frac {(1 - \cos x) (\cos x + 2) ^ {2}}{(1 + \cos x) ^ {3}} \right] ^ {\frac {1}{2}}, \\ \end{array}
$$

因而， $\ln |t(3 + t^2)| = \ln 2 + \frac{1}{2}\ln \frac{(1 - \cos x)(2 + \cos x)^2}{(1 + \cos x)^3}.$

【2027】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x}{\sin x + 2\cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\tan \frac{x}{2} = t$ ，同2025题，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sin^ {2} x}{\sin x + 2 \cos x} d x = 4 \int \frac {t ^ {2} d t}{(1 + t ^ {2}) ^ {2} (1 + t - t ^ {2})} = \frac {4}{5} \int \left[ \frac {1}{1 + t ^ {2}} + \frac {- 2 + t}{(1 + t ^ {2}) ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{1 + t - t ^ {2}} \right] d t \\ = \frac {4}{5} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{1 + t ^ {2}} - \frac {8}{5} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{(1 + t ^ {2}) ^ {2}} + \frac {2}{5} \int \frac {2 t \mathrm {d} t}{(1 + t ^ {2}) ^ {2}} + \frac {4}{5} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (t - \frac {1}{2})}{\frac {5}{4} - (t - \frac {1}{2}) ^ {2}} \\ = \frac {4}{5} \arctan t - \frac {8}{5} \left[ \frac {t}{2 \left(1 + t ^ {2}\right)} + \frac {1}{2} \arctan t \right] ^ {*}) - \frac {2}{5} \cdot \frac {1}{1 + t ^ {2}} + \frac {4}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} + (t - \frac {1}{2})}{\frac {\sqrt {5}}{2} - (t - \frac {1}{2})} \right| + C _ {1} \\ = - \frac {2}{5} \cdot \frac {1 + 2 t}{1 + t ^ {2}} + \frac {4}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\frac {\sqrt {5} - 1}{2} + t}{\frac {\sqrt {5} + 1}{2} - t} \right| + C _ {1} \\ = - \frac {1}{5} (\cos x + 2 \sin x) ^ {* *}) + \frac {4}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) \right| ^ {* * *} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1817题的结果.

$$
* *) \quad - \frac {2}{5} \cdot \frac {1 + 2 t}{1 + t ^ {2}} = - \frac {2}{5} \cdot \frac {1 + 2 \tan \frac {x}{2}}{\sec^ {2} \frac {x}{2}} = - \frac {2}{5} \cdot \frac {1 + 2 \cdot \frac {\sin x}{1 + \cos x}}{\frac {2}{1 + \cos x}} = - \frac {1}{5} (\cos x + 2 \sin x) - \frac {1}{5}.
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left. \right.\left. * * *\right) \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {5} - 1}{2} + t{\frac {\sqrt {5} + 1}{2} - t} \right| = \ln \left| \frac {\tan \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) + \tan \frac {x}{2}}{\cot \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) - \tan \frac {x}{2}} \right| \\ = \ln \left| \frac {\tan \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) + \tan \frac {x}{2}}{1 - \tan \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) \tan \frac {x}{2}} \right| + \ln \frac {1}{\cot \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right)} \\ = \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) \right| - \ln \left[ \cot \left(\frac {\arctan 2}{2}\right) \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2028】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \varepsilon\cos x},\quad (1)0 <   \varepsilon <  1;\quad (2)\varepsilon >1.$

解设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ，同2025题，得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \varepsilon\cos x} = 2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{(1 + \varepsilon) + (1 - \varepsilon)t^2} = I.$

(1) $0 < \varepsilon < 1$

$$
I = \frac {2}{1 + \varepsilon} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{1 + \left(\frac {1 - \varepsilon}{1 + \varepsilon}\right) t ^ {2}} = \frac {2}{\sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2}}} \arctan \left(t \sqrt {\frac {1 - \varepsilon}{1 + \varepsilon}}\right) + C = \frac {2}{\sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2}}} \arctan \left(\sqrt {\frac {1 - \varepsilon}{1 + \varepsilon}} \tan \frac {x}{2}\right) + C;
$$

(2) $\varepsilon > 1$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I = \frac {2}{\varepsilon - 1} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{\left(\frac {\varepsilon + 1}{\varepsilon - 1}\right) - t ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {\varepsilon + 1} + \sqrt {\varepsilon - 1} t}{\sqrt {\varepsilon + 1} - \sqrt {\varepsilon - 1} t} \right| + C \\ = \frac {1}{\sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1}} \ln \left| \frac {\varepsilon + \cos x + \sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1} \sin x}{1 + \varepsilon \cos x} \right| ^ {*}) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

$\frac{\sqrt{\varepsilon + 1} + t\sqrt{\varepsilon - 1}}{\sqrt{\varepsilon + 1} - t\sqrt{\varepsilon - 1}} = \frac{\varepsilon + 1 + 2t\sqrt{\varepsilon^2 - 1} + (\varepsilon - 1)t^2}{(\varepsilon + 1) - (\varepsilon - 1)t^2} = \frac{\varepsilon(1 + t^2) + (1 - t^2) + 2\sqrt{\varepsilon^2 - 1}t}{\varepsilon(1 - t^2) + (1 + t^2)}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {\varepsilon (1 + t ^ {2}) + (1 + t ^ {2}) \cos x + 2 t \sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1}}{\varepsilon (1 + t ^ {2}) \cos x + (1 + t ^ {2})} \\ = \frac {\varepsilon + \cos x + \sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1} \frac {2 t}{1 + t ^ {2}}}{\varepsilon \cos x + 1} = \frac {\varepsilon + \cos x + \sqrt {\varepsilon^ {2} - 1} \sin x}{\varepsilon \cos x + 1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2029】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x}{1 + \sin^2x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x}{1 + \sin^2 x} \mathrm{d}x = \int \left(1 - \frac{1}{1 + \sin^2 x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = x - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan x)}{\sec^2 x + \tan^2 x} = x - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan x)}{1 + 2\tan^2 x}$

$$
= x - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan (\sqrt {2} \tan x) + C.
$$

【2030】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{a^2\sin^2x + b^2\cos^2x}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{a^2\sin^2x + b^2\cos^2x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan x)}{a^2\tan^2x + b^2} = \frac{1}{ab}\arctan \left(\frac{a\tan x}{b}\right) + C,$

其中 $ab\neq 0$

【2031】 $\int \frac{\cos^2 x \mathrm{d}x}{(a^2 \sin^2 x + b^2 \cos^2 x)^2}$ .

解 $\int \frac{\cos^2 x \, \mathrm{d}x}{(a^2 \sin^2 x + b^2 \cos^2 x)^2} = \frac{1}{a} \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(a \tan x)}{(a^2 \tan^2 x + b^2)^2} = \frac{\tan x}{2b^2 (a^2 \tan^2 x + b^2)} + \frac{1}{2ab^3} \arctan \left( \frac{a \tan x}{b} \right)^{*} + C,$ 其中 $ab \neq 0$ .

\*) 利用1921题的结果.

【2032】 $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\sin^2\left(x + \frac{\pi}{4}\right) - \frac{1}{2}}{\sqrt{2}\sin\left(x + \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \sin \left(x + \frac{\pi}{4}\right)\mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin\left(x + \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \cos \left(x + \frac {\pi}{4}\right) - \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\pi}{8}\right) \right| + C \\ = \frac {1}{2} (\sin x - \cos x) - \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\pi}{8}\right) \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2033】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^2}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^2} = \frac{1}{a}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(a\tan x + b)}{(a\tan x + b)^2} = -\frac{1}{a\tan x + b} +C = -\frac{\cos x}{a(a\sin x + b\cos x)} +C.$

【2034】 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3x + \cos^3x}$

解 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^3x + \cos^3x} = \int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{(\sin x + \cos x)(1 - \sin x\cos x)}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {(\sin x - \cos x) d x}{(\sin x + \cos x) (1 - \sin x \cos x)} + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d x}{1 - \sin x \cos x} \\ = \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {- (\cos x - \sin x) d x}{\sin x + \cos x} + \frac {1}{6} \int \frac {\sin^ {2} x - \cos^ {2} x}{1 - \sin x \cos x} d x + \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {d x}{1 - \sin x \cos x} \\ = - \frac {1}{3} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\sin x + \cos x)}{\sin x + \cos x} + \frac {1}{6} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (1 - \sin x \cos x)}{1 - \sin x \cos x} - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\cot x)}{\left(\cot x - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {3}{4}} \\ = - \frac {1}{6} \ln \frac {(\sin x + \cos x) ^ {2}}{1 - \sin x \cos x} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {2 \cos x - \sin x}{\sqrt {3} \sin x}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2035】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 x + \cos^4 x}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 x + \cos^4 x} = \int \frac{2\mathrm{d}x}{2 - \sin^2 2x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan 2x)}{2\sec^2 2x - \tan^2 2x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan 2x)}{2 + \tan^2 2x} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \arctan \left( \frac{\tan 2x}{\sqrt{2}} \right) + C.$

【2036】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x\cos^2x}{\sin^8x + \cos^8x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x \cos^2 x}{\sin^8 x + \cos^8 x} \, \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{2 \sin^2 2x \, \mathrm{d}x}{\sin^4 2x - 8 \sin^2 2x + 8} = \int \frac{\tan^2 2x \, \mathrm{d}(\tan 2x)}{\tan^4 2x - 8 \tan^2 2x \sec^2 2x + 8 \sec^4 2x}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\tan^ {2} 2 x \mathrm {d} (\tan 2 x)}{\tan^ {4} 2 x + 8 \tan^ {2} 2 x + 8} = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{4} (2 + \sqrt {2}) \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\tan 2 x)}{\tan^ {2} 2 x + 4 + 2 \sqrt {2}} - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{4} (2 - \sqrt {2}) \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\tan 2 x)}{\tan^ {2} 2 x + 4 - 2 \sqrt {2}} \\ = \frac {1}{4} \left[ \sqrt {2 + \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\tan 2 x}{\sqrt {4 + 2 \sqrt {2}}}\right) - \sqrt {2 - \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\tan 2 x}{\sqrt {4 - 2 \sqrt {2}}}\right) \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2037】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x - \cos^2x}{\sin^4x + \cos^4x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x - \cos^2 x}{\sin^4 x + \cos^4 x} \mathrm{d}x = -\int \frac{\cos 2x}{1 - \frac{1}{2}\sin^2 2x} \mathrm{d}x = -\frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}} \int \left( \frac{2\cos 2x}{\sqrt{2} - \sin 2x} + \frac{2\cos 2x}{\sqrt{2} + \sin 2x} \right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {2} - \sin 2 x}{\sqrt {2} + \sin 2 x} + C.
$$

【2038】 $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{1 + \sin^4x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{1 + \sin^4x}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\tan x\sec^2x}{\sec^4x + \tan^4x}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\tan^2x)}{2\tan^4x + 2\tan^2x + 1} = \frac{1}{2}\arctan (1 + 2\tan^2 x) + C.$   
【2039】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^6 x + \cos^6 x}$   
解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^6 x + \cos^6 x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 - 3\sin^2 x\cos^2 x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 - \frac{3}{4}\sin^2 2x} = \int \frac{2\mathrm{d}(\tan 2x)}{4\sec^2 2x - 3\tan^2 2x} = \arctan \left(\frac{\tan 2x}{2}\right) + C.$   
【2040】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(\sin^2 x + 2\cos^2 x)^2}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(\sin^2 x + 2\cos^2 x)^2} = \int \frac{\frac{1}{\cos^4 x} \mathrm{d}x}{(\tan^2 x + 2)^2} = \int \frac{\sec^2 x \mathrm{d}(\tan x)}{(\tan^2 x + 2)^2}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {\tan^ {2} x}{(\tan^ {2} x + 2) ^ {2}} d (\tan x) + \int \frac {d (\tan x)}{(\tan^ {2} x + 2) ^ {2}} = \int \frac {(\tan^ {2} x + 2) - 2}{(\tan^ {2} x + 2) ^ {2}} d (\tan x) + \int \frac {d (\tan x)}{(\tan^ {2} x + 2) ^ {2}} \\ = \int \frac {d (\tan x)}{\tan^ {2} x + 2} - \int \frac {d (\tan x)}{(\tan^ {2} x + 2) ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\tan x}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - \frac {\tan x}{4 (\tan^ {2} x + 2)} - \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\tan x}{\sqrt {2}}\right) ^ {*}) + C \\ = \frac {3}{4 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \left(\frac {\tan x}{\sqrt {2}}\right) - \frac {\tan x}{4 (\tan^ {2} x + 2)} + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1817题的结果.

【2041】把分母化为对数的形式，求积分 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{a\sin x + b\cos x}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{a\sin x + b\cos x} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin(x + \varphi)} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}\ln \left|\tan \left(\frac{x + \varphi}{2}\right)\right| + C,$

式中 $\cos \varphi = \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}, \sin \varphi = \frac{b}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}, a^2 + b^2 \neq 0.$

【2042】证明： $\int \frac{a_1\sin x + b_1\cos x}{a\sin x + b\cos x}\mathrm{d}x = Ax + B\ln |a\sin x + b\cos x| + C$ ，式中 $A,B,C$ 为常数.

提示 首先， $a$ 及 $b$ 不可能同时为零.其次，令

$$
a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x \equiv A (a \sin x + b \cos x) + B (a \cos x - b \sin x),
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，可得 $A, B$

$$
A = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, B = \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \quad (a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} \neq 0),
$$

并注意 $(a\cos x - b\sin x)\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{d}(a\sin x + b\cos x)$ ，命题即易获证.

证设 $a_1\sin x + b_1\cos x \equiv A(a\sin x + b\cos x) + B(a\cos x - b\sin x),$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，可得 $A = \frac{aa_1 + bb_1}{a^2 + b^2}$ ， $B = \frac{ab_1 - a_1b}{a^2 + b^2}$ ， $a^2 + b^2 \neq 0$ 。于是，

$$
\int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{a \sin x + b \cos x} d x = A \int d x + B \int \frac {d (a \sin x + b \cos x)}{a \sin x + b \cos x} = A x + B \ln | a \sin x + b \cos x | + C.
$$

求积分：

【2043】 $\int \frac{\sin x - \cos x}{\sin x + 2\cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解此为2042题的特例，这里 $a_1 = 1$ ， $b_{1} = -1$ ， $a = 1$ ， $b = 2$

$$
A = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {1 - 2}{1 + 4} = - \frac {1}{5}, B = \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {- 1 - 2}{1 + 4} = - \frac {3}{5}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin x - \cos x}{\sin x + 2\cos x}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{x}{5} -\frac{3}{5}\ln |\sin x + 2\cos x| + C.$

【2044】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + 5\tan x}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + 5\tan x} = \int \frac{\cos x}{5\sin x + 3\cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$ 此为2042题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 0, \quad b _ {1} = 1, \quad a = 5, \quad b = 3; A = \frac {3}{3 4}, \quad B = \frac {5}{3 4}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + 5\tan x} = \frac{3}{34} x + \frac{5}{34}\ln |5\sin x + 3\cos x| + C.$

【2045】 $\int \frac{a_1\sin x + b_1\cos x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^2}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示仿2042题，并利用2041题的结果

解仿2042题，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {2}} d x = A \int \frac {a \sin x + b \cos x}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {2}} d x + B \int \frac {a \cos x - b \sin x}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {2}} d x \\ = A \int \frac {d x}{a \sin x + b \cos x} d x + B \int \frac {d (a \sin x + b \cos x)}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {2}} = \frac {A}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\varphi}{2}\right) \right| ^ {*}) - \frac {B}{a \sin x + b \cos x} + C \\ = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{\left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\varphi}{2}\right) \right| - \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{\left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}\right) \left(a \sin x + b \cos x\right)} + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

式中 $A = \frac{aa_1 + bb_1}{a^2 + b^2},\quad B = \frac{ab_1 - a_1b}{a^2 + b^2},\cos \varphi = \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}},\quad \sin \varphi = \frac{b}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}},\quad a^2 +b^2\neq 0$

（显然按题意 $a, b$ 不同时为零）.

\*) 利用2041题的结果.

【2046】 证明：

$$
\int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x + c _ {1}}{a \sin x + b \cos x + c} d x = A x + B \ln | a \sin x + b \cos x + c | + C \int \frac {d x}{a \sin x + b \cos x + c},
$$

式中 $A, B, C$ 为常数.

提示 首先， $a$ 及 $b$ 不可能同时为零.其次，令

$$
a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x + c _ {1} = A (a \sin x + b \cos x + c) + B (a \cos x - b \sin x) + C,
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，可得 $A, B, C$

$$
A = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, B = \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, C = \frac {a (a c _ {1} - a _ {1} c) + b (b c _ {1} - b _ {1} c)}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \quad (a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} \neq 0),
$$

并注意 $(a\cos x - b\sin x)\mathrm{d}x = d(a\sin x + b\cos x + c)$ ，命题即易获证.

证 按题意 $a, b$ 不同时为零. 设

$$
a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x + c _ {1} \equiv A (a \sin x + b \cos x + c) + B (a \cos x - b \sin x) + C,
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，则有

$$
A = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, \quad B = \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, C = \frac {a (a c _ {1} - a _ {1} c) + b (b c _ {1} - b _ {1} c)}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{a_1\sin x + b_1\cos x + c_1}{a\sin x + b\cos x + c}\mathrm{d}x = A\int \mathrm{d}x + B\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(a\sin x + b\cos x + c)}{a\sin x + b\cos x + c} +C\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{a\sin x + b\cos x + c}$

$$
= A x + B \ln | a \sin x + b \cos x + c | + C \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{a \sin x + b \cos x + c}.
$$

求积分：

【2047】 $\int \frac{\sin x + 2\cos x - 3}{\sin x - 2\cos x + 3}\mathrm{d}x.$

解此为2046题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 1, b _ {1} = 2, c _ {1} = - 3, a = 1, b = - 2, c = 3;
$$

$$
A = \frac {a a _ {1} + b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {1 - 4}{1 + 4} = - \frac {3}{5}, \quad B = \frac {a b _ {1} - a _ {1} b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {2 + 2}{1 + 4} = \frac {4}{5},
$$

$$
C = \frac {a \left(a c _ {1} - a _ {1} c\right) + b \left(b c _ {1} - b _ {1} c\right)}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {(- 3 - 3) + (- 2) (6 - 6)}{1 + 4} = - \frac {6}{5}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin x + 2\cos x - 3}{\sin x - 2\cos x + 3}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{3}{5} x + \frac{4}{5}\ln |\sin x - 2\cos x + 3| - \frac{6}{5}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x - 2\cos x + 3}$

$$
= - \frac {3}{5} x + \frac {4}{5} \ln | \sin x - 2 \cos x + 3 | - \frac {6}{5} \arctan \frac {1 + 5 \tan \frac {x}{2} \cdot)}{2} + C.
$$

\*) 设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ , 积分即得所求式子.

【2048】 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2} + \sin x + \cos x}.$

解此为2046题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 1, b _ {1} = 0, c _ {1} = 0, a = 1, b = 1, c = \sqrt {2}; A = \frac {1}{2}, B = - \frac {1}{2}, C = - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2} + \sin x + \cos x} = \frac{1}{2} x - \frac{1}{2}\ln |\sqrt{2} +\sin x + \cos x| - \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2} + \sin x + \cos x}$

$$
= \frac {1}{2} x - \frac {1}{2} \ln | \sqrt {2} + \sin x + \cos x | - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {2} + \sqrt {2} \cos \left(x - \frac {\pi}{4}\right)}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} x - \frac {1}{2} \ln | \sqrt {2} + \sin x + \cos x | - \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{2 \cos^ {2} \left(\frac {x}{2} - \frac {\pi}{8}\right)} \\ = \frac {1}{2} x - \frac {1}{2} \ln | \sqrt {2} + \sin x + \cos x | - \frac {1}{2} \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} - \frac {\pi}{8}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2049】 $\int \frac{2\sin x + \cos x}{3\sin x + 4\cos x - 2}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 本题也是2046题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 2, b _ {1} = 1, c _ {1} = 0, a = 3, b = 4, c = - 2; A = \frac {2}{5}, B = - \frac {1}{5}, C = \frac {4}{5}.
$$

代人得 $\int \frac{2\sin x + \cos x}{3\sin x + 4\cos x - 2}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2}{5} x - \frac{1}{5}\ln |3\sin x + 4\cos x - 2| + \frac{4}{5}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3\sin x + 4\cos x - 2}$

$$
= \frac {2}{5} x - \frac {1}{5} \ln | 3 \sin x + 4 \cos x - 2 | + \frac {4}{5 \sqrt {2 1}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {7} + \sqrt {3} (2 \tan \frac {x}{2} - 1)}{\sqrt {7} - \sqrt {3} (2 \tan \frac {x}{2} - 1)} \right| ^ {*}) + C.
$$

\*) 设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ , 积分即得所求式子.

【2050】 证明：

$$
\int \frac {a _ {1} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b _ {1} \sin x \cos x + c _ {1} \cos^ {2} x}{a \sin x + b \cos x} d x = A \sin x + B \cos x + C \int \frac {d x}{a \sin x + b \cos x},
$$

式中 $A, B, C$ 为常数.

提示 首先， $a$ 及 $b$ 不可能同时为零.其次，令

$$
a _ {1} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b _ {1} \sin x \cos x + c _ {1} \cos^ {2} x \equiv A \cos x (a \sin x + b \cos x) - B \sin x (a \sin x + b \cos x) + C,
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，可得 $A, B, C$

$$
A = \frac {b c _ {1} - a _ {1} b + 2 a b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, B = \frac {a c _ {1} - a a _ {1} - 2 b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}, C = \frac {a _ {1} b ^ {2} + a ^ {2} c _ {1} - 2 a b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} (a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} \neq 0),
$$

命题即易获证.

证 按题意 $a, b$ 不同时为零. 设

$$
a _ {1} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b _ {1} \sin x \cos x + c _ {1} \cos^ {2} x \equiv A \cos x (a \sin x + b \cos x) - B \sin x (a \sin x + b \cos x) + C,
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，则有

$$
a A - b B = 2 b _ {1}, \quad C - a B = a _ {1}, \quad C + b A = c _ {1},
$$

从而， $A = \frac{bc_1 - a_1b + 2ab_1}{a^2 + b^2},\quad B = \frac{ac_1 - aa_1 - 2bb_1}{a^2 + b^2},C = \frac{a_1b^2 + a^2c_1 - 2abb_1}{a^2 + b^2}.$

代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {a _ {1} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b _ {1} \sin x \cos x + c _ {1} \cos^ {2} x}{a \sin x + b \cos x} d x = A \int \cos x d x - B \int \sin x d x + C \int \frac {d x}{a \sin x + b \cos x} \\ = A \sin x + B \cos x + C \int \frac {d x}{a \sin x + b \cos x}. \\ \end{array}
$$

求积分：

【2051】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x - 4\sin x\cos x + 3\cos^2x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解此为2050题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 1, b _ {1} = - 2, c _ {1} = 3, a = 1, b = 1;
$$

$$
A = \frac {b c _ {1} - a _ {1} b + 2 a b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {3 - 1 - 4}{1 + 1} = - 1, B = \frac {a c _ {1} - a a _ {1} - 2 b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {3 - 1 + 4}{1 + 1} = 3, C = \frac {a _ {1} b ^ {2} + a ^ {2} c _ {1} - 2 a b b _ {1}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} = \frac {1 + 3 + 4}{1 + 1} = 4.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x - 4\sin x\cos x + 3\cos^2 x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{d}x = -\sin x + 3\cos x + 4\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x + \cos x}$

$$
= - \sin x + 3 \cos x + \frac {4}{\sqrt {2}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin \left(x + \frac {\pi}{4}\right)} = - \sin x + 3 \cos x + 2 \sqrt {2} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\pi}{8}\right) \right| + C.
$$

【2052】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x - \sin x\cos x + 2\cos^2x}{\sin x + 2\cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 本题也是2050题的特例，这里

$$
a _ {1} = 1, b _ {1} = - \frac {1}{2}, c _ {1} = 2, a = 1, b = 2; A = \frac {1}{5}, B = \frac {3}{5}, C = \frac {8}{5}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x - \sin x \cos x + 2 \cos^2 x}{\sin x + 2 \cos x} \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {1}{5} \sin x + \frac {3}{5} \cos x + \frac {8}{5} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin x + 2 \cos x} = \frac {1}{5} (\sin + 3 \cos x) + \frac {8}{5 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {5} + 2 \tan \frac {x}{2} - 1}{\sqrt {5} - 2 \tan \frac {x}{2} + 1} \right| ^ {*}) + C.
$$

\*) 设 $t = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ , 积分即得所求式子.

【2053】 证明：若 $(a - c)^2 + b^2 \neq 0$ ，则

$$
\int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{a \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x = A \int \frac {d u _ {1}}{k _ {1} u _ {1} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {1}} + B \int \frac {d u _ {2}}{k _ {2} u _ {2} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {2}},
$$

式中 $A, B$ 为待定系数， $\lambda_1, \lambda_2$ 为方程 $\left| \begin{array}{cc} a - \lambda & b \\ b & c - \lambda \end{array} \right| = 0 \quad (\lambda_1 \neq \lambda_2)$

的根，而 $u_{i} = (a - \lambda_{i})\sin x + b\cos x, k_{i} = \frac{1}{a - \lambda_{i}} (i = 1,2).$

证记

$$
\begin{array}{l} a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + c \cos^ {2} x = (a - \lambda_ {i}) \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + (c - \lambda_ {i}) \cos^ {2} x + \lambda_ {i} \\ = \frac {1}{a - \lambda_ {i}} \left[ (a - \lambda_ {i}) ^ {2} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b (a - \lambda_ {i}) \sin x \cos x + (c - \lambda_ {i}) (a - \lambda_ {i}) \cos^ {2} x \right] + \lambda_ {i}, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\lambda_{i}(i = 1,2)$ 为方程 $\left| \begin{array}{cc}a - \lambda & b\\ b & c - \lambda \end{array} \right| = 0$ 的根.

由假定 $(a - c)^2 + b^2 \neq 0$ ，从而， $(a - c)^2 + 4b^2 \neq 0$ ，因此 $\lambda_1 \neq \lambda_2$ 。再设 $k_i = \frac{1}{a - \lambda_i} (i = 1, 2)$ 及 $u_i = (a - \lambda_i)$ 。 $\cdot \sin x + b\cos x$ 。由于 $(a - \lambda_i)(c - \lambda_i) - b^2 = 0$ ，即 $b^2 = (a - \lambda_i)(c - \lambda_i)$ 。于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + c \cos^ {2} x = k _ {i} \left[ (a - \lambda_ {i}) ^ {2} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b (a - \lambda_ {i}) \sin x \cos x + b ^ {2} \cos^ {2} x \right] + \lambda_ {i} \\ = k _ {i} \left[ (a - \lambda_ {i}) \sin x + b \cos x \right] ^ {2} + \lambda_ {i} = k _ {i} u _ {i} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {i}. \tag {1} \\ \end{array}
$$

其次，设

$$
a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x = A \left[ (a - \lambda_ {1}) \cos x - b \sin x \right] + B \left[ (a - \lambda_ {2}) \cos x - b \sin x \right], \tag {2}
$$

比较等式两端同类项的系数，则有

$$
- b (A + B) = a _ {1}, \quad A (a - \lambda_ {1}) + B (a - \lambda_ {2}) = b _ {1},
$$

$$
A = - \frac {a _ {1} (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2}) + b b _ {1} + a _ {1} (a - \lambda_ {1})}{b (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2})}, \quad B = \frac {b b _ {1} + a _ {1} (a - \lambda_ {1}) ^ {*}}{b (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2})}.
$$

由（1）式及（2）式即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x \\ = A \int \frac {(a - \lambda_ {1}) \cos x - b \sin x}{k _ {1} [ (a - \lambda_ {1}) \sin x + b \cos x ] ^ {2} + \lambda_ {1}} d x + B \int \frac {(a - \lambda_ {2}) \cos x - b \sin x}{k _ {2} [ (a - \lambda_ {2}) \sin x + b \cos x ] ^ {2} + \lambda_ {2}} d x \\ = A \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u _ {1}}{k _ {1} u _ {1} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {1}} + B \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u _ {2}}{k _ {2} u _ {2} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

*）按题意， $b \neq 0$ 。因若 $b = 0$ ，则 $\lambda_1 = a, \lambda_2 = c$ ，从而， $k_1$ 无意义。不过，当 $b = 0$ 时，仍能化为所要求的类似形式。事实上，当 $b = 0$ 时， $a \neq c$ ，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{a \sin^ {2} x + 2 b \sin x \cos x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x = \int \frac {a _ {1} \sin x + b _ {1} \cos x}{a \sin^ {2} x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x \\ = a _ {1} \int \frac {\sin x}{a \sin^ {2} x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x + b _ {1} \int \frac {\cos x}{a \sin^ {2} x + c \cos^ {2} x} d x = - a _ {1} \int \frac {d (\cos x)}{(c - a) \cos^ {2} x + a} + b _ {1} \int \frac {d (\sin x)}{(a - c) \sin^ {2} x + c} \\ = A \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u _ {1}}{k _ {1} u _ {1} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {1}} + B \int \frac {\mathrm {d} u _ {2}}{k _ {2} u _ {2} ^ {2} + \lambda_ {2}}, \\ \end{array}
$$

式中 $A = -a_{1}, B = b_{1}, k_{1} = c - a, k_{2} = a - c, u_{1} = \cos x, u_{2} = \sin x, \lambda_{1} = a, \lambda_{2} = c.$

本题也可用下法另证：命 $u_{i} = (a - \lambda_{i})\sin x + b\cos x$ ， $k_{i} = \frac{1}{a - \lambda_{i}} (i = 1,2)$ ，代入积分等式.然后两边求导，整理并比较系数，便可知 $\lambda_{i}$ 必为方程 $\left| \begin{array}{cc}a - \lambda & b\\ b & c - \lambda \end{array} \right| = 0$ 的根，相应可求出系数 $A,B$

求积分：

【2054】 $\int \frac{2\sin x - \cos x}{3\sin^2x + 4\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{2\sin x - \cos x}{3\sin^2x + 4\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{2\sin x}{3\sin^2x + 4\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x - \int \frac{\cos x}{3\sin^2x + 4\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= - 2 \int \frac {d (\cos x)}{3 + \cos^ {2} x} - \int \frac {d (\sin x)}{1 - \sin^ {2} x} = - \frac {2}{\sqrt {3}} \arctan \left(\frac {\cos x}{\sqrt {3}}\right) - \frac {1}{4} \ln \frac {2 + \sin x}{2 - \sin x} + C.
$$

【2055】 $\int \frac{\sin x + \cos x}{2\sin^2x - 4\sin x\cos x + 5\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 此为2053题的特例，这里 $a_1 = 1, b_1 = 1, a = 2, b = -2, c = 5.$ 由 $\left| \begin{array}{cc}a - \lambda & b\\ b & c - \lambda \end{array} \right| = \lambda^2 -7\lambda +6 = 0,$ 求得 $\lambda_{1} = 1,\lambda_{2} = 6$ ，从而，

$$
A = - \frac {a _ {1} (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2}) + b _ {1} b + a _ {1} (a - \lambda_ {1})}{b (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2})} = - \frac {(1 - 6) - 2 + (2 - 1)}{- 2 (1 - 6)} = \frac {3}{5},
$$

$$
B = \frac {b b _ {1} + a _ {1} (a - \lambda_ {1})}{b (\lambda_ {1} - \lambda_ {2})} = \frac {- 2 + 1}{1 0} = - \frac {1}{1 0};
$$

$$
u _ {1} = (a - \lambda_ {1}) \sin x + b \cos x = \sin x - 2 \cos x, u _ {2} = (a - \lambda_ {2}) \sin x + b \cos x = - 4 \sin x - 2 \cos x;
$$

$$
k _ {1} = \frac {1}{a - \lambda_ {1}} = 1, \quad k _ {2} = \frac {1}{a - \lambda_ {2}} = - \frac {1}{4}.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin x + \cos x}{2\sin^2x - 4\sin x\cos x + 5\cos^2x}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{3}{5}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sin x - 2\cos x)}{(\sin x - 2\cos x)^2 + 1} +\frac{1}{10}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(4\sin x + 2\cos x)}{6 - \frac{1}{4}(4\sin x + 2\cos x)^2}$

$$
= \frac {3}{5} \arctan (\sin x - 2 \cos x) + \frac {1}{1 0 \sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {6} + 2 \sin x + \cos x}{\sqrt {6} - 2 \sin x - \cos x} \right| + C.
$$

【2056】 $\int \frac{\sin x - 2\cos x}{1 + 4\sin x\cos x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 本题也是2053题的特例，且

$$
\int \frac {\sin x - 2 \cos x}{1 + 4 \sin x \cos x} d x = \int \frac {\sin x - 2 \cos x}{\sin^ {2} x + 4 \sin x \cos x + \cos^ {2} x} d x,
$$

这里， $a_1 = 1, b_1 = -2, a = 1, b = 2, c = 1; \lambda_1 = 3, \lambda_2 = -1; k_1 = -\frac{1}{2}, k_2 = \frac{1}{2}; A = \frac{1}{4}, B = -\frac{3}{4}$

$$
u _ {1} = 2 (\cos x - \sin x), \quad u _ {2} = 2 (\cos x + \sin x).
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\sin x - 2\cos x}{1 + 4\sin x\cos x}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{2\mathrm{d}(\cos x - \sin x)}{-2(\cos x - \sin x)^2 + 3} -\frac{3}{4}\int \frac{2\mathrm{d}(\cos x + \sin x)}{2(\cos x + \sin x)^2 - 1}$

$$
= \frac {3}{4 \sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {2} (\sin x + \cos x) + 1}{\sqrt {2} (\sin x + \cos x) - 1} \right| - \frac {1}{4 \sqrt {6}} \ln \left| \frac {\sqrt {3} + \sqrt {2} (\sin x - \cos x)}{\sqrt {3} - \sqrt {2} (\sin x - \cos x)} \right| + C.
$$

【2057】证明： $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^n} = \frac{A\sin x + B\cos x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} +C\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n - 2}},$

式中 $A, B, C$ 为待定系数.

证 $a\sin x + b\cos x = \sqrt{a^2 + b^2}\sin (x + a)$ ，式中 $\sin \alpha = \frac{b}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}$ $\cos \alpha = \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}.$

于是， $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^n} = (a^2 +b^2)^{-\frac{n}{2}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^n(x + a)} = -(a^2 +b^2)^{-\frac{n}{2}}\int \frac{1}{\sin^{n - 2}(x + a)}\mathrm{d}\left[\cot (x + a)\right]$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}\right) ^ {- \frac {n}{2}} \frac {\cot (x + a)}{\sin^ {n - 2} (x + a)} - \frac {n - 2}{\left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}\right) ^ {\frac {n}{2}}} \int \frac {\cot (x + a) \cos (x + a)}{\sin^ {n - 1} (x + a)} d x \\ = \frac {\frac {b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \sin x - \frac {a}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \cos x}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} - \frac {n - 2}{(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {n}{2}}} \int \frac {1 - \sin^ {2} (x + a)}{\sin^ {n} (x + a)} d x. \\ \end{array}
$$

设 $I_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n}}$ ，则由上式可得

$$
I _ {n} = \frac {\frac {b}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \sin x - \frac {a}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \cos x}{(a \sin x + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + (2 - n) I _ {n} + \frac {n - 2}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} I _ {n - 2}.
$$

于是， $I_{n} = \frac{\frac{b}{(n - 1)(a^{2} + b^{2})}\sin x - \frac{a}{(n - 1)(a^{2} + b^{2})}\cos x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} +\frac{n - 2}{(n - 1)(a^{2} + b^{2})} I_{n - 2}.$

即 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^n} = \frac{A\sin x + B\cos x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} + C\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a\sin x + b\cos x)^{n - 2}},$

式中 $A = \frac{b}{(n - 1)(a^2 + b^2)},\quad B = -\frac{a}{(n - 1)(a^2 + b^2)},\quad C = \frac{n - 2}{(n - 1)(a^2 + b^2)}.$

【2058】 求 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(\sin x + 2\cos x)^3}$

解 此为2057题的特例，这里 $a = 1$ ， $b = 2$ ， $n = 3$ ； $A = \frac{2}{10}$ ， $B = -\frac{1}{10}$ ， $C = \frac{1}{10}$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(\sin x + 2\cos x)^3} = \frac{2\sin x - \cos x}{10(\sin x + 2\cos x)^2} +\frac{1}{10}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x + 2\cos x}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {2 \sin x - \cos x}{1 0 (\sin x + 2 \cos x) ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{1 0 \sqrt {5}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sin (x + \alpha)} \\ = \frac {2 \sin x - \cos x}{1 0 (\sin x + 2 \cos x) ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{1 0 \sqrt {5}} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\alpha}{2}\right) \right| + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\cos \alpha = \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}, \sin \alpha = \frac{2}{\sqrt{5}}, \alpha = \arctan 2.$

【2059】若 $n$ 为大于1的正整数，证明：

$$
\int \frac {d x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n}} = \frac {A \sin x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + B \int \frac {d x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + C \int \frac {d x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 2}} (| a | \neq | b |),
$$

并求出系数 $A, B$ 和 $C$ .

证设 $I_{n} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a + b\cos x)^{n}}$ ，先考虑 $I_{n - 1}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {n - 1} = \frac {1}{a} \int \frac {(a + b \cos x) - b \cos x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} d x = \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b}{a} \int \frac {d (\sin x)}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} \\ = \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b \sin x}{a (a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + \frac {(n - 1) b ^ {2}}{a} \int \frac {\sin^ {2} x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n}} d x \\ = \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b \sin x}{a (a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + \frac {n - 1}{a} \int \frac {(b ^ {2} - a ^ {2}) + (a + b \cos x) (a - b \cos x)}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n}} d x \\ = \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b \sin x}{a (a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + \frac {(n - 1) (b ^ {2} - a ^ {2})}{a} I _ {n} + \frac {n - 1}{a} \int \frac {a - b \cos x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} d x \\ = \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b \sin x}{a (a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + \frac {(n - 1) (b ^ {2} - a ^ {2})}{a} I _ {n} - \frac {n - 1}{a} \int \frac {(a + b \cos x) - 2 a}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} d x \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
= \frac {1}{a} I _ {n - 2} - \frac {b \sin x}{a (a + b \cos x) ^ {n - 1}} + \frac {(n - 1) (b ^ {2} - a ^ {2})}{a} I _ {n} - \frac {n - 1}{a} I _ {n - 2} + 2 (n - 1) I _ {n - 1}.
$$

于是， $\frac{(n - 1)(a^2 - b^2)}{a} I_n = -\frac{b\sin x}{a(a + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} +(2n - 3)I_{n - 1} - \frac{n - 2}{a} I_{n - 2}.$

最后得到 $I_{n} = -\frac{b\sin x}{(n - 1)(a^{2} - b^{2})(a + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} + \frac{(2n - 3)a}{(n - 1)(a^{2} - b^{2})} I_{n - 1} - \frac{n - 2}{(n - 1)(a^{2} - b^{2})} I_{n - 2},$

即 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a + b\cos x)^n} = \frac{A\sin x}{(a + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} +B\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a + b\cos x)^{n - 1}} +C\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a + b\cos x)^{n - 2}}.$

式中 $A = -\frac{b}{(n - 1)(a^2 - b^2)}$ ， $B = \frac{(2n - 3)a}{(n - 1)(a^2 - b^2)}$ ， $C = -\frac{n - 2}{(n - 1)(a^2 - b^2)}$ （ $|a| \neq |b|$ ； $n > 1$ 且 $a \neq 0$ ）

若 $a = 0$ ，则 $b\neq 0$ ，我们有

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(a + b \cos x) ^ {n}} = \frac {1}{b ^ {n}} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\cos^ {n} x} = \frac {1}{b ^ {n}} \left[ \frac {\sin x}{(n - 1) \cos^ {n - 1} x} + \frac {n - 2}{n - 1} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\cos^ {n - 2} x} \right] ^ {*}.
$$

\*) 利用2012题(2)的结果.

求积分：

【2060】 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\cos x\sqrt{1 + \sin^2x}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin x \mathrm{d}x}{\cos x \sqrt{1 + \sin^2 x}} = \int \frac{-\mathrm{d}(\cos x)}{\cos x \sqrt{2 - \cos^2 x}} = -\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\cos x)}{\cos^2 x \sqrt{2 \sec^2 x - 1}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\sec x)}{\sqrt{2 \sec^2 x - 1}}$

$$
= \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \left| \sqrt {2} \sec x + \sqrt {2 \sec^ {2} x - 1} \right| + C = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\sqrt {2} + \sqrt {1 + \sin^ {2} x}}{| \cos x |} + C.
$$

【2061】 $\int \frac{\sin^2x}{\cos^2x\sqrt{\tan x}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \frac{\sin^2 x}{\cos^2 x \sqrt{\tan x}} \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\sin^2 x \mathrm{d}(\tan x)}{\sqrt{\tan x}} = 2 \int \sin^2 x \mathrm{d}(\sqrt{\tan x}) = 2 \int (1 - \cos^2 x) \mathrm{d}(\sqrt{\tan x})$

$$
= 2 \sqrt {\tan x} - 2 \int \frac {d (\sqrt {\tan x})}{1 + \tan^ {2} x} = 2 \sqrt {\tan x} - \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \ln \frac {\tan x + \sqrt {2 \tan x} + 1}{\tan x - \sqrt {2 \tan x} + 1} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \arctan \frac {\sqrt {2 \tan x}}{\tan x - 1} *) + C (\tan x > 0).
$$

\*) 利用1884题的结果.

【2062】 $\int \frac{\sin x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{2 + \sin 2x}}.$

解 由于 $2 + \sin 2x = 1 + (\sin x + \cos x)^{2} = 3 - (\sin x - \cos x)^{2}$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sin x d x}{\sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}} = \int \frac {\cos x - (\cos x - \sin x)}{\sqrt {1 + (\sin x + \cos x) ^ {2}}} d x = \int \frac {\cos x}{\sqrt {3 - (\sin x - \cos x) ^ {2}}} d x - \ln (\sin x + \cos x + \sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}) \\ = - \int \frac {\sin x \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}} + \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\sin x - \cos x)}{\sqrt {3 - (\sin x - \cos x) ^ {2}}} - \ln (\sin x + \cos x + \sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}). \\ \end{array}
$$

因而，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\sin x \mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}} = \frac {1}{2} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} (\sin x - \cos x)}{\sqrt {3 - (\sin x - \cos x) ^ {2}}} - \frac {1}{2} \ln (\sin x + \cos x + \sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}) \\ = \frac {1}{2} \arcsin \left(\frac {\sin x - \cos x}{\sqrt {3}}\right) - \frac {1}{2} \ln (\sin x + \cos x + \sqrt {2 + \sin 2 x}) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2063】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + \varepsilon\cos x)^2}$ （ $0 <   \varepsilon <  1)$

解 此为2059题之特例，这里

$$
a = 1, \quad b = \varepsilon , \quad n = 2, \quad A = - \frac {\varepsilon}{1 - \varepsilon^ {2}}, \quad B = \frac {1}{1 - \varepsilon^ {2}}, \quad C = 0.
$$

代入得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + \varepsilon\cos x)^2} = -\frac{\varepsilon\sin x}{(1 - \varepsilon^2)(1 + \varepsilon\cos x)} +\frac{1}{1 - \varepsilon^2}\int \frac{1}{1 + \varepsilon\cos x}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= - \frac {\varepsilon \sin x}{\left(1 - \varepsilon^ {2}\right) \left(1 + \varepsilon \cos x\right)} + \frac {2}{\left(1 - \varepsilon^ {2}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} \arctan \left(\sqrt {\frac {1 - \varepsilon}{1 + \varepsilon}} \tan \frac {x}{2}\right) ^ {*}) + C.
$$

\*) 利用2028题(1)的结果.

【2064】 $\int \frac{\cos^{n - 1}\frac{x + a}{2}}{\sin^{n + 1}\frac{x - a}{2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 令 $\frac{\cos\frac{x + a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}} = t$ ，则有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin^2\frac{x - a}{2}} = -\frac{2}{\cos a}\mathrm{d}t$ ( $\cos a \neq 0$ )

解设 $t = \frac{\cos\frac{x + a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}$ 则 $\mathrm{dt} = \frac{-\frac{1}{2}\cos a}{\sin^2\frac{x - a}{2}}\mathrm{dx},\quad \frac{\mathrm{dx}}{\sin^2\frac{x - a}{2}} = -\frac{2}{\cos a}\mathrm{dt}.$

于是， $\int \frac{\cos^{n - 1}\frac{x + a}{2}}{\sin^{n + 1}\frac{x - a}{2}}\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{2}{\cos a}\int t^{n - 1}\mathrm{d}t = -\frac{2}{n\cos a} t^n +C = -\frac{2}{n\cos a}\left(\frac{\cos\frac{x + a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}\right)^n +C\quad (\cos a\neq 0).$

【2065】推出积分 $I_{n} = \int \left(\frac{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x + a}{2}}\right)^{n}\mathrm{d}x$ （ $n$ 为正整数）的递推公式.

解 解法1：

设 $t = \frac{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x + a}{2}}$ 则 $x = 2\arctan \left(\frac{1 + t}{1 - t}\tan \frac{a}{2}\right)$ $\mathrm{dx} = \frac{4\tan\frac{a}{2}}{t^2\sec^2\frac{a}{2} + 2t(\tan^2\frac{a}{2} - 1) + \sec^2\frac{a}{2}}\mathrm{dt}.$

由于 $\frac{4t^n\tan\frac{a}{2}}{t^2\sec^2\frac{a}{2} + 2t\left(\tan^2\frac{a}{2} - 1\right) + \sec^2\frac{a}{2}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {4 \tan \frac {a}{2}}{\sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2}} t ^ {n - 2} + \frac {- 4 \tan \frac {a}{2}}{t ^ {2} \sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2} + 2 t \left(\tan^ {2} \frac {a}{2} - 1\right) + \sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2}} \cdot \frac {2 \left(\tan^ {2} \frac {a}{2} - 1\right)}{\sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2}} t ^ {n - 1} \\ + \frac {- 4 \tan \frac {a}{2}}{t ^ {2} \sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2} + 2 t \left(\tan^ {2} \frac {a}{2} - 1\right) + \sec^ {2} \frac {a}{2}} t ^ {n - 2} \quad (n > 2), \\ \end{array}
$$

两端对 $t$ 积分，即得递推公式 $I_{n} = \frac{2\sin a}{n - 1} t^{n - 1} + 2\cos a I_{n - 1} - I_{n - 2}.$

解法2：

设 $y = \frac{x + a}{2}$ 则 $\frac{x - a}{2} = y - a$ ，从而，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {n} = 2 \int \left[ \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \right] ^ {n} d y = 2 \int \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \left[ \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \right] ^ {n - 1} d y = 2 \int \frac {\sin y \cos a - \cos y \sin a}{\sin y} \left[ \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \right] ^ {n - 1} d y \\ = \cos a I _ {n - 1} - 2 \sin a \int \frac {\cos y}{\sin y} \left[ \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \right] ^ {n - 1} d y. \\ \end{array}
$$

再设 $\frac{\sin(y - a)}{\sin y} = t = \frac{\sin\frac{x - a}{2}}{\sin\frac{x + a}{2}}, J_n = 2\int \frac{\cos y}{\sin y} t^n\mathrm{d}y,$

则 $I_{n} = \cos a I_{n - 1} - \sin a J_{n - 1},\quad J_{n - 1} = \frac{\cos a I_{n - 1} - I_{n}}{\sin a}.$ (1)

又 $J_{n} = 2\int \frac{\cos y}{\sin y}\left[\frac{\sin(y - a)}{\sin y}\right]^{n}\mathrm{d}y = -\frac{2}{n}\int \sin^{n}(y - a)\mathrm{d}\left(\frac{1}{\sin^{n}y}\right)$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {2}{n} \left[ \frac {\sin (y - a)}{\sin y} \right] ^ {n} + 2 \int \frac {\sin^ {n - 1} (y - a)}{\sin^ {n} y} \cos (y - a) d y = - \frac {2}{n} t ^ {n} + 2 \int t ^ {n - 1} \frac {\cos y \cos a + \sin y \sin a}{\sin y} d y \\ = - \frac {2}{n} t ^ {n} + \cos a J _ {n - 1} + \sin a I _ {n - 1}. \tag {2} \\ \end{array}
$$

由（1）式和（2）式解得

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {n} = \cos a I _ {n - 1} - \sin a J _ {n - 1} = \cos a I _ {n - 1} - \sin a \left(- \frac {2}{n - 1} t ^ {n - 1} + \cos a J _ {n - 2} + \sin a I _ {n - 2}\right) \\ = \cos a I _ {n - 1} + \frac {2 \sin a}{n - 1} t ^ {n - 1} - \sin a \cos a \left(\frac {\cos a I _ {n - 2} - I _ {n - 1}}{\sin a}\right) - \sin^ {2} a I _ {n - 2} = 2 \cos a I _ {n - 1} - I _ {n - 2} + \frac {2 \sin a}{n - 1} t ^ {n - 1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

# § 5. 各种超越函数的积分法

【2066】证明：若 $P(x)$ 为 $\pmb{n}$ 次多项式，则

$$
\int P (x) \mathrm {e} ^ {a x} \mathrm {d} x = \mathrm {e} ^ {a x} \left[ \frac {P (x)}{a} - \frac {P ^ {\prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \dots + (- 1) ^ {n} \frac {P ^ {(n)} (x)}{a ^ {n + 1}} \right] + C.
$$

证 $\int P(x)\mathrm{e}^{ax}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{a}\int P(x)\mathrm{d}(\mathrm{e}^{ax}) = \frac{1}{a} P(x)\mathrm{e}^{ax} - \frac{1}{a}\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}P'(x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{a} P (x) e ^ {a x} - \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int P ^ {\prime} (x) d \left(e ^ {a x}\right) = \frac {1}{a} P (x) e ^ {a x} - \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} P ^ {\prime} (x) e ^ {a x} + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int e ^ {a x} P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) d x \\ = \dots = e ^ {a x} \left[ \frac {P (x)}{a} - \frac {P ^ {\prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \dots + (- 1) ^ {n} \frac {P ^ {(n)} (x)}{a ^ {n + 1}} \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

因为 $P(x)$ 为 $n$ 次多项式，所以， $P^{(n+1)}(x) \equiv 0.$ 从而，上述等式括号中的导数到 $P^{(n)}(x)$ 为止.

【2067】证明：若 $P(x)$ 为 $\pmb{n}$ 次多项式，则

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int P (x) \cos a x d x = \frac {\sin a x}{a} \left[ P (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(4)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + \frac {\cos a x}{a ^ {2}} \left[ P ^ {\prime} (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(5)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + C, \\ \int P (x) \sin a x d x = - \frac {\cos a x}{a} \left[ P (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(4)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + \frac {\sin a x}{a ^ {2}} \left[ P ^ {\prime} (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(5)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

证 $\int P(x)\cos ax\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{a}\int P(x)\mathrm{d}(\sin ax) = \frac{1}{a} P(x)\sin ax - \frac{1}{a}\int P'(x)\sin ax\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{a} P (x) \sin a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int P ^ {\prime} (x) d (\cos a x) = \frac {1}{a} P (x) \sin a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} P ^ {\prime} (x) \cos a x - \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \cos a x d x \\ = \frac {1}{a} P (x) \sin a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} P ^ {\prime} (x) \cos a x - \frac {1}{a ^ {3}} P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \sin a x - \frac {1}{a ^ {4}} P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {4}} \int P ^ {(4)} (x) \cos a x d x \\ = \dots = \frac {\sin a x}{a} \left[ P (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(4)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + \frac {\cos a x}{a ^ {2}} \left[ P ^ {\prime} (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(5)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + C. \\ \int P (x) \sin a x d x = - \frac {1}{a} \int P (x) d (\cos a x) = - \frac {1}{a} P (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a} \int P ^ {\prime} (x) \cos a x d x \\ = - \frac {1}{a} P (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int P ^ {\prime} (x) d (\sin a x) = - \frac {1}{a} P (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} P ^ {\prime} (x) \sin a x - \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} \int P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \sin a x d x \\ = - \frac {1}{a} P (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {2}} P ^ {\prime} (x) \sin a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {3}} P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \cos a x - \frac {1}{a ^ {4}} P ^ {\prime \prime} (x) \cos a x + \frac {1}{a ^ {4}} \int P ^ {(4)} (x) \cos a x d x \\ = \dots = - \frac {\cos a x}{a} \left[ P (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(4)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + \frac {\sin a x}{a ^ {2}} \left[ P ^ {\prime} (x) - \frac {P ^ {\prime \prime} (x)}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {P ^ {(5)} (x)}{a ^ {4}} - \dots \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

上述导数项是有限的，其阶数 $\leqslant n, a \neq 0$

求积分：

【2068】 $\int x^{3} \mathrm{e}^{3x} \mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^{3} \mathrm{e}^{3x} \mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{e}^{3x}\left(\frac{x^{3}}{3} - \frac{3x^{2}}{9} + \frac{6x}{27} - \frac{6}{81}\right)^{*}) + C = \mathrm{e}^{3x}\left(\frac{x^{3}}{3} - \frac{x^{2}}{3} + \frac{2x}{9} - \frac{2}{27}\right) + C.$

\*) 利用2066题的结果.

【2069】 $\int (x^{2} - 2x + 2)\mathrm{e}^{-x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int (x^{2} - 2x + 2)\mathrm{e}^{-x}\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{e}^{-x}\left(\frac{x^{2} - 2x + 2}{-1} -\frac{2x - 2}{1} +\frac{2}{-1}\right)^{*}) + C = -\mathrm{e}^{-x}(x^{2} + 2) + C.$

\*) 利用2066题的结果.

【2070】 $\int x^5\sin 5x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^{5}\sin 5x\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{\cos 5x}{5}\left(x^{5} - \frac{20x^{3}}{25} +\frac{120x}{625}\right) + \frac{\sin 5x}{25}\left(5x^{4} - \frac{60x^{2}}{25} +\frac{120}{625}\right)^{*}) + C$

$$
= - \frac {\cos 5 x}{5} \left(x ^ {3} - \frac {4 x ^ {3}}{5} + \frac {2 4 x}{1 2 5}\right) + \frac {\sin 5 x}{2 5} \left(5 x ^ {4} - \frac {1 2 x ^ {2}}{5} + \frac {2 4}{1 2 5}\right) + C.
$$

\*) 利用2067题的结果.

【2071】 $\int (1 + x^2)^2\cos x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int (1 + x^2)^2\cos x\mathrm{d}x = \int (1 + 2x^2 +x^4)\cos x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \sin x \left[ \left(1 + 2 x ^ {2} + x ^ {4}\right) - (4 + 1 2 x ^ {2}) + 2 4 \right] + \cos x \left[ \left(4 x + 4 x ^ {3}\right) - 2 4 x \right] ^ {*}) + C \\ = (2 1 - 1 0 x ^ {2} + x ^ {4}) \sin x - (2 0 x - 4 x ^ {3}) \cos x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）利用2067题的结果.

【2072】 $\int x^{7}\mathrm{e}^{-x^{2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^{7} \mathrm{e}^{-x^{2}} \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2} \int (x^{2})^{3} \mathrm{e}^{-x^{2}} \mathrm{d}(x^{2}) = \frac{1}{2} \mathrm{e}^{-x^{2}} \left( \frac{x^{6}}{-1} - \frac{3x^{4}}{1} + \frac{6x^{2}}{-1} - \frac{6}{1} \right)^{+1} + C$

$$
= - \frac {1}{2} e ^ {- x ^ {2}} (x ^ {6} + 3 x ^ {4} + 6 x ^ {2} + 6) + C.
$$

\*) 利用2066题的结果.

【2073】 $\int x^{2}\mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^{2}\mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{d}x = 2\int (\sqrt{x})^{5}\mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{d}(\sqrt{x}) = 2\mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{x}}(x^{\frac{5}{2}} - 5x^{2} + 20x^{\frac{3}{2}} - 60x + 120x^{\frac{1}{2}} - 120)^{*}) + C.$

\*) 利用2066题的结果.

【2074】 $\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\cos^2 bx\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\cos^2 bx\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}(1 + \cos 2bx)\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2a}\mathrm{e}^{ax} + \frac{1}{2}\mathrm{e}^{ax}\frac{a\cos 2bx + 2bsin 2bx}{a^2 + 4b^2} +C.$

\*) 利用1828题的结果.

【2075】 $\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\sin^3 bx\mathrm{d}x.$

提示 注意 $\mathrm{e}^{ax}\sin^3 bx = \mathrm{e}^{ax}\left(\frac{3}{4}\sin bx - \frac{1}{4}\sin 3bx\right)$ ，并利用1829题的结果.

解 $\int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\sin^3 bx\mathrm{d}x = \int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\sin bx\frac{1 - \cos 2bx}{2}\mathrm{d}x = \int \mathrm{e}^{ax}\left(\frac{3}{4}\sin bx - \frac{1}{4}\sin 3bx\right)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {3}{4} e ^ {a x} \frac {a \sin b x - b \cos b x ^ {*}}{a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{4} e ^ {a x} \frac {a \sin 3 b x - 3 b \cos 3 b x ^ {*}}{a ^ {2} + 9 b ^ {2}} + C.
$$

\*) 利用1829题的结果.

【2076】 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin x\mathrm{d}x = \int x\sin x\mathrm{d}(\mathrm{e}^{x}) = x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin x - \int \mathrm{e}^{x}(\sin x + x\cos x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin x - \int (\sin x + x \cos x) \mathrm {d} \left(\mathrm {e} ^ {x}\right) = \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (x \sin x - \sin x - x \cos x) + \int \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (2 \cos x - x \sin x) \mathrm {d} x \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (x \sin x - \sin x - x \cos x) + 2 \int \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos x \mathrm {d} x - \int x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin x \mathrm {d} x. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{\mathrm{e}^{x}}{2} (x\sin x - \sin x - x\cos x) + \int \mathrm{e}^{x}\cos x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac {e ^ {x}}{2} (x \sin x - \sin x - x \cos x) + \frac {e ^ {x}}{2} (\sin x + \cos x) ^ {\cdot}) + C = \frac {e ^ {x}}{2} [ x (\sin x - \cos x) + \cos x ] + C.
$$

\*）利用1828题的结果.

【2077】 $\int x^{2}\mathrm{e}^{x}\cos x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x^{2} \mathrm{e}^{x} \cos x \mathrm{~d} x = \int x^{2} \cos x \mathrm{~d} (\mathrm{e}^{x}) = x^{2} \mathrm{e}^{x} \cos x - \int \mathrm{e}^{x} (2 x \cos x - x^{2} \sin x) \mathrm{~d} x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = x ^ {2} \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos x - \int (2 x \cos x - x ^ {2} \sin x) \mathrm {d} (\mathrm {e} ^ {x}) \\ = x ^ {2} \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos x - \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (2 x \cos x - x ^ {2} \sin x) + \int \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (2 \cos x - 4 x \sin x - x ^ {2} \cos x) \mathrm {d} x \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {x} [ x ^ {2} (\sin x + \cos x) - 2 x \cos x ] + 2 \int \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos x \mathrm {d} x - 4 \int x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin x \mathrm {d} x - \int x ^ {2} \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos x \mathrm {d} x. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $\int x^{2}\mathrm{e}^{x}\cos x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{\mathrm{e}^{x}}{2} [x^{2}(\sin x + \cos x) - 2x\cos x] + \int \mathrm{e}^{x}\cos x\mathrm{d}x - 2\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{2} \left[ x ^ {2} (\sin x + \cos x) - 2 x \cos x \right] + \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{2} (\sin x + \cos x) ^ {*}) - 2 \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{2} \left[ x (\sin x - \cos x) + \cos x \right] ^ {* *} + C \\ = \frac {e ^ {x}}{2} \left[ x ^ {2} (\sin x + \cos x) - 2 x \sin x + (\sin x - \cos x) \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用1828题的结果.

\*\*）利用2076题的结果.

【2078】 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin^{2}x\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin^{2}x\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}(1 - \cos 2x)\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2}\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\cos 2x\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{2} e ^ {x} (x - 1) - \frac {1}{2} \int x \cos 2 x d \left(e ^ {x}\right) = \frac {1}{2} e ^ {x} (x - 1) - \frac {1}{2} x e ^ {x} \cos 2 x + \frac {1}{2} \int e ^ {x} (\cos 2 x - 2 x \sin 2 x) d x \\ = \frac {1}{2} e ^ {x} (x - 1) - \frac {1}{2} x e ^ {x} \cos 2 x + \frac {e ^ {x}}{2} \cdot \frac {\cos 2 x + 2 \sin 2 x ^ {*})}{5} - \int x e ^ {x} \sin 2 x d x, \\ \end{array}
$$

而 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin 2x\mathrm{d}x = \int x\sin 2x\mathrm{d}(\mathrm{e}^{x}) = x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin 2x - \int \mathrm{e}^{x}(\sin 2x + 2x\cos 2x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin 2 x - \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{5} (\sin 2 x - 2 \cos 2 x) ^ {* *}) - 2 \int x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (1 - 2 \sin^ {2} x) \mathrm {d} x \\ = x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin 2 x - \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{5} (\sin 2 x - 2 \cos 2 x) - 2 (x - 1) \mathrm {e} ^ {x} + 4 \int x \mathrm {e} ^ {x} \sin^ {2} x \mathrm {d} x. \\ \end{array}
$$

代入得 $\int x\mathrm{e}^{x}\sin^{2}x\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{e}^{x}\left[\frac{x - 1}{2} -\frac{x}{10} (2\sin 2x + \cos 2x) + \frac{1}{50} (4\sin 2x - 3\cos 2x)\right] + C.$

\*) 利用1828题的结果.

\*\*）利用1829题的结果.

【2079】 $\int (x - \sin x)^3\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int (x - \sin x)^3\mathrm{d}x = \int (x^3 -3x^2\sin x + 3x\sin^2 x - \sin^3 x)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {x ^ {4}}{4} + 3 \int x ^ {2} \mathrm {d} (\cos x) + \frac {3}{2} \int x (1 - \cos 2 x) \mathrm {d} x + \int (1 - \cos^ {2} x) \mathrm {d} (\cos x) \\ = \frac {x ^ {4}}{4} + 3 x ^ {2} \cos x - 6 \int x \cos x d x + \frac {3}{4} x ^ {2} - \frac {3}{4} \int x d (\sin 2 x) + \cos x - \frac {1}{3} \cos^ {3} x \\ = \frac {x ^ {4}}{4} + \frac {3 x ^ {2}}{4} + 3 x ^ {2} \cos x - 6 \int x d (\sin x) - \frac {3}{4} x \sin 2 x + \frac {3}{4} \int \sin 2 x d x + \cos x - \frac {1}{3} \cos^ {3} x \\ = \frac {x ^ {4}}{4} + \frac {3 x ^ {2}}{4} + 3 x ^ {2} \cos x - 6 x \sin x - 6 \cos x - \frac {3}{4} x \sin 2 x + \cos x - \frac {3}{8} \cos 2 x - \frac {1}{3} \cos^ {3} x + C \\ = \frac {x ^ {4}}{4} + \frac {3 x ^ {2}}{4} + 3 x ^ {2} \cos x - x \left(6 \sin x + \frac {3}{4} \sin 2 x\right) - \left(5 \cos x + \frac {3}{8} \cos 2 x\right) - \frac {1}{3} \cos^ {3} x + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2080】 $\int \cos^2\sqrt{x}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\sqrt{x} = t$ ，则 $x = t^2, \mathrm{d}x = 2t\mathrm{d}t.$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \cos^ {2} \sqrt {x} d x = 2 \int t \cos^ {2} t d t = \int t (1 + \cos 2 t) d t \\ = \frac {t ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {1}{2} \int t d (\sin 2 t) = \frac {t ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {1}{2} t \sin 2 t - \frac {1}{2} \int \sin 2 t d t \\ = \frac {t ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {1}{2} t \sin 2 t + \frac {1}{4} \cos 2 t + C = \frac {x}{2} + \frac {1}{2} \sqrt {x} \sin (2 \sqrt {x}) + \frac {1}{4} \cos (2 \sqrt {x}) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2081】证明：若 $R$ 为有理函数，数 $a_1, a_2, \dots, a_n$ 为可公约的，则积分

$$
\int R \left(\mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {1} x}, \mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {2} x}, \dots , \mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {n} x}\right) \mathrm {d} x
$$

是初等函数.

证明思路 由题设 $a_1, a_2, \dots, a_n$ 为可公约的数，故存在一个不为零的实数 $\alpha$ ，使有

$$
a _ {1} = k _ {1} \alpha , a _ {2} = k _ {2} \alpha , \dots , a _ {n} = k _ {n} \alpha ,
$$

其中， $k_{1}, k_{2}, \dots, k_{n}$ 为整数.

令 $\mathrm{e}^{\alpha x} = t$ ，即可获证.

证 按题意 $a_1, a_2, \cdots, a_n$ 为可公约的数，于是，存在一个实数 $\alpha$ ，使得

$$
a _ {1} = k _ {1} \alpha , a _ {2} = k _ {2} \alpha , \dots , a _ {n} = k _ {n} \alpha \quad (\alpha \neq 0),
$$

其中， $k_{1}, k_{2}, \dots, k_{n}$ 为整数.

设 $\mathrm{e}^{\alpha x} = t$ ，则 $x = \frac{1}{\alpha}\ln t$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\alpha t}\mathrm{d}t$ 于是，

$$
\int R \left(\mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {1} x}, \mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {2} x}, \dots , \mathrm {e} ^ {a _ {n} x}\right) \mathrm {d} x = \frac {1}{\alpha} \int R \left(t ^ {k _ {1}}, t ^ {k _ {2}}, \dots , t ^ {k _ {n}}\right) \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t} = \int R ^ {*} (t) \mathrm {d} t,
$$

其中 $R^{*}(t)$ 是 $\pmb{t}$ 的有理函数.因此，积分 $\int R(\mathrm{e}^{a_1x},\mathrm{e}^{a_2x},\dots ,\mathrm{e}^{a_n x})\mathrm{d}x$ 为初等函数

求下列积分：

【2082】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)^2}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)^2} = \int \frac{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x) - \mathrm{e}^x}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)^2}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} -\int \frac{\mathrm{e}^x\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)^2} = \int \left(1 - \frac{\mathrm{e}^x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x}\right)\mathrm{d}x - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^x)^2}$

$$
= x - \ln (1 + e ^ {x}) + \frac {1}{1 + e ^ {x}} + C.
$$

【2083】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{e}^{2x}\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{e}^{2x}\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} = \int \frac{(\mathrm{e}^{2x} - 1) + 1}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x}\mathrm{d}x = \int (\mathrm{e}^x -1)\mathrm{d}x + \int \frac{1}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x}\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{e}^x -x + \int \left(1 - \frac{\mathrm{e}^x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^x}\right)\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= e ^ {x} - \ln (1 + e ^ {x}) + C.
$$

【2084】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + \mathrm{e}^x - 2}$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + \mathrm{e}^x - 2} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(e^x + 2)(e^x - 1)} = \frac{1}{3}\int \frac{1}{e^x - 1}\mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{3}\int \frac{1}{e^x + 2}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{3} \int \left(1 - \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{\mathrm {e} ^ {x} - 1}\right) \mathrm {d} x - \frac {1}{6} \int \left(1 - \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{\mathrm {e} ^ {x} + 2}\right) \mathrm {d} x = - \frac {x}{3} + \frac {1}{3} \ln | \mathrm {e} ^ {x} - 1 | - \frac {x}{6} + \frac {1}{6} \ln (\mathrm {e} ^ {x} + 2) + C \\ = - \frac {x}{2} + \frac {1}{3} \ln | e ^ {x} - 1 | + \frac {1}{6} \ln (e ^ {x} + 2) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2085】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{2}} + \mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{3}} + \mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{6}}}$

解设 $\mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{6}} = t$ ，则 $x = 6\ln t$ ， $\mathrm{dx} = \frac{6}{t}\mathrm{dt}$ .代入得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{1 + \mathrm {e} ^ {\frac {x}{2}} + \mathrm {e} ^ {\frac {t}{3}} + \mathrm {e} ^ {\frac {t}{6}}} = 6 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t (1 + t ^ {3} + t ^ {2} + t)} \\ = 6 \int \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t (t + 1) \left(t ^ {2} + 1\right)} = 6 \int \left[ \frac {1}{t} - \frac {1}{2 (t + 1)} - \frac {t + 1}{2 \left(t ^ {2} + 1\right)} \right] \mathrm {d} t \\ = 6 \ln t - 3 \ln (t + 1) - \frac {3}{2} \ln (1 + t ^ {2}) - 3 \arctan t + C \\ = x - 3 \ln \left[ \left(1 + e ^ {\frac {x}{6}}\right) \sqrt {1 + e ^ {\frac {x}{3}}} \right] - 3 \arctan \left(e ^ {\frac {x}{6}}\right) + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

【2086】 $\int \frac{1 + \mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{2}}}{(1 + \mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{4}})^{2}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解设 $\mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{4}} = t$ ，则 $x = 4\ln t$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = \frac{4}{t}\mathrm{d}t$ ，代人得

$$
\int \frac {1 + e ^ {\frac {x}{2}}}{(1 + e ^ {\frac {x}{4}}) ^ {2}} d x = 4 \int \frac {1 + t ^ {2}}{t (1 + t) ^ {2}} d t = 4 \int \left[ \frac {1}{t} - \frac {2}{(1 + t) ^ {2}} \right] d t = 4 \ln t + \frac {8}{1 + t} + C = x + \frac {8}{1 + e ^ {\frac {x}{4}}} + C.
$$

【2087】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\mathrm{e}^x - 1}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\mathrm{e}^x - 1}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{e}^{\frac{x}{2}}\sqrt{1 - (\mathrm{e}^{-\frac{x}{2}})^2}} = -2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}(\mathrm{e}^{-\frac{x}{2}})}{\sqrt{1 - (\mathrm{e}^{-\frac{x}{2}})^2}} = -2\arcsin (\mathrm{e}^{-\frac{x}{2}}) + C.$

【2088】 $\int \sqrt{\frac{e^x - 1}{e^x + 1}}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sqrt{\frac{e^x - 1}{e^x + 1}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{e^x - 1}{\sqrt{e^{2x} - 1}}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{e^x\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{e^{2x} - 1}} -\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{e^{2x} - 1}}$

$$
= \int \frac {d \left(e ^ {x}\right)}{\sqrt {\left(e ^ {x}\right) ^ {2} - 1}} + \int \frac {d \left(e ^ {- x}\right)}{\sqrt {1 - \left(e ^ {- x}\right) ^ {2}}} = \ln \left(e ^ {x} + \sqrt {e ^ {2 x} - 1}\right) + \arcsin \left(e ^ {- x}\right) + C.
$$

【2089】 $\int \sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + 4\mathrm{e}^x - 1}\mathrm{d}x.$

解 $\int \sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + 4\mathrm{e}^x - 1}\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + 4\mathrm{e}^x - 1}{\sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{2x} + 4\mathrm{e}^x - 1}}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int \frac {2 e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x}}{2 \sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1}} d x + 2 \int \frac {e ^ {x} d x}{\sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1}} - \int \frac {d x}{\sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1}} \\ = \int \frac {d \left(e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1\right)}{2 \sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1}} + 2 \int \frac {d (e ^ {x} + 2)}{\sqrt {(e ^ {x} + 2) ^ {2} - 5}} + \int \frac {d (e ^ {- x} - 2)}{\sqrt {5 - (e ^ {- x} - 2) ^ {2}}} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
= \sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1} + 2 \ln (e ^ {x} + 2 + \sqrt {e ^ {2 x} + 4 e ^ {x} - 1}) - \arcsin \frac {2 e ^ {x} - 1}{\sqrt {5} e ^ {x}} + C.
$$

【2090】 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} + \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x}}.$

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} + \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \mathrm{e}^{-x}(\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} -\sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x})\mathrm{d}x$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {1}{2} \int \left(\sqrt {1 + e ^ {x}} - \sqrt {1 - e ^ {x}}\right) d \left(e ^ {- x}\right) \\ = - \frac {e ^ {- x}}{2} \left(\sqrt {1 + e ^ {x}} - \sqrt {1 - e ^ {y}}\right) + \frac {1}{4} \int \left(\frac {1}{\sqrt {1 + e ^ {x}}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {1 - e ^ {x}}}\right) d x \\ = - \frac {1}{2} e ^ {- r} \left(\sqrt {1 + e ^ {x}} - \sqrt {1 - e ^ {x}}\right) + \frac {1}{4} I _ {1} + \frac {1}{4} I _ {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

对于 $I_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^{x}}}$ 设 $\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} = t$ ，则 $x = \ln (t^2 - 1)$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2t\mathrm{d}t}{t^2 - 1}$

于是， $I_{1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^{x}}} = 2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{t^{2} - 1} = \ln \frac{t - 1}{t + 1} + C = \ln \frac{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^{x}} - 1}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^{x}} + 1} + C_{1}.$

对于 $I_{2} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^{x}}}$ 设 $\sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x} = t$ ，则 $x = \ln (1 - t^2)$ ， $\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{2t\mathrm{d}t}{1 - t^2}$

于是， $I_{2} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^{x}}} = -2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 - t^{2}} = -\ln \frac{1 + t}{1 - t} +C_{2} = -\ln \frac{1 + \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^{x}}}{1 - \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^{x}}} +C_{2}.$

代人得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} + \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x}} = -\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-x}}{2} (\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} - \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x}) + \frac{1}{4}\ln \frac{(\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} - 1)(1 - \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x})}{(\sqrt{1 + \mathrm{e}^x} + 1)(1 + \sqrt{1 - \mathrm{e}^x})} + C.$

【2091】证明：若 $R$ 为有理函数，其分母仅有实根，则积分 $\int R(x)\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i}\pi x}\mathrm{d}x$ 可用初等函数和超越函数

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x}}{x} \mathrm {d} x = \operatorname {l i} (\mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x}) + C, \text {式 中} \operatorname {l i} x = \int \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\ln x}
$$

来表示.

证 因为 $R$ 的分母仅有实根，所以仅包含形如 $(x - a_i)^{k_i}$ 的因子 $(i = 1,2,\dots ,l)$ . 分解 $R(x)$ 为部分分式得

$$
R (x) = P (x) + \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {l} \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {k _ {i}} \frac {A _ {i j}}{(x - a _ {i}) ^ {j}},
$$

其中 $P(x)$ 为 $\pmb{x}$ 的多项式， $A_{ij}$ 是常系数．从而，积分

$$
\int R (x) \mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x} \mathrm {d} x = \int P (x) \mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x} \mathrm {d} x + \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {l} \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {k _ {i}} A _ {i j} \int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x}}{(x - a ^ {i}) ^ {j}} \mathrm {d} x.
$$

上式右端第一个积分显然是初等函数. 而积分 $\int \frac{\mathrm{e}^{ax}}{(x - a_i)^j}\mathrm{d}x$ 可用初等函数和超越函数来表示. 事实上, 设 $x - a_{i} = t$ , 则

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a x}}{(x - a _ {i}) ^ {j}} \mathrm {d} x = \int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a (a _ {i} + t)}}{t ^ {j}} \mathrm {d} t = \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a x _ {i}}}{1 - j} \int \mathrm {e} ^ {a} \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {1}{t ^ {j - 1}}\right) = \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a x _ {i}}}{1 - j} \mathrm {e} ^ {\prime} \cdot \frac {1}{t ^ {j - 1}} - \frac {a \mathrm {e} ^ {a x _ {i}}}{1 - j} \int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a t}}{t ^ {j - 1}} \mathrm {d} t.
$$

这样，被积函数中分母的次数便降低一次，再继续运用分部积分法 $(j - 2)$ 次，即可得

$$
\int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {a x}}{(x - a _ {i}) ^ {\prime}} \mathrm {d} x = g _ {i j} (x) + B _ {i j} \operatorname {l i} \left(\mathrm {e} ^ {a (x - a _ {i})}\right),
$$

其中 $g_{ij}(x)$ 为 $x$ 的初等函数， $B_{ij}$ 为常数。因此，积分

$$
\int R (x) \mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x} \mathrm {d} x = \int P (x) \mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha x} \mathrm {d} x + \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {l} \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {k _ {i}} A _ {i j} g _ {i j} (x) + \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {l} \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {k _ {i}} A _ {i j} B _ {i j} \operatorname {l i} \left(\mathrm {e} ^ {\alpha (x - a _ {i})}\right)
$$

是初等函数与超越函数之和.

【2092】若 $P\left(\frac{1}{x}\right) = a_0 + \frac{a_1}{x} + \dots + \frac{a_n}{x^n}, a_0, a_1, \dots, a_n$ 为常数，则在什么情形下，积分 $\int P\left(\frac{1}{x}\right) \mathrm{e}^x \mathrm{d}x$

为初等函数？

解 $\int \frac{a_k}{x^k}\mathrm{e}^x\mathrm{d}x = -\frac{a_k}{k - 1}\cdot \frac{\mathrm{e}^x}{x^{k - 1}} +\frac{a_k}{k - 1}\int \frac{\mathrm{e}^x}{x^{k - 1}}\mathrm{d}x = \dots$

$$
= - \frac {a _ {k}}{k - 1} \cdot \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{x ^ {k - 1}} - \frac {a _ {k}}{(k - 1) (k - 2)} \cdot \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{x ^ {k - 2}} - \dots - \frac {a _ {k}}{(k - 1) !} \cdot \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{x} + \frac {a _ {k}}{(k - 1) !} \int \frac {\mathrm {e} ^ {x}}{x} d x.
$$

于是， $\int P\left(\frac{1}{x}\right)\mathrm{e}^{x}\mathrm{d}x = \int \left(\sum_{k = 0}^{n}\frac{a_k}{x^k}\right)\mathrm{e}^{x}\mathrm{d}x = \sum_{k = 0}^{n}\int \frac{a_k}{x^k}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
